Isi wajah se ek poor aadmi magnificent nahi ho sakta, kyunki uske paas large sums fittingly spend karne ke means nahi hain; aur jo koshish karta hai wo ek fool hai, kyunki wo uske alawa expect kiya jaane se zyada spend karta hai aur jo proper hai usse zyada, lekin ye right expenditure hai jo virtuous hai. Lekin great expenditure un logo ko becoming hai jinke paas shuru se hi suitable means hain, apne khud ke efforts se acquire ki gayi ya ancestors ya connections se, aur high birth ya reputation ke logo ko, aur waghera; kyunki ye sab cheezein greatness aur prestige apne saath laati hain. Primarily, to, magnificent aadmi is kism ka hai, aur magnificence is kism ki expenditures mein dikhayi jaati hai, jaisa kaha gaya hai; kyunki ye sabse greatest aur sabse honourable hain.

Private occasions ke expenditure ke liye sabse suitable wo hain jo once for all hote hain, jaise ek wedding ya isi kism ki koi cheez, ya koi bhi cheez jo poori city ke ya usme position ke logo ke interest ki ho, aur foreign guests ko receive karna aur unhe unke raaste bhejna, aur gifts aur counter-gifts; kyunki magnificent aadmi khud par nahi balki public objects par spend karta hai, aur gifts votive offerings se ek resemblance rakhte hain. Ek magnificent aadmi apne house ko bhi apni wealth ke suitably furnish karega (kyunki ek house bhi ek kism ka public ornament hai), aur un works par preference se spend karega jo lasting hain (kyunki ye sabse beautiful hain), aur har class of things par wo jo becoming hai wo spend karega; kyunki same cheezein gods aur men ke liye suitable nahi hain, na hi ek temple mein aur ek tomb mein. Aur kyunki har expenditure apni kind mein great ho sakti hai, aur jo absolutely most magnificent hai wo great object par great expenditure hai, lekin jo yahan magnificent hai wo in circumstances mein great hai, aur work mein greatness expense mein greatness se differ karti hai (kyunki most beautiful ball ya bottle ek child ko gift ke roop mein magnificent hai, lekin iski price small aur mean hai) — isliye ye magnificent aadmi ka characteristic hai, chahe wo kisi bhi kism ka result produce kar raha ho, ise magnificently produce karna (kyunki aisa result aasaani se surpass nahi hota) aur ise expenditure ke worthy banana. Aisa, to, magnificent aadmi hai; jo aadmi excess mein jaata hai aur vulgar hai wo exceed karta hai, jaisa kaha gaya hai, right se zyada spend karke. Kyunki small objects of expenditure par wo bahut kuch spend karta hai aur ek tasteless showiness display karta hai; jaise wo ek club dinner ek wedding banquet ke scale par deta hai, aur jab wo comedy ke liye chorus provide karta hai wo unhe stage par purple mein le aata hai, jaise Megara mein karte hain. Aur ye sab cheezein wo noble ki khaatir nahi balki apni wealth show off karne ke liye karega, aur kyunki wo sochta hai ki wo in cheezon ke liye admire kiya jaata hai, aur jahan usse bahut spend karna chahiye wahan wo thoda spend karta hai aur jahan thoda wahan bahut. Niggardly aadmi doosri taraf sab kuch mein short fall karega, aur greatest sums spend karne ke baad result ki beauty ko ek trifle ke liye spoil karega, aur wo jo bhi kar raha ho wo hesitate karega aur consider karega kaise wo least spend kare, aur usse bhi lament karega, aur sochega ki wo har cheez ek bigger scale par kar raha hai jitni usse karni chahiye.

Ye states of character, to, vices hain; phir bhi wo disgrace nahi laati kyunki wo na to apne neighbour ke liye harmful hain na hi bahut unseemly.

## VIRTUES CONCERNED WITH HONOUR

**Pride**

**3.** Pride apne naam se hi great things se concerned lagti hai; kis kism ki great things, ye pehla sawaal hai jiska humein answer try karna chahiye. Isse koi farak nahi padta ki hum state of character consider karein ya us aadmi ko jise ye characterize karti hai. Ab aadmi proud maana jaata hai jo khud ko great things ka worthy sochta hai aur unka worthy hai; kyunki jo aisa apne deserts se pare karta hai wo ek fool hai, lekin koi bhi virtuous aadmi foolish ya silly nahi hai. Proud aadmi, to, wo aadmi hai jise humne describe kiya hai. Kyunki jo little ka worthy hai aur khud ko little ka worthy sochta hai wo temperate hai, lekin proud nahi; kyunki pride greatness imply karti hai, jaise beauty ek good-sized body imply karti hai, aur little log neat aur well-proportioned ho sakte hain lekin beautiful nahi ho sakte. Doosri taraf, jo khud ko great things ka worthy sochta hai, unka unworthy hote hue, wo vain hai; halaanki har wo aadmi jo khud ko usse zyada worthy sochta hai jitna wo really worthy hai wo vain nahi hai. Jo aadmi khud ko usse kam worthy sochta hai jitna wo really worthy hai wo unduly humble hai, chahe uske deserts great ho ya moderate, ya uske deserts small hon lekin uske claims usse bhi smaller hon. Aur jis aadmi ke deserts great hain wo sabse zyada unduly humble lagta hai; kyunki agar wo less hote to wo kya karta? Proud aadmi, to, apne claims ki greatness ke respect mein ek extreme hai, lekin unki rightness ke respect mein intermediate; kyunki wo wahi claim karta hai jo uske merits ke according hai, jabki doosre excess ya deficiency mein jaate hain.

Agar, to, wo great things deserve aur claim karta hai, aur sabse upar greatest things, wo ek particular cheez se concerned hoga. Desert external goods ke relative hai; aur inme se greatest, hum kahenge, wo hai jo hum gods ko render karte hain, aur jise position ke log sabse zyada aim karte hain, aur jo noblest deeds ke liye appointed prize hai; aur ye honour hai; ye surely external goods mein sabse greatest hai. Honours aur dishonours, isliye, wo objects hain jinke respect mein proud aadmi hai jaisa usse hona chahiye. Aur argument ke bina bhi ye evident hai ki proud men honour se concerned hain; kyunki honour hi wo hai jise wo chiefly claim karte hain, lekin apne deserts ke according. Unduly humble aadmi apne khud ke merits ki comparison mein aur proud aadmi ke claims ki comparison mein dono se short falls karta hai. Vain aadmi apne khud ke merits ki comparison mein excess mein jaata hai, lekin proud aadmi ke claims ko exceed nahi karta.

Ab proud aadmi, kyunki wo sabse zyada deserve karta hai, use highest degree mein good hona chahiye; kyunki better aadmi hamesha zyada deserve karta hai, aur best aadmi sabse zyada. Isliye truly proud aadmi ko good hona chahiye. Aur har virtue mein greatness proud aadmi ka characteristic lagti hai. Aur ye ek proud aadmi ke liye bahut unbecoming hoga danger se fly karna, apne arms swing karte hue, ya kisi doosre ko wrong karna; kyunki disgraceful acts karne ka use kya end hoga, jise kuch bhi great nahi lagta? Agar hum use point by point consider karein hum ek proud aadmi ki utter absurdity dekhenge jo good nahi hai. Na hi, phir se, wo honour ka worthy hoga agar wo bad hota; kyunki honour virtue ka prize hai, aur ye good ko hi render kiya jaata hai. Pride, to, virtues ka ek kism ka crown lagta hai; kyunki ye unhe greater banata hai, aur ye unke bina nahi milta. Isliye truly proud hona hard hai; kyunki ye nobility aur goodness of character ke bina impossible hai. Chiefly honours aur dishonours se, to, proud aadmi concerned hai; aur great honours par jo good men dwara conferred hain wo moderately pleased hoga, ye sochte hue ki wo apna khud ka hi paa raha hai ya apna khud se bhi kam; kyunki koi bhi honour aisa nahi ho sakta jo perfect virtue ka worthy ho, phir bhi wo ise accept karega kam se kam kyunki unke paas usse zyada koi cheez bestow karne ke liye nahi hai; lekin casual people se honour aur trifling grounds par wo utterly despise karega, kyunki ye wo nahi hai jo wo deserve karta hai, aur dishonour bhi, kyunki uske case mein ye just nahi ho sakti. Pehli baat, to, jaisa kaha gaya hai, proud aadmi honours se concerned hai; phir bhi wo wealth aur power aur sab good ya evil fortune ke prati bhi moderation ke saath khud ko rakhega, jo bhi usse befall ho, aur na to good fortune se overjoyed hoga na evil se over-pained. Kyunki even honour ke prati bhi wo aise behave nahi karta jaise ye ek bahut great cheez ho. Power aur wealth honour ki khaatir desirable hain (kam se kam jinke paas ye hain wo inke means se honour paana chahte hain); aur jiske liye even honour bhi ek little thing hai baaki bhi honi chahiye. Isi wajah se proud men disdainful maane jaate hain.

Fortune ke goods bhi pride mein contribute karte lagte hain. Kyunki jo men well-born hain unhe honour ka worthy maana jaata hai, aur isi tarah jo power ya wealth enjoy karte hain; kyunki wo ek superior position mein hain, aur har cheez jismein kisi good cheez mein superiority hai wo greater honour mein rakhi jaati hai. Isi wajah se aisi cheezein bhi men ko prouder banaati hain; kyunki wo kuch logo dwara unhe rakhne ke liye honoured hote hain; lekin truth mein sirf good aadmi hi honoured hone ka worthy hai; wo, phir bhi, jiske paas dono advantages hain wo zyada honour ka worthy maana jaata hai. Lekin jo log bina virtue ke aise goods rakhte hain wo na to great claims banane mein justified hain na hi 'proud' ke naam ke entitled; kyunki ye cheezein perfect virtue imply karti hain. Disdainful aur insolent, phir bhi, even wo bhi ban jaate hain jinke paas aise goods hain. Kyunki bina virtue ke fortune ke goods ko gracefully bear karna aasan nahi hai; aur, unhe bear karne ke unable hote hue, aur khud ko doosron se superior sochte hue, wo doosron ko despise karte hain aur khud jo chahein karte hain. Wo proud aadmi ko imitate karte hain uske jaise hue bina, aur ye wo karte hain jahan wo kar sakte hain; isliye wo virtuously act nahi karte, lekin wo doosron ko despise zaroor karte hain. Kyunki proud aadmi justly despise karta hai (kyunki wo truly sochta hai), lekin many random mein aisa karte hain.

Wo trifling dangers mein nahi bhaagta, na hi wo danger ka fond hai, kyunki wo few cheezon ko honour karta hai; lekin wo great dangers face karega, aur jab wo danger mein hota hai wo apni life ka unsparing hai, ye jaante hue ki kuch conditions aisi hain jinme life worth having nahi hai. Aur wo is kism ka aadmi hai benefits confer karne ke liye, lekin unhe receive karne mein wo ashamed hai; kyunki ek superior ka mark hai, doosra inferior ka. Aur wo return mein greater benefits confer karne ke apt hai; kyunki isi tarah original benefactor, paid hone ke alawa, uska debt bhi incur karega, aur transaction se gainer hoga. Wo apne kiye gaye kisi bhi service ko yaad rakhte lagte hain, lekin jo unhone receive kiye hain unhe nahi (kyunki jo service receive karta hai wo us se inferior hai jisne ise kiya, lekin proud aadmi superior hona chahta hai), aur pehle ke baare mein pleasure se aur doosre ke baare mein displeasure se sunte hain; ye, lagta hai, isliye hai ki Thetis ne Zeus ko un services ka mention nahi kiya jo usne unhe kiye the, aur Spartans ne Athenians ko apni services recount nahi ki, balki wo jo unhone receive ki thi. Ye proud aadmi ka bhi ek mark hai kuch bhi na maangna ya shayad hi kuch, lekin help readily dena, aur high position aur good fortune enjoy karne wale logo ke prati dignified hona, lekin middle class ke logo ke prati unassuming; kyunki pehle wale se superior hona ek difficult aur lofty cheez hai, lekin doosre se aisa hona easy hai, aur pehle ke upar lofty bearing ill-breeding ka mark nahi hai, lekin humble people ke beech ye utna hi vulgar hai jitna weak ke against strength ka display. Phir, ye proud aadmi ka characteristic hai un cheezon ko aim na karna jo commonly honour mein rakhi jaati hain, ya un cheezon ko jinme doosre excel karte hain; sluggish hona aur hold back karna siwaye jahan great honour ya ek great work stake par ho, aur few deeds ka aadmi hona, lekin great aur notable ones ka. Use apne hate mein aur apne love mein open bhi hona chahiye (kyunki apne feelings ko conceal karna, yani truth ki koi kam care lena log kya sochenge iski zyada, ek coward ka part hai), aur openly speak aur act karna chahiye; kyunki wo speech mein free hai kyunki wo contemptuous hai, aur wo truth batane ke liye given hai, siwaye jab wo vulgar se irony mein baat karta hai. Use apni life ko doosre ke around revolve karne ke unable hona chahiye, siwaye ek friend ke; kyunki ye slavish hai, aur is reason ke liye sab flatterers servile hain aur self-respect mein lacking log flatterers hain. Na hi wo admiration ke liye given hai; kyunki uske liye kuch bhi great nahi hai. Na hi wo wrongs ka mindful hai; kyunki ek proud aadmi ke liye ye proper nahi hai ki uski long memory ho, khaas kar wrongs ke liye, balki unhe overlook karna. Na hi wo ek gossip hai; kyunki wo na to apne baare mein baat karega na doosre ke baare mein, kyunki use praise kiye jaane ki koi care nahi na doosron ke blame kiye jaane ki; na hi wo phir se praise ke liye given hai; aur isi reason ke liye wo evil-speaker bhi nahi hai, apne enemies ke baare mein bhi nahi, siwaye haughtiness se. Necessary ya small matters ke respect mein wo sab men mein least given hai lamentation ya favours maangne ke; kyunki ye us aadmi ka part hai jo aise matters ko seriously leta hai unke respect mein aisa behave karna. Wo aisa hai jo beautiful aur profitless cheezein rakhega profitable aur useful cheezon se zyada; kyunki ye ek aise character ke zyada proper hai jo khud ko suffice karta hai.

Further, ek slow step proud aadmi ke liye proper mana jaata hai, ek deep voice, aur ek level utterance; kyunki jo aadmi few cheezon ko seriously leta hai wo hurried hone ki likelihood nahi rakhta, na hi jo aadmi kuch bhi great nahi maanta wo excited hone ki, jabki ek shrill voice aur ek rapid gait hurry aur excitement ke results hain.

Aisa, to, proud aadmi hai; jo aadmi usse short fall karta hai wo unduly humble hai, aur jo aadmi usse beyond jaata hai wo vain hai. Ab ye bhi bad nahi maane jaate (kyunki ye evildoers nahi hain), balki sirf mistaken. Kyunki unduly humble aadmi, good things ka worthy hote hue, khud ko jo wo deserve karta hai usse rob karta hai, aur usme kuch bad lagta hai is fact se ki wo khud ko good things ka worthy nahi sochta, aur khud ko na jaanta bhi lagta hai; nahi to wo un cheezon ko desire karta jinka wo worthy tha, kyunki ye good thi. Phir bhi aise log fools nahi maane jaate, balki unduly retiring. Aisa estimate, phir bhi, actually unhe worse bana deta lagta hai; kyunki har class of people wo aim karta hai jo uske worth ke corresponding hai, aur ye log noble actions aur undertakings se bhi back stand karte hain, khud ko unworthy deem karte hue, aur external goods se bhi kam nahi. Vain people, doosri taraf, fools hain aur khud ke ignorant hain, aur ye manifestly hai; kyunki, unke worthy na hote hue, wo honourable undertakings attempt karte hain, aur phir found out ho jaate hain; aur wo khud ko clothing aur outward show aur aisi cheezon se adorn karte hain, aur chahte hain ki unki good fortune ke strokes public ki jaayein, aur unke baare mein aise baat karte hain jaise unhe inke liye honoured kiya jaayega. Lekin undue humility pride ke zyada opposed hai vanity se; kyunki ye commoner bhi hai aur worse bhi.

Pride, to, grand scale par honour se concerned hai, jaisa kaha gaya hai.

**Ambition aur unambitiousness ke beech ka intermediate virtue**

**4.** Honour ke sphere mein bhi lagta hai, jaisa humne subject par apni first remarks mein kaha, ek virtue hai jo pride se related lagti hai jaise liberality magnificence se hai. Kyunki in mein se kisi ka bhi grand scale se kuch lena-dena nahi hai, lekin dono humein right ke according dispose karte hain middling aur unimportant objects ke respect mein; jaise wealth ke getting aur giving mein ek mean hai aur ek excess aur defect, waise hi honour bhi right se zyada, ya less, desire ki ja sakti hai, ya right sources se aur right way mein. Hum ambitious aadmi ko blame karte hain right se zyada honour aim karne ke liye aur wrong sources se, aur unambitious aadmi ko honoured hone ke liye willing na hone ke liye even noble reasons ke liye bhi. Lekin kabhi-kabhi hum ambitious aadmi ko praise karte hain manly hone ke liye aur noble ka lover hone ke liye, aur unambitious aadmi ko moderate aur self-controlled hone ke liye, jaisa humne subject ke apne first treatment mein kaha. Evidently, kyunki 'fond of such and such an object' ka ek se zyada meaning hai, hum term 'ambition' ya 'love of honour' ko hamesha same cheez ko assign nahi karte, balki jab hum quality praise karte hain hum us aadmi ke baare mein sochte hain jo zyadatar logo se zyada honour ko pyaar karta hai, aur jab hum ise blame karte hain hum uske baare mein sochte hain jo ise right se zyada pyaar karta hai. Mean bina naam ke hone ke naate, extremes iski jagah ke liye dispute karte lagte hain jaise ki wo default se vacant ho. Lekin jahan excess aur defect hai, wahan ek intermediate bhi hai; ab men honour ko dono jitna unhe chahiye usse zyada aur kam desire karte hain; isliye ye possible bhi hai ki aisa jaise one should karein; sab surat mein yahi wo state of character hai jo praise ki jaati hai, honour ke respect mein ek unnamed mean hone ke naate. Ambition ke relative ye unambitiousness lagta hai, aur unambitiousness ke relative ye ambition lagta hai, jabki dono ke severally relative ye ek sense mein dono ek saath lagta hai. Ye doosre virtues ke liye bhi true lagta hai. Lekin is case mein extremes contradictories lagte hain kyunki intermediate ko koi naam nahi mila hai.

## THE VIRTUE CONCERNED WITH ANGER

**Good temper**

**5.** Good temper anger ke respect mein ek mean hai; middle state unnamed hone ke naate, aur extremes bhi almost bina naam ke, hum good temper ko middle position mein rakhte hain, halaanki ye deficiency ki taraf incline karta hai, jo bina naam ke hai. Excess ko ek kism ki 'irascibility' kaha ja sakta hai. Kyunki passion anger hai, jabki iske causes many aur diverse hain.

Jo aadmi right cheezon par aur right logo ke saath angry hota hai, aur, further, jaise usse hona chahiye, jab usse hona chahiye, aur jab tak usse hona chahiye, wo praise kiya jaata hai. Ye good-tempered aadmi hoga, to, kyunki good temper praise ki jaati hai. Kyunki good-tempered aadmi unperturbed rehne aur passion se led na hone ki tendency rakhta hai, balki manner mein, cheezon mein, aur time ki length mein angry hone ki tendency rakhta hai jo reason dictate karta hai; lekin wo zyada deficiency ki direction mein err karta lagta hai; kyunki good-tempered aadmi revengeful nahi hai, balki allowances banaane ki zyada tendency rakhta hai.

Deficiency, chahe ye ek kism ki 'unirascibility' ho ya jo bhi ho, blame ki jaati hai. Kyunki jo log un cheezon par angry nahi hote jinpar unhe hona chahiye wo fools maane jaate hain, aur isi tarah wo bhi jo right way mein, right time par, ya right persons ke saath angry nahi hote; kyunki aise aadmi ko cheezein feel na karne wala ya unse pained na hone wala maana jaata hai, aur, kyunki wo angry nahi hota, use apna defense karne mein unlikely maana jaata hai; aur insulted hona endure karna aur apne friends ko insult put up karna slavish hai. Excess sab points mein manifest ho sakta hai jo naam liye gaye hain (kyunki koi bhi wrong persons ke saath angry ho sakta hai, wrong things par, right se zyada, too quickly, ya too long); phir bhi ye sab same person mein nahi milte. Indeed wo mil bhi nahi sakte; kyunki evil khud ko bhi destroy karta hai, aur agar ye complete hai to ye unbearable ban jaata hai. Ab hot-tempered log quickly angry hote hain aur wrong persons ke saath aur wrong things par aur right se zyada, lekin unka anger quickly cease ho jaata hai — jo unke baare mein sabse best point hai. Ye unhe isliye hota hai kyunki wo apna anger restrain nahi karte balki apni temper ki quickness ki wajah se openly retaliate karte hain, aur phir unka anger cease ho jaata hai. Excess ki wajah se choleric log quick-tempered hain aur har cheez se aur har occasion par angry hone ke ready; isi se unka naam aata hai. Sulky log appease karna hard hain, aur apna anger lambe samay tak retain karte hain; kyunki wo apni passion repress karte hain. Lekin ye cease ho jaata hai jab wo retaliate karte hain; kyunki revenge unhe unke anger se relieve karta hai, unme pain ki jagah pleasure produce karte hue. Agar aisa nahi hota to wo apna burden retain karte hain; kyunki iske obvious na hone ki wajah se koi bhi unke saath reason nahi karta, aur khud mein apna anger digest karna time leta hai. Aise log khud ke liye aur apne dearest friends ke liye sabse zyada troublesome hote hain. Hum un logo ko bad-tempered kehte hain jo wrong things par, right se zyada, aur longer angry hote hain, aur jab tak wo vengeance ya punishment inflict na kar dein tab tak appease nahi ho sakte. Good temper ke against hum excess ko defect se zyada oppose karte hain; kyunki na sirf ye commoner hai (kyunki revenge zyada human hai), balki bad-tempered log saath rehne mein worse hain.

Jo humne apni earlier subject ki treatment mein kaha wo abhi jo hum keh rahe hain usse bhi plain hai; namely, ki ye define karna aasan nahi hai kaise, kis ke saath, kis par, aur kitni der tak koi angry ho, aur kis point par right action cease hoti hai aur wrong shuru hoti hai. Kyunki jo aadmi raaste se thoda stray karta hai, chahe zyada ki taraf ho ya kam ki taraf, use blame nahi kiya jaata; kyunki kabhi-kabhi hum un logo ko praise karte hain jo deficiency exhibit karte hain, aur unhe good-tempered kehte hain, aur kabhi hum angry logo ko manly kehte hain, ruling karne ke capable hone ke roop mein. Kitna far, isliye, aur kaise ek aadmi ko stray karna chahiye isse pehle wo blameworthy ban jaaye, ye words mein state karna aasan nahi hai; kyunki decision particular facts aur perception par depend karta hai. Lekin itna kam se kam plain hai, ki middle state praiseworthy hai — wo state jiske virtue se hum right people ke saath, right things par, right way mein angry hote hain, aur waghera, jabki excesses aur defects blameworthy hain — slightly agar wo low degree mein present hain, zyada agar higher degree mein, aur bahut zyada agar high degree mein. Evidently, to, humein middle state ko cling karna chahiye. Anger ke relative states ke liye itna kaafi hai.

## VIRTUES OF SOCIAL INTERCOURSE

**Friendliness**

**6.** Men ki gatherings mein, social life mein aur words aur deeds ke interchange mein, kuch men obsequious maane jaate hain, namely, jo pleasure dene ke liye sab kuch praise karte hain aur kabhi oppose nahi karte, balki apni duty samajhte hain 'un logo ko koi pain na dena jinse wo milte hain'; jabki jo, iske contrary, har cheez oppose karte hain aur pain dene ki koi parwaah nahi karte unhe churlish aur contentious kaha jaata hai. Ki humne naam liye gaye states culpable hain ye kaafi plain hai, aur ki middle state laudable hai — wo state jiske virtue se ek aadmi right things ko right way mein put up karega, aur resent karega; lekin isko koi naam assign nahi kiya gaya, halaanki ye friendship se sabse zyada resemble karta hai. Kyunki jo aadmi is middle state ke corresponding hai wo bahut kuch waisa hi hai, affection add karne par, jise hum ek good friend kehte hain. Lekin question mein state friendship se ismein differ karti hai ki ye apne associates ke prati koi passion ya affection imply nahi karti; kyunki ye loving ya hating ke reason se nahi hai ki aisa aadmi har cheez ko right way mein leta hai, balki ek certain kism ka aadmi hone se. Kyunki wo un logo ke prati bhi waise hi behave karega jinhe wo jaanta hai aur jinhe nahi jaanta, intimates ke prati aur un ke prati jo nahi hain, siwaye is ke ki in mein se har case mein wo jaisa befitting hai waisa behave karega; kyunki ye proper nahi hai intimates aur strangers ke liye same care rakhna, na hi ye same conditions hain jo unhe pain dena right banati hain. Ab humne generally kaha hai ki wo logo ke saath right way mein associate karega; lekin ye honourable aur expedient ke reference se hai ki wo pain na dene ya pleasure contribute karne ko aim karega. Kyunki wo social life ke pleasures aur pains se concerned lagta hai; aur jahan kahin bhi ye honourable nahi hai, ya usko pleasure contribute karna harmful hai, wo refuse karega, aur pain dena prefer karega; bhi agar kisi doosre ki action mein uska acquiescence disgrace layega, aur high degree mein, ya injury, us doosre par, jabki uska opposition thoda pain laata hai, wo acquiesce nahi karega balki decline karega. Wo high station ke logo ke saath aur ordinary people ke saath differently associate karega, closer aur zyada distant acquaintances ke saath, aur isi tarah doosri sab differences ke respect mein bhi, har class ko wahi rendering karega jo befitting hai, aur jabki apni khud ki khaatir wo pleasure contribute karna choose karta hai, aur pain dena avoid karta hai, wo consequences se guide hoga, agar ye greater hain, yani honour aur expediency. Ek great future pleasure ki khaatir bhi, wo small pains inflict karega.

Jo aadmi intermediate attain karta hai, to, wo hai jaisa humne describe kiya hai, lekin usne koi naam nahi paaya; jo log pleasure contribute karte hain unme se, jo aadmi bina kisi ulterior object ke pleasant hona aim karta hai wo obsequious hai, lekin jo aadmi aisa isliye karta hai taaki wo money ki ya cheezon ki direction mein kuch advantage paaye jo money khareed sakti hai wo ek flatterer hai; jabki wo aadmi jo har cheez se quarrel karta hai wo, jaisa kaha gaya hai, churlish aur contentious hai. Aur extremes ek doosre ke contradictory lagte hain kyunki intermediate bina naam ke hai.

**Truthfulness**

**7.** Boastfulness ke against opposed mean almost isi sphere mein milta hai; aur ye bhi bina naam ke hai. Ye ek bad plan nahi hoga in states ko bhi describe karna; kyunki hum character ke facts ko better jaanenge agar hum inhe detail mein jaayein, aur hum convince ho jaayenge ki virtues means hain agar hum ye sab cases mein aisa dekhein. Social life ke field mein wo log describe kiye ja chuke hain jo doosron ke saath associate karte hue pleasure ya pain dene ko apna object banaate hain; chaliye ab describe karein un logo ko jo truth ya falsehood ko words aur deeds mein aur jo claims wo aage rakhte hain unme equally pursue karte hain. Boastful aadmi, to, apt lagta hai un cheezon ko claim karne ke jo glory laati hain, jab uske paas wo nahi hain, ya un mein se usse zyada claim karne ke jitni uske paas hain, aur mock-modest aadmi doosri taraf jo uske paas hai use disclaim karne ke ya use belittle karne ke, jabki wo aadmi jo mean observe karta hai wo ek aisa hai jo ek cheez ko uske khud ke naam se pukaarta hai, life mein aur word mein truthful hote hue, jo uske paas hai use own karte hue, na zyada na kam. Ab in mein se har course kisi object ke saath ya bina object ke adopt kiya ja sakta hai. Lekin har aadmi apne character ke according speak aur act aur jeeta hai, agar wo kisi ulterior object ke liye act nahi kar raha. Aur falsehood khud mein mean aur culpable hai, aur truth noble aur praise ka worthy hai. Isliye truthful aadmi ek aur case hai us aadmi ka jo, intermediate hote hue, praise ka worthy hai, aur untruthful aadmi ke dono forms culpable hain, aur khaas kar boastful aadmi.

Chaliye dono discuss karein, lekin sab se pehle truthful aadmi. Hum us aadmi ki baat nahi kar rahe jo apni agreements mein faith rakhta hai, yani un cheezon mein jo justice ya injustice se pertain karti hain (kyunki ye ek doosri virtue se belong karega), balki us aadmi ki jo un matters mein jinme is kism ki koi cheez stake par nahi hai wo word aur life dono mein true hai kyunki uska character aisa hai. Lekin aisa aadmi as a matter of fact equitable lagta hai. Kyunki jo aadmi truth se pyaar karta hai, aur wahan truthful hai jahan kuch bhi stake par nahi hai, wo aur bhi zyada truthful hoga jahan kuch stake par hai; wo falsehood ko ek base cheez ki tarah avoid karega, ye dekhte hue ki usne ise khud iski khaatir bhi avoid kiya; aur aisa aadmi praise ka worthy hai. Wo truth ko understate karne ki taraf zyada incline karta hai; kyunki ye better taste mein lagta hai kyunki exaggerations wearisome hain.

Jo aadmi apne paas jitna hai usse zyada claim karta hai bina kisi ulterior object ke wo ek contemptible kism ka fellow hai (nahi to wo falsehood mein delight nahi leta), lekin bad se zyada futile lagta hai; lekin agar wo isse ek object ke liye karta hai, jo aadmi ise reputation ya honour ki khaatir karta hai wo (ek boaster ke liye) bahut zyada blame ka worthy nahi hai, lekin jo isse money ke liye ya un cheezon ke liye karta hai jo money tak le jaati hain wo ek uglier character hai (ye capacity nahi hai jo boaster banati hai, balki purpose; kyunki ye uski state of character ki wajah se hai aur ek certain kism ka aadmi hone se hi hai ki wo ek boaster hai); jaise ek aadmi liar hai kyunki wo lie ko khud enjoy karta hai, aur doosra kyunki wo reputation ya gain desire karta hai. Ab jo reputation ki khaatir boast karte hain wo aisi qualities claim karte hain jo praise ya congratulation win karti hain, lekin jinka object gain hai wo qualities claim karte hain jo neighbours ke liye value ki hain aur jinki kami aasaani se detect nahi hoti, jaise ek seer, ek sage, ya ek physician ki powers. Is reason ke liye ye is kism ki cheezein hain jinhe zyadatar log claim aur boast karte hain; kyunki inme mentioned qualities milti hain.

Mock-modest log, jo cheezein understate karte hain, character mein zyada attractive lagte hain; kyunki wo gain ke liye nahi balki parade avoid karne ke liye speak karte lagte hain; aur yahan bhi ye wo qualities hain jo reputation laati hain jinhe wo disclaim karte hain, jaise Socrates karte the. Jo log trifling aur obvious qualities disclaim karte hain unhe humbugs kaha jaata hai aur wo zyada contemptible hain; aur kabhi-kabhi ye boastfulness lagta hai, jaise Spartan dress; kyunki excess aur great deficiency dono boastful hain. Lekin jo log moderation ke saath understatement use karte hain aur matters ke baare mein understate karte hain jo humari notice par bahut zyada force nahi karte wo attractive lagte hain. Aur ye boaster hi hai jo truthful aadmi ke opposed lagta hai; kyunki wo worse character hai.

**Ready wit**

**8.** Kyunki life mein activity ki tarah rest bhi shaamil hai, aur ismein leisure aur amusement shaamil hai, yahan bhi ek kism ka intercourse lagta hai jo tasteful hai; kuch aisa kehna hai — aur phir se sunna hai — jo koi kehna chahiye aur jaise usse kehna chahiye. Kis kism ke log se koi baat kar raha hai ya sun raha hai isse bhi farak padega. Evidently yahan bhi mean ke comparison mein excess aur deficiency dono hain. Jo log humour ko excess tak le jaate hain unhe vulgar buffoons maana jaata hai, sab costs par humour ke liye striving, aur becoming ke bajaye laugh raise karne mein aim karte hue aur apne fun ke object ko pain avoid karne se zyada; jabki jo log na khud joke bana sakte hain na un logo ko put up kar sakte hain jo aisa karte hain unhe boorish aur unpolished maana jaata hai. Lekin jo log tasteful way mein joke karte hain unhe ready-witted kaha jaata hai, jo ek kism ki readiness suggest karta hai is way aur us way turn karne ki; kyunki aise sallies character ke movements maane jaate hain, aur jaise bodies apne movements se discriminate ki jaati hain, waise hi characters bhi. Ridiculous side of things, phir bhi, dhoondhne mein far nahi hai, aur zyadatar log usse zyada amusement aur jesting mein delight karte hain jitna unhe karna chahiye, aur isliye even buffoons ko bhi ready-witted kaha jaata hai kyunki wo attractive paaye jaate hain; lekin ki wo ready-witted aadmi se differ karte hain, aur no small extent tak, ye jo kaha gaya hai usse clear hai.

Middle state mein tact bhi belong karta hai; ek tactful aadmi ka mark ye hai ki wo aisi cheezein kahe aur sune jo ek good aur well-bred aadmi ko befit karti hain; kyunki kuch cheezein hain jo aise aadmi ko jest ke tareeke se kehni aur sunni befit karti hain, aur ek well-bred aadmi ka jesting ek vulgar aadmi ke jesting se differ karta hai, aur ek educated aadmi ka joking ek uneducated aadmi ke joking se. Koi bhi ye purani aur nayi comedies se bhi dekh sakta hai; pehle wale ke authors ke liye language ki indecency amusing thi, doosre ke logo ke liye innuendo zyada aisa hai; aur ye propriety ke respect mein no small degree mein differ karte hain. Ab kya humein us aadmi ko define karna chahiye jo achhe se joke banata hai apni saying se jo ek well-bred aadmi ko unbecoming nahi hai, ya apne pain na dene se, ya even hearer ko delight dene se? Ya kya doosri definition, kam se kam, khud indefinite hai, kyunki different cheezein different logo ko hateful ya pleasant hoti hain? Wo kis kism ke jokes ko sunega wahi hoga jise wo bana sakta hai; kyunki jis kism ko wo put up kar sakta hai wo bhi wahi kism hai jise wo banaata lagta hai. Kuch jokes hain, to, jo wo nahi banayega; kyunki jest ek kism ka abuse hai, aur kuch cheezein hain jinhe abuse karne se lawgivers humein forbid karte hain; aur unhe shayad humein aisi cheezon ka jest banane se bhi forbid karna chahiye tha. Refined aur well-bred aadmi, isliye, waisa hoga jaisa humne describe kiya hai, khud ke liye ek law jaisa hote hue. Aisa, to, intermediate aadmi hai, chahe use tactful kaha jaaye ya ready-witted. Buffoon, doosri taraf, apne sense of humour ka slave hai, aur na khud ko na doosron ko spare karta hai agar wo laugh raise kar sake, aur aisi cheezein kehta hai jinme se koi bhi refinement wala aadmi nahi kahega, aur kuch aisi cheezon ko wo sunega bhi nahi. Boor, phir se, aisi social intercourse ke liye useless hai; kyunki wo kuch bhi contribute nahi karta aur har cheez mein fault dhoondta hai. Lekin relaxation aur amusement life mein ek necessary element maane jaate hain.

Life mein describe kiye gaye means, to, number mein teen hain, aur sab ek kism ke words aur deeds ke interchange se concerned hain. Wo, phir bhi, differ karte hain is mein ki ek truth se concerned hai, aur doosre do pleasantness se. Pleasure se concerned in mein se, ek jests mein display hota hai, doosra life ke general social intercourse mein.

## A QUASI-VIRTUE

**Shame**

**9.** Shame ko ek virtue ke roop mein describe nahi kiya jaana chahiye; kyunki ye ek state of character se zyada ek passion jaisa hai. Ye, kam se kam, dishonour ke ek kism ke fear ke roop mein define kiya jaata hai, aur danger ke fear se produce hone wale effect jaisa ek effect produce karta hai; kyunki jo log disgraced feel karte hain wo blush karte hain, aur jo death se fear karte hain wo pale ho jaate hain. Dono, isliye, ek sense mein bodily conditions lagte hain, jo state of character se zyada passion ke characteristic maane jaate hain.

Passion har age ke liye becoming nahi hai, balki sirf youth ke liye. Kyunki hum sochte hain young people ko shame ke prone hona chahiye kyunki wo passion se jeete hain aur isliye bahut se errors commit karte hain, lekin shame se restrain kiye jaate hain; aur hum un young people ko praise karte hain jo is passion ke prone hain, lekin ek older person ko koi bhi praise nahi karega disgrace ke sense ke prone hone ke liye, kyunki hum sochte hain use kuch aisa nahi karna chahiye jo ye sense cause kare. Kyunki disgrace ka sense even ek good aadmi ka characteristic bhi nahi hai, kyunki ye bad actions ka consequent hai (kyunki aisi actions nahi ki jaani chahiye; aur agar kuch actions very truth mein disgraceful hain aur doosri sirf common opinion ke according, ye koi farak nahi padta; kyunki na to us class ki actions ki jaani chahiye, isliye koi disgrace feel nahi honi chahiye); aur ye ek bad aadmi ka bhi mark hai even aisa hona ki koi bhi disgraceful action kare. Isliye constituted hona ki koi disgraced feel kare agar wo aisi action kare, aur is reason ke liye khud ko good sochna, absurd hai; kyunki shame voluntary actions ke liye feel ki jaati hai, aur good aadmi kabhi voluntarily bad actions nahi karega. Lekin shame conditionally ek good cheez kahi ja sakti hai; agar ek good aadmi aisi actions kare, wo disgraced feel karega; lekin virtues aisi qualification ke subject nahi hain. Aur agar shamelessness — base actions karne mein ashamed na hona — bad hai, isse aisi actions karne mein ashamed hona good nahi ban jaata. Continence bhi virtue nahi hai, balki ek mixed kism ki state hai; ye baad mein dikhaya jaayega.

Ab, phir bhi, chaliye justice discuss karein.

---

# BOOK V • JUSTICE

## JUSTICE: ITS SPHERE AND OUTER NATURE: IN WHAT SENSE IT IS A MEAN

**Just as the lawful (universal justice) aur just as the fair and equal (particular justice): pehla wala consider kiya gaya**

**1.** Justice aur injustice ke respect mein humein consider karna chahiye ki wo kis kism ke actions se concerned hain, kis kism ka mean justice hai, aur kaunse extremes ke beech just act intermediate hai. Hamari investigation wahi course follow karegi jo preceding discussions ka tha.

Hum dekhte hain ki sab log justice se matlab is kism ki state of character se lete hain jo logo ko just karne ke liye dispose karti hai aur unhe justly act karne aur just ke liye wish karne banaati hai; aur similarly injustice se matlab wo state jo unhe unjustly act karne aur unjust ke liye wish karne banati hai. Chaliye hum bhi, to, ise ek general basis maan lein. Kyunki sciences aur faculties ke liye wahi true nahi hai jo states of character ke liye hai. Ek faculty ya ek science jo ek aur same hai wo contrary objects se relate karti maani jaati hai, lekin ek state jo do contraries mein se ek hai wo contrary results produce nahi karti; jaise health ke result mein hum wo nahi karte jo healthy ke opposite hai, balki sirf wo jo healthy hai; kyunki hum kehte hain ek aadmi healthily walk karta hai, jab wo waise walk karta hai jaise ek healthy aadmi karega.

Ab often ek contrary state uski contrary se recognize ki jaati hai, aur often states un subjects se recognize ki jaati hain jo unhe exhibit karte hain; kyunki agar good condition known hai, bad condition bhi known ban jaati hai, aur good condition un cheezon se known hoti hai jo good condition mein hain, aur wo isse. Agar good condition flesh ki firmness hai, to ye necessary hai ki bad condition flesh ki flabbiness ho aur ki wholesome wo ho jo flesh mein firmness cause kare. Aur most part isse follow karta hai ki agar ek contrary ambiguous hai to doosra bhi ambiguous hoga; jaise agar 'just' aisa hai, 'unjust' bhi aisa hoga.

Ab 'justice' aur 'injustice' ambiguous lagti hain, lekin kyunki unke different meanings ek doosre ke near approach karte hain ambiguity notice se escape ho jaati hai aur itni obvious nahi hai jitni ki, comparatively, jab meanings far apart hote hain, jaise (kyunki yahan outward form mein difference great hai) jaise kleis word ka use ek animal ki collar-bone ke liye aur us cheez ke liye jisse hum ek door lock karte hain. Chaliye ek starting-point ke roop mein, 'an unjust man' ke various meanings lein. Dono lawless aadmi aur grasping aur unfair aadmi ko unjust maana jaata hai, isliye evidently dono law-abiding aur fair aadmi just honge. Just, to, lawful aur fair hai, unjust unlawful aur unfair.

Kyunki unjust aadmi grasping hai, use goods se concerned hona chahiye — sab goods nahi, balki wo jinse prosperity aur adversity ka lena-dena hai, jo absolutely liye jaayein to hamesha good hain, lekin ek particular person ke liye hamesha good nahi hain. Ab men in cheezon ke liye pray aur pursue karte hain; lekin unhe nahi karna chahiye, balki pray karna chahiye ki jo cheezein absolutely good hain wo unke liye bhi good hon, aur unhe wo cheezein choose karni chahiye jo unke liye good hain. Unjust aadmi hamesha greater choose nahi karta, balki less bhi karta hai — un cheezon ke case mein jo absolutely bad hain; lekin kyunki lesser evil khud ek sense mein good maana jaata hai, aur graspingness good ki taraf directed hai, isliye use grasping maana jaata hai. Aur wo unfair hai; kyunki ye dono ko contain aur common banaata hai.

Kyunki lawless aadmi ko unjust dekha gaya aur law-abiding aadmi just, evidently sab lawful acts ek sense mein just acts hain; kyunki legislative art dwara laid down acts lawful hain, aur inme se har ek, hum kehte hain, just hai. Ab laws apne sab subjects par enactments mein common advantage ko aim karti hain — chahe sab ka ho ya best ka ya un logo ka jo power hold karte hain, ya isi kism ki koi cheez; isliye ek sense mein hum un acts ko just kehte hain jo political society ke liye happiness aur uske components produce aur preserve karne ki tendency rakhte hain. Aur law humein order karti hai dono brave aadmi ke acts karne ke liye (jaise apne post ko desert na karna na hi flight ko take karna na apne arms fenkna), aur ek temperate aadmi ke (jaise adultery commit na karna na apni lust gratify karna), aur ek good-tempered aadmi ke (jaise doosre ko strike na karna na evil speak karna), aur similarly doosri virtues aur wickedness ke forms ke respect mein bhi, kuch acts commanding aur doosre forbidding; aur rightly-framed law ye rightly karti hai, aur hastily conceived wali kam well karti hai.

Justice ka ye form, to, complete virtue hai, halaanki bina qualification ke nahi, balki kisi doosre ke reference mein. Aur isliye justice ko aksar virtues mein sabse greatest maana jaata hai, aur 'na evening na morning star' itna wonderful hai; aur proverbially 'justice mein har virtue comprehended hai'. Aur ye apni fullest sense mein complete virtue hai kyunki ye complete virtue ka actual exercise hai. Ye complete hai kyunki jo ise possess karta hai wo apni virtue na sirf khud mein balki doosre ke prati bhi exercise kar sakta hai; kyunki bahut se men apni khud ki affairs mein virtue exercise kar sakte hain, lekin doosron ke prati apne relations mein nahi. Isi wajah se Bias ki saying true lagti hai, ki 'rule aadmi ko dikhaayega'; kyunki ek ruler necessarily doosre men ke relation mein hai, aur ek society ka member. Isi same reason ke liye justice, virtues mein akeli, 'doosre ka good' maani jaati hai, kyunki ye doosre se related hai; kyunki ye wo karti hai jo doosre ke liye advantageous hai, chahe ek ruler ho ya ek co-partner.

Ab worst aadmi wo hai jo apni wickedness khud ke prati bhi aur apne friends ke prati bhi exercise karta hai, aur best aadmi wo nahi hai jo apni virtue khud ke prati exercise karta hai balki wo jo ise doosre ke prati exercise karta hai; kyunki ye ek difficult task hai. Justice is sense mein, to, virtue ka part nahi balki poori virtue hai, na hi contrary injustice vice ka part hai balki poora vice hai. Is sense mein virtue aur justice ke beech kya difference hai ye jo humne kaha usse plain hai; wo same hain lekin unka essence same nahi hai; jo, ek doosre ke relation ke roop mein, justice hai, wo, bina qualification ke ek certain kism ki state ke roop mein, virtue hai.

**Just as the fair and equal: distributive aur rectificatory justice mein divided**

**2.** Lekin sab surat mein jo hum investigate kar rahe hain wo justice hai jo virtue ka ek part hai; kyunki is kism ki ek justice hai, jaisa hum maintain karte hain. Similarly injustice ke particular sense mein bhi hum concerned hain. Ki aisi koi cheez hai ye is fact se indicate hota hai ki jabki jo aadmi wickedness ke doosre forms action mein exhibit karta hai wo wrongly act karta hai indeed, lekin graspingly nahi (jaise jo aadmi cowardice ki wajah se apna shield fenkta hai ya bad temper ki wajah se harshly speak karta hai ya meanness ki wajah se ek friend ko money se help karne mein fail karta hai), jab ek aadmi graspingly act karta hai wo often in vices mein se koi bhi exhibit nahi karta — na, na hi sab saath, lekin certainly ek kism ki wickedness (kyunki hum use blame karte hain) aur injustice. Isliye ek aur kism ki injustice hai jo wide sense mein injustice ka ek part hai, aur 'unjust' word ka ek use jo wide sense mein unjust ke 'contrary to the law' wale part ke corresponding hai. Phir, agar ek aadmi gain ki khaatir adultery commit karta hai aur isse money banaata hai, jabki doosra appetite ke bidding par aisa karta hai halaanki wo money lose karta hai aur iske liye penalize kiya jaata hai, doosre wale ko self-indulgent maana jaayega grasping se zyada, lekin pehla unjust hai, lekin self-indulgent nahi; evidently, isliye, wo unjust hai apne act se gain karne ki wajah se. Phir, doosre sab unjust acts kisi na kisi particular kind ki wickedness ko ascribe kiye jaate hain, jaise adultery ko self-indulgence, battle mein comrade ke desertion ko cowardice, physical violence ko anger; lekin agar ek aadmi gain karta hai, uski action ko wickedness ke kisi form ko nahi balki injustice ko ascribe kiya jaata hai. Evidently, isliye, wide sense ki injustice ke alawa ek aur, 'particular', injustice hai jo pehle ka naam aur nature share karti hai, kyunki iski definition same genus ke andar aati hai; kyunki dono ki significance ek doosre ke relation mein hai, lekin ek honour ya money ya safety se concerned hai — ya jo in sab ko include karti hai, agar humare paas iske liye ek single naam ho — aur iska motive wo pleasure hai jo gain se arise hoti hai; jabki doosri un sab objects se concerned hai jinse good aadmi concerned hai.

Ye clear hai, to, ki justice ki ek se zyada kism hai, aur ki ek hai jo poori virtue se distinct hai; humein try karna chahiye ki ye kya hai aur kis kism ki cheez hai.

Unjust ko unlawful aur unfair mein divide kiya gaya hai, aur just ko lawful aur fair mein. Unlawful ke corresponding pehle mentioned sense of injustice hai. Lekin kyunki unfair aur unlawful same nahi hain, balki different hain jaise ek part apne whole se hota hai (kyunki jo bhi unfair hai wo unlawful hai, lekin jo unlawful hai wo sab unfair nahi hai), unjust aur unfair sense mein injustice pehle kism se same nahi hain balki different hain, part se whole ki tarah; kyunki is sense mein injustice wide sense ki injustice ka ek part hai, aur similarly ek sense mein justice doosre sense ki justice ka ek part hai.

Isliye humein particular justice aur particular injustice ke baare mein bhi baat karni chahiye, aur similarly just aur unjust ke baare mein bhi. Justice, to, jo poori virtue ke corresponding hai, aur corresponding injustice, ek poori virtue ka exercise hote hue, aur doosri poore vice ka, doosre ke prati, humein ek taraf chhod dena chahiye. Aur kaise 'just' aur 'unjust' ke meanings jo inhe corresponding hain distinguish kiye jaayein ye evident hai; kyunki practically law dwara commanded acts ki majority wo hain jo virtue ko poore ke roop mein liye gaye point of view se prescribe kiye gaye hain; kyunki law humein har virtue practise karne ka order deti hai aur har vice ko practise karne se forbid karti hai. Aur jo cheezein poori virtue produce karne ki tendency rakhti hain wo un acts mein se hain jo law dwara prescribe kiye gaye hain common good ke liye education ke view se. Lekin individual ki education ke respect mein jo use bina qualification ke ek good aadmi banati hai, humein baad mein determine karna chahiye ki ye political art ka function hai ya kisi aur ka; kyunki shayad ek good aadmi hona aur kisi bhi random state ka ek good citizen hona same na ho.

Particular justice ka, aur is corresponding sense mein just cheez ka, (A) ek kism wo hai jo honour ya money ya doosri cheezon ke distributions mein manifest hoti hai jo constitution mein share rakhne walon ke beech divide hone wali hain (kyunki inme ek aadmi ke paas doosre ke equal ya unequal ek share hona possible hai), aur (B) ek wo hai jo man aur man ke beech transactions mein ek rectifying part play karti hai. Iske do divisions hain; transactions ke (1) kuch voluntary hain aur (2) doosre involuntary — voluntary jaise sale, purchase, loan for consumption, pledging, loan for use, depositing, letting (inhe voluntary kaha jaata hai kyunki in transactions ka origin voluntary hai), jabki involuntary mein se (a) kuch clandestine hain, jaise theft, adultery, poisoning, procuring, slaves ka enticement, assassination, false witness, aur (b) doosre force involve karte hain, jaise assault, imprisonment, murder, robbery with violence, mutilation, abuse, insult.

**Distributive justice, geometrical proportion ke according**

**3.** (A) Humne dikhaya hai ki dono unjust aadmi aur unjust act unfair ya unequal hain; ab ye clear hai ki dono unequals ke beech bhi ek intermediate hai jo har case mein involve hota hai. Aur ye equal hai; kyunki kisi bhi kism ki action mein jisme ek more aur ek less hai wahan ek equal bhi hai. Agar, to, unjust unequal hai, just equal hai, jaisa sab men suppose karte hain, argument ke bina bhi. Aur kyunki equal intermediate hai, just ek intermediate hoga. Ab equality kam se kam do cheezon ko imply karti hai. Just, to, dono intermediate aur equal aur relative hona chahiye (yani, certain persons ke liye). Aur intermediate hone ke naate ye certain cheezon ke beech hona chahiye (jo respectively greater aur less hain); equal hone ke naate ye do cheezein involve karta hai; just hone ke naate ye certain people ke liye hai. Just, isliye, kam se kam char terms involve karta hai; kyunki wo persons jinke liye ye actually just hai do hain, aur cheezein jinme ye manifest hai, distributed objects, do hain.

Aur wahi equality persons ke beech bhi hogi aur concerned cheezon ke beech bhi; kyunki jaise doosri — concerned cheezein — related hain, waise hi pehli bhi; agar wo equal nahi hain, unke paas jo equal hai wo nahi hoga, lekin yahi quarrels aur complaints ka origin hai — jab ya to equals ke paas unequal shares hain aur unhe award kiye jaate hain, ya un-equals ke paas equal shares. Further, ye plain hai is fact se ki awards 'merit ke according' hone chahiye; kyunki sab men agree karte hain ki distribution mein just kya hai ye kisi na kisi sense mein merit ke according hona chahiye, halaanki wo sab same kism ka merit specify nahi karte, lekin democrats ise freeman ke status se identify karte hain, oligarchy ke supporters wealth se (ya noble birth se), aur aristocracy ke supporters virtue se.

Just, to, proportionate ki ek species hai (proportion sirf abstract units se consist hone wale number ki kism ki property nahi hai, balki number ki general mein). Kyunki proportion ratios ki equality hai, aur kam se kam char terms involve karti hai (ki discrete proportion char terms involve karti hai ye plain hai, lekin continuous proportion bhi karti hai, kyunki ye ek term ko do ki tarah use karti hai aur ise do baar mention karti hai; jaise 'jaise line A hai line B ke liye, waise hi line B hai line C ke liye'; line B, to, do baar mentioned hui hai, isliye agar line B do baar assume ki jaaye, proportional terms char honge); aur just bhi, kam se kam char terms involve karta hai, aur ek pair ke beech ka ratio doosre pair ke beech ke ratio jaisa hi hai; kyunki persons ke beech aur cheezon ke beech ek similar distinction hai. Jaise term A, to, B se hai, waise hi C hoga D se, aur isliye, alternando, jaise A C se hai, B D se hoga. Isliye whole bhi same ratio mein whole se hai; aur distribution unhe is tarah pair karti hai, aur agar wo is tarah combine kiye jaayein, unhe justly pair karti hai. Term A ka C ke saath aur B ka D ke saath conjunction, to, distribution mein just kya hai wahi hai, aur just ki ye species intermediate hai, aur unjust wo hai jo proportion violate karta hai; kyunki proportional intermediate hai, aur just proportional hai. (Mathematicians is kism ki proportion ko geometrical kehte hain; kyunki geometrical proportion mein ye follow karta hai ki whole whole se hai jaise ki koi bhi part corresponding part se hai.) Ye proportion continuous nahi hai; kyunki humein ek single term nahi milta jo ek person aur ek cheez dono ke liye stand kare.

Ye, to, wahi hai jo just hai — proportional; unjust wo hai jo proportion violate karta hai. Isi wajah se ek term too great ban jaata hai, doosra too small, jaisa indeed practice mein hota hai; kyunki jo aadmi unjustly act karta hai uske paas too much hai, aur jise unjustly treat kiya jaata hai uske paas too little hai, us cheez ka jo good hai. Evil ke case mein reverse true hai; kyunki lesser evil ek good ki tarah greater evil ke comparison mein reckon kiya jaata hai, kyunki lesser evil greater se zyada choose karne layak hai, aur jo choice ka worthy hai wo good hai, aur jo choice ka zyada worthy hai wo ek greater good hai.

Ye, to, just ki ek species hai.

**Rectificatory justice, arithmetical proportion ke according**

**4.** (B) Reh jaane wali ek hai rectificatory, jo dono voluntary aur involuntary transactions ke connection mein arise hoti hai. Just ka ye form pehle wale se ek different specific character rakhta hai. Kyunki wo justice jo common possessions ko distribute karti hai wo hamesha upar mentioned proportion ki kism ke according hai (kyunki us case mein bhi jisme distribution ek partnership ke common funds se ki jaati hai ye same ratio ke according hoga jo partners dwara business mein put ki gayi funds ek doosre se hoti hain); aur is kism ki justice ke against opposed injustice wo hai jo proportion violate karti hai. Lekin man aur man ke beech transactions mein justice ek kism ki equality hi hai, aur injustice ek kism ki inequality; us kism ki proportion ke according nahi, phir bhi, balki arithmetical proportion ke according. Kyunki isse koi farak nahi padta ki ek good aadmi ne ek bad aadmi ko defraud kiya hai ya ek bad aadmi ne ek good ko, na hi ki ye ek good ya ek bad aadmi hai jisne adultery commit ki hai; law sirf injury ke distinctive character ko dekhti hai, aur parties ko equal treat karti hai, agar ek wrong mein hai aur doosra wronged ho raha hai, aur agar ek ne injury inflict ki aur doosre ne ise receive kiya. Isliye, is kism ki injustice ek inequality hone ke naate, judge ise equalize karne ki koshish karta hai; kyunki us case mein bhi jisme ek ne receive kiya hai aur doosre ne ek wound inflict ki hai, ya ek ne slay kiya hai aur doosra slain hua hai, suffering aur action unequally distributed hue hain; lekin judge penalty ke means se cheezon ko equalize karne ki koshish karta hai, assailant ke gain se le kar. Kyunki term 'gain' aise cases par generally apply hoti hai — even agar ye kisi certain cases ke liye appropriate term na ho, jaise us person ke liye jo ek wound inflict karta hai — aur 'loss' sufferer ko; sab surat mein jab suffering estimate ki jaa chuki ho, ek ko loss kaha jaata hai aur doosre ko gain. Isliye equal greater aur less ke beech intermediate hai, lekin gain aur loss respectively greater aur less hain contrary ways mein; good ka zyada aur evil ka kam gain hai, aur contrary loss hai; inke beech intermediate hai, jaisa humne dekha, equal, jise hum kehte hain just hai; isliye rectification mein just intermediate hoga loss aur gain ke beech. Isi wajah se, jab log dispute karte hain, wo judge ke paas refuge lete hain; aur judge ke paas jaana justice ke paas jaana hai; kyunki judge ki nature ek kism ki animate justice hona hai; aur wo judge ko ek intermediate ke roop mein seek karte hain, aur kuch states mein wo judges ko mediators kehte hain, is assumption par ki agar unhe jo intermediate hai wo milta hai to unhe jo just hai wo milega. Just, to, ek intermediate hai, kyunki judge aisa hai. Ab judge equality restore karta hai; ye jaisa ki ek line unequal parts mein divided ho, aur usne wo hataya jisse greater segment half se exceed karta hai, aur ise smaller segment mein add kar diya. Aur jab whole equally divided ho chuka hai, tab wo kehte hain unke paas 'apna khud ka' hai — yani jab unhe wahi milta hai jo equal hai. Equal greater aur lesser line ke beech intermediate hai arithmetical proportion ke according. Isi reason se ise just (dikaion) bhi kaha jaata hai, kyunki ye do equal parts (dikha) mein ek division hai, jaise koi ise dikhaion kahe; aur judge (dikastēs) wo hai jo bisect karta hai (dikhastēs). Kyunki jab kuch do equals mein se ek se subtract kiya jaata hai aur doosre mein add kiya jaata hai, doosra in do se excess mein hota hai; kyunki agar jo ek se liya gaya tha wo doosre mein add na kiya gaya hota, doosra sirf ek se excess mein hota. Ye isliye intermediate ko ek se exceed karta hai, aur intermediate us se ek se exceed karta hai jisse kuch liya gaya tha. Isse, to, hum recognize karenge ki us cheez se humein kya subtract karna hai jiske paas zyada hai, aur us cheez mein kya add karna hai jiske paas kam hai; humein doosre mein wo add karna chahiye jisse intermediate use exceed karta hai, aur greatest se wo subtract karna chahiye jisse ye intermediate ko exceed karta hai.

In names, dono loss aur gain, voluntary exchange se aaye hain; kyunki apni khud ki cheez se zyada rakhna gaining kehlaata hai, aur apni original share se kam rakhna losing kehlaata hai, jaise buying aur selling mein aur doosre sab matters mein jisme law ne logo ko free chhoda hai apni khud ki terms banaane ke liye; lekin jab unhe na zyada na kam milta hai balki bilkul wahi jo khud unka hai, wo kehte hain ki unke paas apna khud ka hai aur ki wo na lose karte hain na gain.

Isliye just ek kism ke gain aur ek kism ke loss ke beech intermediate hai, namely, wo jo involuntary hain; ye transaction se pehle aur baad ek equal amount rakhne mein consist karta hai.

**Exchange mein justice, reciprocity**

**5.** Kuch log sochte hain ki reciprocity bina qualification ke just hai, jaisa Pythagoreans ne kaha; kyunki unhone justice ko bina qualification ke reciprocity ke roop mein define kiya. Ab 'reciprocity' na to distributive na hi rectificatory justice ke fit hoti hai — phir bhi log chahte hain ki even Rhadamanthus ki justice ka matlab yahi ho: 'Agar koi aadmi jo usne kiya wo suffer kare, right justice ho jaayegi' — kyunki bahut se cases mein reciprocity aur rectificatory justice accord mein nahi hain; jaise (1) agar ek official ne ek wound inflict kiya hai, use return mein wounded nahi hona chahiye, aur agar kisi ne ek official ko wound kiya hai, use na sirf wounded balki additionally punished kiya jaana chahiye. Further (2) ek voluntary aur ek involuntary act ke beech ek great difference hai. Lekin exchange ke liye associations mein is kism ki justice men ko together hold karti hai — reciprocity ek proportion ke according, na ki precisely equal return ke basis par. Kyunki proportionate requital se hi city together hold hoti hai. Men seek karte hain ya to evil ke liye evil return karna — aur agar wo aisa na kar sakein, apni position ko mere slavery samajhte hain — ya good ke liye good — aur agar wo aisa na kar sakein to koi exchange nahi hai, lekin exchange se hi wo together hold hote hain. Isi wajah se wo Graces ke temple ko ek prominent place dete hain — services ke requital ko promote karne ke liye; kyunki ye grace ka characteristic hai — humein return mein us aadmi ki serve karni chahiye jisne humpar grace show ki hai, aur kisi doosre time isse show karne mein initiative leni chahiye.

Ab proportionate return cross-conjunction se secured hoti hai. Let A ek builder ho, B ek shoemaker, C ek house, D ek shoe. Builder, to, shoemaker se uska kaam paana chahiye, aur khud return mein use apna khud ka dena chahiye. Agar, to, pehle goods ki proportionate equality hai, aur phir reciprocal action hoti hai, jo result humne mention kiya wo effect hoga. Agar nahi, bargain equal nahi hai, aur hold nahi karti; kyunki isse rokne ke liye kuch nahi hai ki ek ka kaam doosre se better ho; unhe isliye equate kiya jaana chahiye. (Aur ye doosre arts ke liye bhi true hai; kyunki wo destroy ho gaye hote agar patient ne jo suffer kiya wo bilkul waisa na hota jo agent ne kiya, aur same amount aur kind mein na hota.) Kyunki exchange ke liye associate karne wale do doctors nahi hain, balki ek doctor aur ek farmer, ya generally log jo different aur unequal hain; lekin inhe equate kiya jaana chahiye. Isi wajah se sab cheezein jo exchange ki jaati hain unhe somehow comparable hona chahiye. Isi end ke liye money introduce ki gayi hai, aur ye ek sense mein ek intermediate ban jaata hai; kyunki ye sab cheezein measure karta hai, aur isliye excess aur defect bhi — kitne shoes ek house ke equal hain ya food ki ek diye gayi amount ke. Ek house ke liye [ya food ki ek diye gayi amount ke liye] exchange kiye gaye shoes ki number, isliye, builder aur shoemaker ke ratio ke corresponding honi chahiye. Kyunki agar aisa na ho, koi exchange nahi hoga aur koi intercourse nahi. Aur ye proportion effect nahi hogi jab tak goods somehow equal na hon. Sab goods, isliye, kisi ek cheez se measure kiye jaane chahiye, jaisa humne pehle kaha. Ab ye unit truth mein need hai, jo sab cheezon ko together hold karti hai (kyunki agar men ek doosre ke goods ki koi zaroorat na rakhte, ya unki equally zaroorat na rakhte, to ya to koi exchange na hoti ya same exchange na hoti); lekin money convention se need ka ek kism ka representative ban gayi hai; aur isi wajah se iska naam 'money' (nomisma) hai — kyunki ye nature se nahi balki law (nomos) se exist karti hai aur ye humari power mein hai ise change karna aur useless banana. Reciprocity, to, hogi jab terms equate ki gayi hongi taaki jaise farmer shoemaker se hai, waise hi shoemaker ke kaam ki amount farmer ke kaam se ho jiske badle isse exchange kiya jaata hai. Lekin humein unhe ek proportion ki figure mein tab nahi laana chahiye jab wo already exchange kar chuke hon (nahi to ek extreme dono excesses rakhega), balki jab unke paas abhi bhi apna khud ka goods ho. Isi tarah wo equals aur associates hain kyunki ye equality unke case mein effect ki ja sakti hai. Let A ek farmer ho, C food, B ek shoemaker, D uska product jo C ke equate kiya gaya hai. Agar aisa possible na hota ki reciprocity is tarah effect ki jaaye, parties ka koi association na hota. Ki need cheezon ko ek single unit ki tarah together hold karti hai ye is fact se dikhta hai ki jab men ek doosre ki zaroorat nahi rakhte, yani jab na to koi doosre ki zaroorat rakhta hai ya ek doosre ki zaroorat nahi rakhta, wo exchange nahi karte, jaise hum tab karte hain jab koi wo chahta hai jo khud humare paas hai, jaise jab log corn ki exportation permit karte hain wine ke exchange mein. Ye equation isliye establish kiya jaana chahiye.

Aur future exchange ke liye — ki agar humein ek cheez ki zaroorat abhi nahi hai to humare paas wo hogi jab bhi humein iski zaroorat ho — money jaise ki hamari surety hai; kyunki humare liye possible hona chahiye ki money le kar hum jo chahte hain wo paayein. Ab wahi cheez money ke saath bhi hoti hai jo goods ke saath hoti hai — ye hamesha same worth nahi hoti; phir bhi ye zyada steady rehne ki tendency rakhti hai. Isi wajah se sab goods par ek price set kiya jaana chahiye; kyunki tab hamesha exchange hogi, aur agar aisa hai, to man aur man ka association hoga.

Money, to, ek measure ki tarah act karte hue, goods ko commensurate banata hai aur equate karta hai; kyunki na to koi association hota agar koi exchange na hoti, na exchange agar koi equality na hoti, na equality agar koi commensurability na hoti. Ab truth mein ye impossible hai ki cheezein jo itni differ karti hain wo commensurate ban jaayein, lekin need ke reference mein wo sufficiently aisa ban sakti hain. Ek unit hona chahiye, to, aur wo agreement se fix ki gayi (isi reason se ise money kaha jaata hai); kyunki yahi hai jo sab cheezon ko commensurate banata hai, kyunki sab cheezein money se measure ki jaati hain. Let A ek house ho, B das minae, C ek bed. A B ka half hai, agar house five minae ka worth hai ya inke equal hai; bed, C, B ka ek tenth hai; ye plain hai, to, kitne beds ek house ke equal hain, namely, five. Ki exchange money se pehle isi tarah hoti thi ye plain hai; kyunki isse koi farak nahi padta ki ye five beds hain jo ek house ke exchange mein aate hain, ya five beds ki money value.

Humne ab unjust aur just define kar diya hai. Ye ek doosre se mark off kiye jaane ke baad, ye plain hai ki just action unjustly act karne aur unjustly treat kiye jaane ke beech intermediate hai; kyunki ek ke paas too much hai aur doosre ke paas too little. Justice ek kism ka mean hai, lekin doosri virtues ki tarah nahi, balki kyunki ye ek intermediate amount se relate karti hai, jabki injustice extremes se relate karti hai. Aur justice wo hai jiski wajah se just aadmi ko kaha jaata hai ek doer jo choice se just hai use karta hai, aur ek jo khud aur doosre ke beech ya do doosron ke beech distribute karega is tarah nahi ki khud ko usse zyada desirable de aur doosre ko kam (aur conversely harmful ke saath), balki is tarah ki proportion ke according jo equal hai wahi de; aur similarly do doosre persons ke beech distribute karne mein. Injustice, doosri taraf, similarly unjust se related hai, jo excess aur defect hai, proportion ke contrary, useful ya hurtful ka. Isi reason ke liye injustice excess aur defect hai, namely, kyunki ye excess aur defect ka productive hai — apne khud ke case mein us cheez ka excess jo apni khud ki nature mein useful hai aur us cheez ka defect jo hurtful hai, jabki doosron ke case mein ye poore ke roop mein waisa hi hai jaisa khud ke case mein hai, lekin proportion kisi bhi direction mein violate ki ja sakti hai. Unjust act mein too little rakhna unjustly treated hona hai; too much rakhna unjustly act karna hai.

Ise humara justice aur injustice ki nature ka account maan lete hain, aur similarly generally just aur unjust ka.

**Political justice aur analogous kism ki justice**

**6.** Kyunki unjustly act karna necessarily imply nahi karta ki doer unjust hai, humein poochna chahiye kis kism ke unjust acts imply karte hain ki doer unjust hai har type ki injustice ke respect mein, jaise ek thief, ek adulterer, ya ek brigand. Surely jawaab in types ke beech ke difference par turn nahi karta. Kyunki ek aadmi ek woman ke saath lie kar sakta hai ye jaante hue ki wo kaun hai, lekin uske act ka origin deliberate choice nahi balki passion ho sakta hai. Wo unjustly, to, act karta hai, lekin unjust nahi hai; jaise ek aadmi thief nahi hai, phir bhi usne steal kiya; na adulterer, phir bhi usne adultery commit ki; aur similarly doosre sab cases mein.

Ab humne previously state kiya hai ki reciprocal just se kaise related hai; lekin humein ye nahi bhoolna chahiye ki hum jo dhoondh rahe hain wo sirf bina qualification ke just nahi hai balki political justice bhi hai. Ye un men mein milti hai jo apni life self-sufficiency ke view se share karte hain, men jo free hain aur ya to proportionately ya arithmetically equal hain, isliye jo is condition ko fulfil nahi karte unke beech koi political justice nahi hai balki ek special sense mein aur analogy se justice hai. Kyunki justice sirf un men ke beech exist karti hai jinke mutual relations law se governed hote hain; aur law un men ke liye exist karta hai jinke beech injustice hai; kyunki legal justice just aur unjust ka discrimination hai. Aur un men ke beech jinke beech injustice ki jaati hai unjust action bhi hai (halaanki sab in ke beech injustice nahi hai jinke beech unjust action hai), aur ye khud ko usse zyada assign karna hai jo khud mein good hai aur usse kam jo khud mein evil hai. Isi wajah se hum ek aadmi ko rule karne nahi dete, balki rational principle ko, kyunki ek aadmi is tarah apne interests mein behave karta hai aur ek tyrant ban jaata hai. Magistrate doosri taraf justice ka guardian hai, aur, agar justice ka, to equality ka bhi. Aur kyunki use apne share se zyada nahi rakhne wale ke roop mein assume kiya jaata hai, agar wo just hai (kyunki wo khud ko usse zyada assign nahi karta jo khud mein good hai, jab tak aisa share uske merits ke proportional na ho — isliye ye doosron ke liye hai ki wo labour karta hai, aur isi reason se log, jaisa humne previously state kiya, kehte hain justice 'doosre ka good' hai), isliye use ek reward diya jaana chahiye, aur ye honour aur privilege hai; lekin jinke liye aisi cheezein enough nahi hain wo tyrants ban jaate hain.

Ek master ki justice aur ek father ki justice citizens ki justice se same nahi hain, halaanki wo iske jaisi hain; kyunki bina qualification ke sense mein apni khud ki cheezon ke prati koi injustice nahi ho sakti, lekin ek aadmi ka chattel, aur uska child ek certain age tak jab tak wo khud ke liye set up nahi karta, uske part jaise hain, aur koi bhi khud ko hurt karne ke liye choose nahi karta (isi reason se khud ke prati koi injustice nahi ho sakti). Isliye citizens ki justice ya injustice in relations mein manifest nahi hoti; kyunki ye, jaisa humne dekha, law ke according thi, aur un logo ke beech jo naturally law ke subject hain, aur ye, jaisa humne dekha, wo log hain jinke paas ruling aur ruled hone mein ek equal share hai. Isliye justice ek wife ke prati children aur chattels se zyada truly manifest ho sakti hai, kyunki pehla household justice hai; lekin ye bhi political justice se different hai.

**Natural aur legal justice**

**7.** Political justice ka part natural hai, part legal — natural, wo jo har jagah same force rakhta hai aur logo ke ye ya wo sochne se exist nahi karta; legal, wo jo originally indifferent hai, lekin jab laid down ho chuka hai to indifferent nahi hai, jaise ki ek prisoner ka ransom ek mina hoga, ya ki ek goat aur do sheep nahi sacrifice ki jaayegi, aur phir sab laws jo particular cases ke liye pass ki jaati hain, jaise ki Brasidas ke honour mein sacrifice ki jaayegi, aur decrees ke provisions. Ab kuch log sochte hain ki saari justice is kism ki hai, kyunki jo nature se hai wo unchangeable hai aur har jagah same force rakhta hai (jaise fire yahan bhi jalti hai aur Persia mein bhi), jabki wo just ke roop mein recognize ki gayi cheezon mein change dekhte hain. Ye, phir bhi, is bina qualification ke way mein true nahi hai, balki ek sense mein true hai; ya better, gods ke saath ye shayad bilkul bhi true nahi hai, jabki humare saath kuch aisa hai jo nature se bhi just hai, phir bhi iska sab kuch changeable hai; lekin phir bhi kuch nature se hai, kuch nahi. Ye evident hai ki, un cheezon mein se jo otherwise ho sakti hain, kaunsi nature se hai; aur kaunsi nahi balki legal aur conventional hai, dono ko equally changeable maante hue. Aur doosri sab cheezon mein bhi wahi distinction apply hogi; nature se right hand stronger hai, phir bhi ye possible hai ki sab men ambidextrous ban jaayein. Wo cheezein jo convention aur expediency ki wajah se just hain wo measures jaisi hain; kyunki wine aur corn measures har jagah equal nahi hain, balki wholesale mein larger hain aur retail markets mein smaller. Similarly, wo cheezein jo nature se nahi balki human enactment se just hain wo har jagah same nahi hain, kyunki constitutions bhi same nahi hain, halaanki ek hi hai jo har jagah nature se best hai.

Just aur lawful cheezon mein se har ek particulars ke universal se related hai; kyunki jo cheezein ki jaati hain wo many hain, lekin har type ek hai, kyunki ye universal hai.

Injustice ke act aur unjust cheez ke beech ek difference hai, aur justice ke act aur just cheez ke beech; kyunki ek cheez nature se ya enactment se unjust hai; aur yahi cheez, jab ye ki jaa chuki hai, injustice ka ek act hai, lekin jab tak ye ki nahi jaati wo abhi wo nahi balki unjust hai. Isi tarah, justice ke act ke saath bhi (halaanki general term zyada 'just action' hai, aur 'act of justice' injustice ke act ke correction ke liye apply hota hai).

In mein se har ek ko baad mein separately examine kiya jaana chahiye iski species ki nature aur number ke respect mein aur un cheezon ki nature ke respect mein jinse ye concerned hai.

## JUSTICE: ITS INNER NATURE AS INVOLVING CHOICE

**Wrongdoing ke degrees ka scale**

**8.** Just aur unjust acts jaisa humne describe kiya hai, ek aadmi unjustly ya justly act karta hai jab bhi wo aise acts voluntarily karta hai; jab involuntarily, wo na unjustly na justly act karta hai siwaye ek incidental tareeke se; kyunki wo aisi cheezein karta hai jo just ya unjust hone ka happen hota hai. Chahe ek act injustice ka (ya justice ka) hai ya nahi ye uski voluntariness ya involuntariness se determine hota hai; kyunki jab ye voluntary hai ye blame kiya jaata hai, aur usi waqt ye tab injustice ka ek act bhi hai; isliye aisi cheezein hongi jo unjust hain lekin abhi injustice ke acts nahi, agar voluntariness bhi present na ho. Voluntary se mera matlab hai, jaisa pehle bhi kaha ja chuka hai, kisi bhi cheez se jo ek aadmi ki khud ki power mein hai aur wo ise knowledge ke saath karta hai, yani na to person ke ignorance mein jispar act kiya gaya hai na hi instrument ke jo use kiya gaya, na hi end ke jo attain hoga (jaise wo kis par strike kar raha hai, kis se, aur kis end tak), aisi har act ka incidentally na hona aur na hi forced hona (jaise agar A B ka hand leta hai aur usse C ko strike karta hai, B voluntarily act nahi karta; kyunki act uski khud ki power mein nahi tha). Struck person striker ka father ho sakta hai, aur striker ko pata ho sakta hai ki ye ek man hai ya present logo mein se ek, lekin ye pata na ho ki ye uska father hai; ek similar distinction end ke case mein bhi ki ja sakti hai, aur poori action ke respect mein bhi. Isliye jo ignorance mein kiya jaata hai, ya ignorance mein kiye bina bhi agent ki power mein nahi hai, ya forced hai, wo involuntary hai (kyunki bahut si natural processes bhi, hum knowingly perform ya undergo karte hain, jinme se koi bhi voluntary ya involuntary nahi hai; jaise old age ya dying). Lekin unjust aur just acts dono ke case mein injustice ya justice sirf incidental ho sakti hai; kyunki ek aadmi unwillingly aur fear se ek deposit return kar sakta hai, aur tab isse ye nahi kaha jaana chahiye ki wo just kar raha hai ya justly act kar raha hai, siwaye ek incidental tareeke se. Similarly jo aadmi compulsion ke under aur unwillingly deposit return karne mein fail karta hai use unjustly act karna aur unjust karna kaha jaana chahiye, sirf incidentally. Voluntary acts mein se hum kuch choice se karte hain, doosre choice se nahi; choice se wo jo hum deliberation ke baad karte hain, choice se nahi wo jo hum bina previous deliberation ke karte hain. Isliye man aur man ke beech transactions mein injury ki teen kisms hain; ignorance involve karne wali mistakes hain jab person acted on, act, instrument, ya attained end wo hai jo agent ne suppose kiya usse different hai; agent ne socha tha ki ya to wo kisi ko hit nahi kar raha ya wo is missile se hit nahi kar raha ya is person ko hit nahi kar raha ya is end tak nahi, lekin ek result follow hua doosra jo usne socha tha likely hoga (jaise usne wound karne ke intent se throw nahi kiya balki sirf prick karne ke), ya hit person ya missile doosra tha jo usne suppose kiya tha. Ab jab injury reasonable expectation ke contrary hoti hai, ye ek misadventure hai. Jab ye reasonable expectation ke contrary nahi hai, lekin vice imply nahi karti, ye ek mistake hai (kyunki ek aadmi mistake karta hai jab fault khud usme originate hoti hai, lekin misfortune ka victim hai jab origin uske bahar hai). Jab wo knowledge ke saath act karta hai lekin deliberation ke baad nahi, ye injustice ka ek act hai — jaise anger ya doosre passions ki wajah se hone wale acts jo man ke liye necessary ya natural hain; kyunki jab men aise harmful aur mistaken acts karte hain wo unjustly act karte hain, aur acts injustice ke acts hain, lekin isse ye imply nahi hota ki doers unjust ya wicked hain; kyunki injury vice ki wajah se nahi hai. Lekin jab ek aadmi choice se act karta hai, wo ek unjust aadmi aur ek vicious aadmi hai.

Isi wajah se anger se proceed karne wale acts ko rightly judge kiya jaata hai ki wo malice aforethought se nahi kiye jaate; kyunki mischief shuru karne wala wo aadmi nahi hai jo anger mein act karta hai balki wo jisne use enrage kiya. Phir, dispute mein matter ye nahi hai ki cheez hui ya nahi, balki iski justice; kyunki ye apparent injustice hai jo rage occasion karti hai. Kyunki wo act ki occurrence ke baare mein dispute nahi karte — jaise commercial transactions mein jahan do parties mein se ek ko vicious hona chahiye jab tak forgetfulness na ho; balki, fact ke baare mein agree karte hue, wo dispute karte hain ki kis side justice hai (jabki jis aadmi ne deliberately doosre ko injure kiya hai wo ye jaanne se bach nahi sakta ki usne aisa kiya hai), isliye ek sochta hai ki uske saath unjustly treat kiya ja raha hai aur doosra disagree karta hai.

Lekin agar ek aadmi choice se doosre ko harm karta hai, wo unjustly act karta hai; aur ye injustice ke acts hain jo imply karte hain ki doer ek unjust aadmi hai, agar act proportion ya equality violate karta hai. Similarly, ek aadmi just hai jab wo choice se justly act karta hai; lekin wo justly act karta hai agar wo simply voluntarily act karta hai.

Involuntary acts mein se kuch excusable hain, doosre nahi. Kyunki mistakes jo men na sirf ignorance mein balki ignorance ke reason se bhi karte hain excusable hain, jabki wo jo men ignorance ke reason se nahi (halaanki wo unhe ignorance mein karte hain) balki ek passion ki wajah se karte hain jo na natural hai na hi is kism ki jiske man liable hain, excusable nahi hain.

**Kya kisi insaan ke saath voluntarily unjustly treat kiya ja sakta hai? Kya distribution mein injustice ka guilty distributor hai ya recipient? Justice utni aasan nahi hai jitni lag sakti hai, kyunki ye acting ka ek tarika nahi balki ek inner disposition hai**

**9.** Assume karte hue ki humne sufficiently define kiya hai injustice ka suffering aur doing, ye poocha ja sakta hai (1) kya truth Euripides ke paradoxical words mein expressed hai: 'Maine apni mother ko slay kiya, yahi mera tale hai brief mein.' 'Kya tum dono willing the, ya unwilling dono?' Kya truly possible hai willingly unjustly treat kiya jaana, ya kya injustice ka sab suffering iske contrary involuntary hai, jaise sab unjust action voluntary hai? Aur kya injustice ka suffering sab ek kism ka hai ya sab doosre kism ka, ya ye kabhi voluntary hai, kabhi involuntary? Isi tarah, justly treat kiye jaane ke case ke saath bhi; sab just action voluntary hai, isliye ye reasonable hai ki dono cases mein ek similar opposition ho — ki dono unjustly aur justly treat kiye jaane dono ya to alike voluntary hon ya alike involuntary. Lekin ye paradoxical lagega even justly treat kiye jaane ke case mein bhi, agar ye hamesha voluntary hota; kyunki kuch unwillingly justly treat kiye jaate hain. (2) Koi ye sawaal bhi uthaa sakta hai, kya har koi jisne wo suffer kiya jo unjust hai wo unjustly treat kiya ja raha hai, ya doosri taraf ye acting jaisa hi hai. Action aur passivity dono mein justice incidentally kiya jaana possible hai, aur similarly (ye plain hai) injustice bhi; kyunki jo unjust hai use karna unjustly act karne jaisa same nahi hai, na hi jo unjust hai use suffer karna unjustly treat kiye jaane jaisa, aur similarly justly act karne aur justly treat kiye jaane ke case mein bhi; kyunki impossible hai unjustly treat kiya jaana agar doosra unjustly act na kare, ya justly treat kiya jaana jab tak wo justly act na kare. Ab agar unjustly act karna simply kisi ko voluntarily harm karna hai, aur 'voluntarily' ka matlab hai 'person acted on, instrument, aur act karne ke manner ko jaanna', aur incontinent aadmi voluntarily khud ko harm karta hai, na sirf wo voluntarily unjustly treat kiya jaayega balki khud ko unjustly treat karna possible hoga. (Ye bhi doubt mein rakhi gayi questions mein se ek hai, kya ek aadmi khud ko unjustly treat kar sakta hai.) Phir, ek aadmi voluntarily, incontinence ki wajah se, doosre dwara harm kiya ja sakta hai jo voluntarily act karta hai, isliye voluntarily unjustly treat kiya jaana possible hoga. Ya humari definition incorrect hai; kya humein 'doosre ko harm karna, person acted on, instrument, aur manner dono ki knowledge ke saath' mein 'person acted on ki wish ke contrary' add karna chahiye? Tab ek aadmi voluntarily harm ho sakta hai aur voluntarily unjust ko suffer kar sakta hai, lekin koi bhi voluntarily unjustly treat nahi kiya jaata; kyunki koi bhi unjustly treat kiya jaana wish nahi karta, even incontinent aadmi bhi nahi. Wo apni wish ke contrary act karta hai; kyunki koi bhi wo wish nahi karta jise wo good nahi sochta, lekin incontinent aadmi wo cheezein karta hai jo usse nahi sochta ki usse karni chahiye. Phir, jo apna khud ka deta hai, jaise Homer kehta hai Glaucus ne Diomede ko diya 'Gold ke liye armour, brazen ke liye, sau oxen ki price nine ke liye', unjustly treat nahi kiya jaata; kyunki dena uski power mein hai, unjustly treat kiya jaana nahi hai, balki koi hona chahiye jo use unjustly treat kare. Ye plain hai, to, ki unjustly treat kiya jaana voluntary nahi hai.
