Jin sawaalon ko hum discuss karna chahte the unme se do abhi bhi discussion ke liye rehte hain; (3) kya ye wo aadmi hai jisne doosre ko usse zyada assign kiya hai jo unjustly act karta hai, ya wo jiske paas excessive share hai, aur (4) kya khud ko unjustly treat karna possible hai. Ye sawaal connected hain; kyunki agar pehla alternative possible hai aur distributor unjustly act karta hai aur wo aadmi nahi jiske paas excessive share hai, to agar ek aadmi doosre ko khud se zyada assign karta hai, knowingly aur voluntarily, wo khud ko unjustly treat karta hai; jo modest log karte lagte hain, kyunki virtuous aadmi apni share se kam lene ki tendency rakhta hai. Ya kya ye statement bhi qualification chahti hai? Kyunki (a) wo shayad kisi doosre good ka usse zyada share paata hai, jaise reputation ka ya intrinsic nobility ka. (b) Sawaal solve ho jaata hai wahi distinction apply karke jo humne unjust action par apply ki thi; kyunki wo apni khud ki wish ke contrary kuch bhi suffer nahi karta, isliye wo is extent tak unjustly treat nahi kiya jaata, balki zyada se zyada harm hi suffer karta hai.

Ye bhi plain hai ki distributor unjustly act karta hai, lekin hamesha wo aadmi nahi jiske paas excessive share hai; kyunki wo aadmi unjustly act nahi karta jise injustice ki jaati hai, balki wo jiske paas voluntarily unjust act karne ka right hai, yani wo person jisme action ka origin hai, aur ye distributor mein hai, receiver mein nahi. Phir, kyunki word 'do' ambiguous hai, aur ek sense hai jisme lifeless things, ya ek hand, ya ek servant jo order obey karta hai, slay karne wala kaha ja sakta hai, jo excessive share paata hai wo unjustly act nahi karta, halaanki wo unjust 'karta' hai.

Phir, agar distributor ne apna judgement ignorance mein diya, wo legal justice ke respect mein unjustly act nahi karta, aur uska judgement is sense mein unjust nahi hai, lekin ek sense mein ye unjust hai (kyunki law se just kya hai, aur primary way mein, different hain); lekin agar knowledge ke saath usne unjustly judge kiya, to wo khud gratitude ka ya revenge ka ek excessive share aim kar raha hai. Utna hi, to, jaise wo plunder mein share karega, jis aadmi ne in reasons ke liye unjustly judge kiya hai usne too much paaya hai; ki jo wo paata hai wo different hai jo wo distribute karta hai isse koi farak nahi padta, kyunki agar wo plunder mein share karne ke view se land award karta hai to wo land nahi money paata hai.

Men sochte hain ki unjustly act karna unki power mein hai, aur isliye ki just hona easy hai. Lekin ye nahi hai; apne neighbour ki wife ke saath lie karna, doosre ko wound karna, ek bribe deliver karna, easy hai aur hamari power mein hai, lekin in cheezon ko ek certain state of character ke result mein karna na easy hai na hamari power mein. Similarly just aur unjust ko jaanna, men sochte hain, koi great wisdom require nahi karta, kyunki laws dwara deal ki gayi matters ko samajhna hard nahi hai (halaanki ye wo cheezein nahi hain jo just hain, siwaye incidentally); lekin actions kaise done ki jaayein aur distributions effect ki jaayein taaki just hon, ise jaanna health ke liye kya good hai ise jaanne se ek greater achievement hai; halaanki wahan bhi, honey, wine, hellebore, cautery, aur knife ka use aise hain ye jaanna easy hai, lekin kaise, kis se, aur kab ye apply kiye jaane chahiye health produce karne ke view se, ye jaanna ek physician hone se kam achievement nahi hai. Phir, isi very reason ke liye men sochte hain ki unjustly act karna just aadmi ka characteristic hai unjust se kam nahi, kyunki wo in mein se har unjust acts karne mein less nahi balki even more capable hoga; kyunki wo ek woman ke saath lie kar sakta hai ya ek neighbour ko wound kar sakta hai; aur brave aadmi apna shield fenk sakta hai aur is direction ya us direction mein flight tak turn kar sakta hai. Lekin coward khelna ya unjustly act karna in cheezon ko karne mein consist nahi karta, siwaye incidentally, balki inhe ek certain state of character ke result mein karne mein, jaise medicine aur healing practise karna knife apply karne ya na karne mein consist nahi karta, medicines use karne ya na karne mein, balki ise ek certain way mein karne mein.

Just acts un logo ke beech occur karte hain jo khud mein good cheezon mein participate karte hain aur inme too much ya too little ho sakta hai; kyunki kuch beings (jaise presumably gods) inme too much nahi rakh sakte, aur doosron ke liye, jo incurably bad hain, inme se sabse smallest share bhi beneficial nahi hai balki sab aise goods harmful hain, jabki doosron ke liye wo ek point tak beneficial hain; isliye justice essentially kuch human hai.

**Equity, legal justice ka ek corrective**

**10.** Hamara agla subject equity aur equitable hai, aur unka justice aur just se respective relations. Kyunki examination par wo na to absolutely same lagte hain na hi generically different; aur jabki hum kabhi equitable aur equitable aadmi ki praise karte hain (isliye hum naam ko praise ke way mein doosri virtues ke instances tak bhi apply karte hain, 'good' ki jagah, 'more equitable' se matlab lete hue ki ek cheez better hai), doosre times, jab hum reason karte hain, ye strange lagta hai agar equitable, just se ek different cheez hote hue, phir bhi praiseworthy hai; kyunki ya to just ya equitable good nahi hai, agar wo different hain; ya, agar dono good hain, wo same hain.

Ye, to, kaafi hain wo considerations jo equitable ke baare mein problem ko rise dete hain; wo sab ek sense mein correct hain aur ek doosre ke opposed nahi hain; kyunki equitable, halaanki ye ek kism ki justice se better hai, phir bhi just hai, aur ye ek different class of thing hone ke roop mein nahi hai ki ye just se better hai. Wahi cheez, to, just aur equitable hai, aur jabki dono good hain equitable superior hai.

Jo problem create karta hai wo ye hai ki equitable just hai, lekin legally just nahi balki legal justice ka ek correction. Reason ye hai ki saara law universal hai lekin kuch cheezon ke baare mein ek universal statement banaana possible nahi hai jo correct ho. Un cases mein, to, jisme universally speak karna necessary hai, lekin correctly aisa karna possible nahi hai, law usual case leti hai, halaanki ye error ki possibility se ignorant nahi hai. Aur ye none the less correct hai; kyunki error na to law mein hai na legislator mein, balki cheez ki nature mein, kyunki practical affairs ka matter shuru se hi is kism ka hai. Jab law universally baat karti hai, to, aur usme ek case arise hota hai jo universal statement se covered nahi hai, tab ye right hai, jahan legislator humein fail karta hai aur over-simplicity se err kiya hai, omission ko correct karna — wo kehna jo legislator khud kehta agar wo present hota, aur apne law mein daalta agar use pata hota. Isi wajah se equitable just hai, aur ek kism ki justice se better — absolute justice se better nahi, balki us error se better jo statement ki absoluteness se arise hoti hai. Aur yahi equitable ki nature hai, law ka ek correction jahan ye apni universality ki wajah se defective hai. Fact mein yahi reason hai ki sab cheezein law se determine nahi ki jaati hain, namely, ki kuch cheezon ke baare mein law lay down karna impossible hai, isliye ek decree ki zaroorat hai. Kyunki jab cheez indefinite hai rule bhi indefinite hai, jaise leaden rule jo Lesbian moulding banaane mein use hota hai; rule khud ko stone ki shape ke adapt karta hai aur rigid nahi hai, aur isi tarah decree bhi facts ke adapted hai.

Ye plain hai, to, ki equitable kya hai, aur ki ye just hai aur ek kism ki justice se better hai. Isse ye bhi evident hai ki equitable aadmi kaun hai; wo aadmi jo aise acts choose aur karta hai, aur bad sense mein apne rights ke liye stickler nahi hai balki apni share se kam lene ki tendency rakhta hai halaanki uske paas law hai apne side par, equitable hai, aur ye state of character equity hai, jo ek kism ki justice hai aur ek different state of character nahi.

**Kya koi insaan khud ke saath unjustly treat kar sakta hai?**

**11.** Kya ek aadmi khud ko unjustly treat kar sakta hai ya nahi, ye jo kaha gaya hai usse evident hai. Kyunki (a) just acts ki ek class wo hai jo kisi bhi virtue ke saath accord karti hai aur law dwara prescribed hai; jaise law expressly suicide permit nahi karti, aur jo ye expressly permit nahi karti wo forbid karti hai. Phir, jab ek aadmi law ke violation mein doosre ko harm karta hai (retaliation mein alawa) voluntarily, wo unjustly act karta hai, aur ek voluntary agent wo hai jo dono person ko jaanta hai jise wo apni action se affect kar raha hai aur instrument jo wo use kar raha hai; aur jo anger se voluntarily khud ko stab karta hai wo ye life ke right rule ke contrary karta hai, aur ye law nahi allow karti; isliye wo unjustly act kar raha hai. Lekin kiske prati? Surely state ke prati, khud ke prati nahi. Kyunki wo voluntarily suffer karta hai, lekin koi bhi voluntarily unjustly treat nahi kiya jaata. Yahi bhi reason hai ki state punish karta hai; civil rights ka ek certain loss us aadmi ko attach hota hai jo khud ko destroy karta hai, is ground par ki wo state ko unjustly treat kar raha hai.

Further, (b) 'acting unjustly' ke us sense mein jisme jo aadmi 'unjustly act' karta hai wo sirf unjust hai aur poori tarah bad nahi, khud ko unjustly treat karna possible nahi hai (ye pehle sense se different hai; term ka unjust aadmi ek sense mein ek particularized way mein wicked hai jaise coward hai, wo poori tarah wicked hone ke sense mein nahi, isliye uska 'unjust act' general mein wickedness manifest nahi karta). Kyunki (i) isse ye imply hota ki same cheez ek hi same time par same cheez se subtract aur add ki gayi hai; lekin ye impossible hai — just aur unjust hamesha ek se zyada person involve karte hain. Further, (ii) unjust action voluntary hai aur choice se ki jaati hai, aur initiative leti hai (kyunki jo aadmi suffer karne ki wajah se return mein wahi karta hai use unjustly act karta nahi maana jaata); lekin agar ek aadmi khud ko harm karta hai wo same time par same cheezein suffer aur karta hai. Further, (iii) agar ek aadmi khud ko unjustly treat kar sakta, wo voluntarily unjustly treat kiya ja sakta. Besides, (iv) koi bhi bina particular injustice ke acts commit kiye unjustly act nahi karta; lekin koi bhi apni khud ki wife ke saath adultery ya apne khud ke house par housebreaking ya apni khud ki property par theft commit nahi kar sakta.

General mein, sawaal 'Kya ek aadmi khud ko unjustly treat kar sakta hai?' solve bhi hota hai wahi distinction se jo humne sawaal 'Kya ek aadmi voluntarily unjustly treat kiya ja sakta hai?' par apply kiya.

(Ye bhi evident hai ki dono bad hain, unjustly treat kiya jaana aur unjustly act karna; kyunki ek ka matlab hai less rakhna aur doosre ka more rakhna intermediate amount se, jo yahan wahi part play karta hai jo medical art mein healthy karta hai, aur bodily training ki art mein good condition karti hai. Lekin phir bhi unjustly act karna worse hai, kyunki isme vice involve hai aur ye blameworthy hai — vice involve karta hai jo ya to complete aur unqualified kism ka hai ya almost aisa hai (humein doosra alternative admit karna chahiye, kyunki sab voluntary unjust action state of character ke roop mein injustice imply nahi karta), jabki unjustly treat kiya jaana khud mein vice aur injustice involve nahi karta. Khud mein, to, unjustly treat kiya jaana kam bad hai, lekin isse rokne ke liye kuch nahi hai ki ye incidentally ek greater evil ho. Lekin theory isse koi parwaah nahi karti; ye pleurisy ko ek stumble se zyada serious mischief kehta hai; phir bhi doosra incidentally zyada serious ban sakta hai, agar isse hone wala fall aapko enemy dwara prisoner banaya jaana ya death diya jaana leads karta hai.)

Metaphorically aur ek certain resemblance ki wajah se ek justice hai, na ki ek aadmi aur khud ke beech, balki uske certain parts ke beech; phir bhi justice ki har kism nahi balki wo jo master aur servant ki hai ya husband aur wife ki. Kyunki ye wo ratios hain jinme soul ka wo part jiske paas rational principle hai wo irrational part se stand karta hai; aur inhi parts ke view se log ye bhi sochte hain ki ek aadmi khud ke prati unjust ho sakta hai, namely, kyunki ye parts apni respective desires ke contrary kuch suffer karne ke liable hain; isliye inke beech ek mutual justice maani jaati hai jaise ruler aur ruled ke beech.

Ise humara justice aur baaki, yani baaki moral, virtues ka account maan lete hain.

---

# BOOK VI · INTELLECTUAL VIRTUE 

## INTRODUCTION

**Intellectual virtue study karne ke reasons: intellect contemplative aur calculative mein divided hai**

**1.** Kyunki humne previously kaha hai ki insaan ko wo choose karna chahiye jo intermediate hai, na excess na defect, aur ki intermediate reason se determine hota hai, chaliye is baat ko discuss karein. Sab states of character mein jo humne mention ki hain, jaise doosre sab matters mein bhi, ek mark hai jiski taraf wo aadmi dekhta hai jiske paas reason hai, aur us anusaar apni activity ko heighten ya relax karta hai, aur ek standard hai jo mean states ko determine karta hai jinhe hum kehte hain excess aur defect ke beech intermediate hain, correct reason ke according hote hue. Lekin aisi statement, true hote hue bhi, by no means clear hai; kyunki na sirf yahan balki doosri sab pursuits mein jo knowledge ke objects hain ye indeed true kehna hai ki humein na to bahut zyada na bahut kam exert karna chahiye ya apne efforts relax karne chahiye, balki ek intermediate extent tak aur jaise correct reason dictate kare; lekin agar ek aadmi ke paas sirf ye knowledge ho wo none the wiser hoga — jaise humein ye nahi pata hoga kis kism ki medicines apni body par apply karni hain agar koi kahe 'wo sab jo medical art prescribe karti hai, aur jo us practice se agree karti hain jise ek aisa aadmi possess karta hai jo art rakhta hai'. Isliye ye zaroori hai soul ke states ke respect mein bhi, na sirf ki ye true statement banayi jaani chahiye, balki ye bhi determine kiya jaana chahiye ki correct reason kya hai aur standard kya hai jo ise fix karta hai.

Humne soul ke virtues ko divide kiya aur kaha ki kuch moral virtues hain aur doosre intellect ke virtues. Ab humne moral virtues ko detail mein discuss kar diya hai; baaki ke respect mein chaliye apna view is tarah express karein, soul ke baare mein kuch remarks se shuru karte hue. Humne pehle kaha ki soul ke do parts hain — wo jo ek rational principle grasp karta hai, aur non-rational; chaliye ab is part ke andar ek similar distinction draw karein jo rational principle grasp karta hai. Aur assume kiya jaaye ki do parts hain jo ek rational principle grasp karte hain — ek jisse hum un cheezon ko contemplate karte hain jinke originative causes invariable hain, aur ek jisse hum variable cheezon ko contemplate karte hain; kyunki jahan objects kind mein differ karte hain wahan soul ka part jo in dono mein se har ek ke corresponding hai wo bhi kind mein different hai, kyunki ye ek certain likeness aur kinship se hai apne objects ke saath jo unhe apni knowledge deti hai jo unke paas hai. Chaliye in mein se ek part ko scientific kaha jaaye aur doosre ko calculative; kyunki deliberate karna aur calculate karna same cheez hai, lekin koi bhi invariable ke baare mein deliberate nahi karta. Isliye calculative us faculty ka ek part hai jo ek rational principle grasp karta hai. Humein, to, seekhna chahiye in do parts mein se har ek ka best state kya hai; kyunki yahi har ek ki virtue hai.

**Pehle ka object truth hai, doosre ka truth jo right desire ke corresponding hai**

**2.** Kisi cheez ki virtue uske proper work ke relative hai. Ab soul mein teen cheezein hain jo action aur truth ko control karti hain — perception, reason, desire. Inme se perception koi action originate nahi karti; ye is fact se plain hai ki lower animals mein perception hai lekin action mein koi share nahi. Jo affirmation aur negation thinking mein hain, wahi pursuit aur avoidance desire mein hain; isliye kyunki moral virtue choice se concerned ek state of character hai, aur choice deliberate desire hai, isliye reasoning true honi chahiye aur desire right, agar choice good honi hai, aur doosre ko wahi pursue karna chahiye jo pehla assert karta hai. Ab is kism ka intellect aur truth practical hai; contemplative intellect ka, jo practical na productive hai, good aur bad state respectively truth aur falsity hain (kyunki yahi har intellectual cheez ka work hai); jabki us part ka jo practical aur intellectual hai good state right desire ke agreement mein truth hai.

Action ka origin — iska efficient, na ki final cause — choice hai, aur choice ka desire aur reasoning ek end ke view se hai. Isi wajah se choice na to reason aur intellect ke bina exist kar sakti hai na hi ek moral state ke bina; kyunki good action aur uska opposite intellect aur character ke combination ke bina exist nahi kar sakte. Intellect khud, phir bhi, kuch bhi move nahi karta, balki sirf wo intellect jo ek end ko aim karta hai aur practical hai; kyunki ye productive intellect ko bhi rule karta hai, kyunki har koi jo banata hai wo ek end ke liye banata hai, aur jo banaya jaata hai wo unqualified sense mein ek end nahi hai (balki sirf ek particular relation mein ek end, aur ek particular operation ka end) — sirf wo jo kiya jaata hai wahi hai; kyunki good action ek end hai, aur desire ise aim karti hai. Isi wajah se choice ya to desiderative reason hai ya ratiocinative desire, aur action ka aisa origin hi insaan hai. (Ye note kiya jaana chahiye ki jo past hai wo kabhi choice ka object nahi hai, jaise koi bhi Troy ko sack karne ka choice nahi karta; kyunki koi bhi past ke baare mein deliberate nahi karta, balki future ke baare mein aur jo otherwise hone ke capable hai, jabki jo past hai wo na hone ka capable nahi hai; isliye Agathon right hai jab wo kehta hai: 'Kyunki yehi ek cheez hai jo even god ke liye bhi lacking hai, jo cheezein ek baar ho chuki hain unhe undone banana.') Dono intellectual parts ka work, to, truth hai. Isliye wo states jo sabse strictly wo hain jinke respect mein in mein se har part truth tak pahunchega dono parts ke virtues hain.

## THE CHIEF INTELLECTUAL VIRTUES

**Scientific knowledge — necessary aur eternal ka demonstrative knowledge**

**3.** Chaliye shuru se shuru karein, aur in states ko ek baar phir discuss karein. Assume kiya jaaye ki wo states jinke virtue se soul affirmation ya denial ke way se truth possess karti hai number mein paanch hain, yani, art, scientific knowledge, practical wisdom, philosophic wisdom, intuitive reason; hum judgement aur opinion ko include nahi karte kyunki inme hum mistaken ho sakte hain.

Ab scientific knowledge kya hai, agar humein exactly baat karni hai aur mere similarities follow nahi karni, ye plain hai jo follow karta hai usse. Hum sab suppose karte hain ki jo hum jaante hain wo otherwise hone ke capable bhi nahi hai; un cheezon ka jo otherwise hone ke capable hain humein pata nahi hai, jab wo hamari observation ke bahar chali jaati hain, ki wo exist karti hain ya nahi. Isliye scientific knowledge ka object necessity ka hai. Isliye ye eternal hai; kyunki cheezein jo unqualified sense mein necessity ki hain wo sab eternal hain; aur cheezein jo eternal hain wo ungenerated aur imperishable hain. Phir, har science taught hone ke capable maani jaati hai, aur iska object learnt hone ke. Aur sab teaching us se shuru hoti hai jo already known hai, jaisa hum Analytics mein bhi maintain karte hain; kyunki ye kabhi induction se aur kabhi deduction se proceed karti hai. Ab induction wo starting-point hai jise universal ki knowledge bhi presuppose karti hai, jabki deduction universals se proceed karti hai. Isliye starting-points hain jinse deduction proceed karti hai, jo deduction se reach nahi hote; isliye ye induction se hi hai ki wo acquire kiye jaate hain. Scientific knowledge, to, demonstrate karne ki ek capacity ki state hai, aur iske doosre limiting characteristics hain jo hum Analytics mein specify karte hain; kyunki ye tab hai jab ek aadmi ek certain way mein believe karta hai aur starting-points use known hain ki uske paas scientific knowledge hai, kyunki agar wo use conclusion se better known nahi hain, uski knowledge sirf incidentally hogi.

Ise, to, humara scientific knowledge ka account maan lein.

**Art — cheezein banane ka knowledge**

**4.** Variable mein dono things made aur things done shaamil hain; making aur acting different hain (unki nature ke liye hum apne school ke bahar ki discussions ko bhi reliable treat karte hain); isliye act karne ki capacity ki reasoned state make karne ki capacity ki reasoned state se different hai. Isi wajah se wo ek doosre mein included bhi nahi hain; kyunki na to acting making hai na hi making acting hai. Ab kyunki architecture ek art hai aur essentially make karne ki capacity ki ek reasoned state hai, aur na koi bhi art hai jo aisi state na ho na hi koi aisi state hai jo art na ho, art make karne ki capacity ki ek state ke identical hai, true reasoning involve karte hue. Sab art coming into being se concerned hai, yani kuch aisa contrive aur consider karne se jo being ya not being ke capable hai, aur jiska origin maker mein hai aur cheez mein nahi jo banayi gayi hai; kyunki art na to un cheezon se concerned hai jo hain, ya necessity se coming into being mein hain, na un cheezon se jo nature ke according aisa karti hain (kyunki inka origin khud unme hai). Making aur acting different hone ke naate, art making ka matter hona chahiye, acting ka nahi. Aur ek sense mein chance aur art same objects se concerned hain; jaise Agathon kehta hai, 'Art chance ko pyaar karti hai aur chance art ko pyaar karta hai.' Art, to, jaisa kaha gaya hai, ek state hai jo making se concerned hai, true reasoning involve karte hue, aur art ki lack iske contrary ek state hai jo making se concerned hai, false course of reasoning involve karte hue; dono variable se concerned hain.

**Practical wisdom — human life ke ends secure karne ka knowledge**

**5.** Practical wisdom ke respect mein hum truth tak pahunchenge un persons ko consider karke jinhe hum iska credit dete hain. Ab ye ek practical wisdom wale aadmi ka mark maana jaata hai ki wo apne liye kya good aur expedient hai iske baare mein well deliberate kar sake, kisi particular respect mein nahi, jaise kis kism ki cheezein health ya strength ki taraf conduce karti hain, balki kis kism ki cheezein general mein good life ki taraf conduce karti hain. Ye is fact se dikhta hai ki hum men ko particular respect mein practical wisdom ka credit dete hain jab unhone kisi good end ke view se well calculate kiya ho jo un mein se ek hai jo kisi bhi art ka object nahi hai. Isse follow karta hai ki general sense mein bhi wo aadmi jo deliberate karne ke capable hai practical wisdom rakhta hai. Ab koi bhi invariable cheezon ke baare mein deliberate nahi karta, ya un cheezon ke baare mein jo uske liye karna impossible hai. Isliye, kyunki scientific knowledge demonstration involve karti hai, lekin un cheezon ka koi demonstration nahi hai jinke first principles variable hain (kyunki sab aisi cheezein actually otherwise ho sakti hain), aur kyunki un cheezon ke baare mein deliberate karna impossible hai jo necessity ki hain, practical wisdom na to scientific knowledge ho sakti hai na art; science nahi kyunki jo kiya ja sakta hai wo otherwise hone ke capable hai, art nahi kyunki action aur making different kism ki cheezein hain. Reh jaane wala alternative, to, ye hai ki ye man ke liye good ya bad cheezon ke respect mein act karne ki capacity ki ek true aur reasoned state hai. Kyunki jabki making ka apne alawa ek doosra end hai, action nahi kar sakti; kyunki good action khud iska end hai. Isi reason ke liye hum sochte hain Pericles aur unke jaise log practical wisdom rakhte hain, namely, kyunki wo dekh sakte hain khud ke liye kya good hai aur men ke liye general mein kya good hai; hum consider karte hain ki ye wo log kar sakte hain jo households ya states manage karne mein good hain. (Isi wajah se hum temperance (sōphrosunē) ko is naam se pukarte hain; hum imply karte hain ki ye kisi ki practical wisdom (sōzousa ten phronēsin) ko preserve karti hai. Ab jo ye preserve karta hai wo hai ek judgement is kism ki jo humne describe ki hai. Kyunki ye koi bhi aur har judgement nahi hai jise pleasant aur painful objects destroy aur pervert karte hain, jaise judgement ki triangle ke angles do right angles ke equal hain ya nahi, balki sirf judgements ki kya karna chahiye. Kyunki jo cheezein ki jaati hain unke originating causes us end mein consist karte hain jise wo aim karti hain; lekin jo aadmi pleasure ya pain se ruined ho chuka hai forthwith aisi kisi bhi originating cause ko dekhne mein fail karta hai — ye dekhne mein ki isi ki khaatir ya iski wajah se usse choose aur karna chahiye jo bhi wo choose karta hai aur karta hai; kyunki vice action ki originating cause ka destructive hai.)

Practical wisdom, to, human goods ke respect mein act karne ki capacity ki ek reasoned aur true state honi chahiye. Lekin further, jabki art mein excellence jaisi koi cheez hai, practical wisdom mein excellence jaisi koi cheez nahi hai; aur art mein jo willingly errs karta hai wo preferable hai, lekin practical wisdom mein, jaise virtues mein, wo reverse hai. Plainly, to, practical wisdom ek virtue hai aur art nahi. Soul ke do parts hone ke naate jo ek course of reasoning follow kar sakte hain, ye do mein se ek ki virtue honi chahiye, yani us part ki jo opinions form karta hai; kyunki opinion variable ke baare mein hai aur isi tarah practical wisdom bhi. Lekin phir bhi ye sirf ek reasoned state nahi hai; ye is fact se dikhta hai ki us kism ki ek state bhool sakti hai lekin practical wisdom nahi.

**Intuitive reason — un principles ka knowledge jinse science proceed karti hai**

**6.** Scientific knowledge un cheezon ke baare mein judgement hai jo universal aur necessary hain; aur demonstration ke conclusions, aur saari scientific knowledge, first principles se follow karti hain (kyunki scientific knowledge demonstration involve karti hai). Ye aisa hone ke naate, first principle jisse scientifically known cheez follow karti hai wo scientific knowledge, art, ya practical wisdom ka object nahi ho sakta; kyunki jo scientifically known ho sakta hai wo demonstrate kiya ja sakta hai, aur art aur practical wisdom un cheezon se deal karte hain jo variable hain. Na hi ye first principles philosophic wisdom ke objects hain, kyunki philosopher ka mark kuch cheezon ke baare mein demonstration rakhna hai. Agar, to, mind ke states jinse humein truth milti hai aur invariable ya even variable cheezon ke baare mein hum kabhi deceived nahi hote wo scientific knowledge, practical wisdom, philosophic wisdom, aur intuitive reason hain, aur ye teen mein se koi bhi (yani practical wisdom, scientific knowledge, ya philosophic wisdom) nahi ho sakta, reh jaane wala alternative ye hai ki ye intuitive reason hai jo first principles ko grasp karta hai.

**Philosophic wisdom — intuitive reason aur science ka union**

**7.** Wisdom (1) arts mein hum unke sabse finished exponents ko ascribe karte hain, jaise Phidias ko ek sculptor ke roop mein aur Polyclitus ko ek portrait-statues ke maker ke roop mein, aur yahan hamara matlab wisdom se kuch aur nahi balki art mein excellence hi hai; lekin (2) hum sochte hain ki kuch log general mein wise hain, kisi particular field mein ya kisi doosre limited respect mein nahi, jaise Homer Margites mein kehta hai, 'Use gods ne na digger banaya na hi ek ploughman, na kisi aur cheez mein wise.' Isliye wisdom plainly knowledge ke forms mein sabse finished honi chahiye. Isse follow karta hai ki wise aadmi ko na sirf ye jaanna chahiye ki first principles se kya follow karta hai, balki use first principles ke baare mein bhi truth possess karni chahiye. Isliye wisdom intuitive reason honi chahiye scientific knowledge ke saath combined — highest objects ki scientific knowledge jise iska proper completion mil chuka hai.

Highest objects ki, hum kehte hain; kyunki ye strange hoga sochna ki politics ki art, ya practical wisdom, best knowledge hai, kyunki man duniya mein best cheez nahi hai. Ab agar healthy ya good jo men ke liye hai aur fishes ke liye hai wo different hai, lekin jo white ya straight hai wo hamesha same hai, koi bhi kahega ki jo wise hai wo same hai lekin jo practically wise hai wo different hai; kyunki wo cheez jo khud se concerned various matters ko well consider karti hai wahi practical wisdom ko ascribe ki jaati hai, aur isi ko koi aise matters entrust karega. Isi wajah se hum kehte hain ki lower animals mein se bhi kuch practical wisdom rakhte hain, namely, wo jo apni khud ki life ke respect mein foresight ki ek power rakhte paaye jaate hain. Ye bhi evident hai ki philosophic wisdom aur politics ki art same nahi ho sakte; kyunki agar ek aadmi ke khud ke interests se concerned mind ki state ko philosophic wisdom kaha jaaye, to bahut si philosophic wisdoms hongi; koi ek bhi nahi hogi jo sab animals ke good se concerned ho (na hi koi ek medicine ki art hai sab existing things ke liye), balki har species ke good ke baare mein ek different philosophic wisdom.

Lekin agar argument ye ho ki man animals mein best hai, isse koi farak nahi padta; kyunki doosri cheezein bhi hain jo apni nature mein even man se zyada divine hain, jaise, sabse conspicuously, wo bodies jinse heavens framed hain. Jo kaha gaya hai usse ye plain hai, to, ki philosophic wisdom scientific knowledge hai, intuitive reason ke saath combined, un cheezon ki jo nature se highest hain. Isi wajah se hum kehte hain Anaxagoras, Thales, aur unke jaise log philosophic lekin practical wisdom nahi rakhte, jab hum unhe apne khud ke advantage ke baare mein ignorant dekhte hain, aur isi wajah se hum kehte hain ki wo aisi cheezein jaante hain jo remarkable, admirable, difficult, aur divine hain, lekin useless; namely, kyunki wo human goods nahi seek karte.

Practical wisdom doosri taraf human matters se aur un cheezon se concerned hai jinke baare mein deliberate karna possible hai; kyunki hum kehte hain ye sab se upar practical wisdom wale aadmi ka work hai, well deliberate karna, lekin koi bhi invariable cheezon ke baare mein deliberate nahi karta, ya un cheezon ke baare mein jinka koi end nahi hai jo action se brought about ki ja sakne wali ek good hai. Wo aadmi jo bina qualification ke deliberate karne mein good hai wo hai jo calculation ke according man ke liye action se attainable cheezon mein best ko aim karne ke capable hai. Na hi practical wisdom sirf universals se concerned hai — ye particulars ko bhi recognize karni chahiye; kyunki ye practical hai, aur practice particulars se concerned hai. Isi wajah se kuch log jo nahi jaante, aur khaas kar wo jinke paas experience hai, doosron se zyada practical hain jo jaante hain; kyunki agar ek aadmi ko pata ho ki light meats digestible aur wholesome hain, lekin ye na pata ho ki kis kism ka meat light hai, wo health produce nahi karega, lekin wo aadmi jise pata hai ki chicken wholesome hai wo health produce karne ki zyada likelihood rakhta hai.

Ab practical wisdom action se concerned hai; isliye kisi ko dono forms rakhne chahiye, ya baad wale ko pehle se zyada preference mein. Lekin yahan bhi, ek controlling kind hona chahiye.

**Practical wisdom aur political science ke beech relations**

**8.** Political wisdom aur practical wisdom mind ki same state hain, lekin unka essence same nahi hai. City se concerned wisdom mein se, practical wisdom jo ek controlling part play karti hai wo legislative wisdom hai, jabki wo jo iske universal ke particulars ki tarah related hai wo general naam 'political wisdom' se jaana jaata hai; ise action aur deliberation se lena-dena hai, kyunki ek decree ek cheez hai jo ek individual act ki form mein carry out ki jaani hai. Isi wajah se is art ke exponents ko akele 'politics mein part lete hain' kaha jaata hai; kyunki ye akele 'cheezein karte hain' jaise manual labourers 'cheezein karte hain'.

Practical wisdom bhi especially us form se identify ki jaati hai jo ek aadmi khud se concerned hai — individual se; aur ise general naam 'practical wisdom' se jaana jaata hai; doosri kisms mein se ek ko household management kaha jaata hai, doosri legislation, teesri politics, aur teesri mein se ek part deliberative kaha jaata hai aur doosra judicial. Ab khud ke liye kya good hai jaanna ek kism ki knowledge hogi, lekin ye doosri kisms se bahut different hai; aur jo aadmi apne khud ke interests ko jaanta hai aur unse concerned rehta hai use practical wisdom rakhne wala maana jaata hai, jabki politicians ko busybodies maana jaata hai; isi wajah se Euripides ke words hain: 'Lekin main wise kaise ho sakta tha, jo ease se, army ke multitude mein numbered, ek equal share paa sakta tha?... Un logo ke liye jo too high aim karte hain aur bahut zyada karte hain...' Jo aise sochte hain wo apna khud ka good seek karte hain, aur consider karte hain ki koi bhi aisa karna chahiye. Is opinion se, to, ye view aayi hai ki aise men practical wisdom rakhte hain; phir bhi shayad kisi ka khud ka good household management ke bina, ya government ke kisi form ke bina, exist nahi kar sakta. Further, koi apne khud ke affairs ko kaise order kare ye clear nahi hai aur inquiry ki zaroorat hai.

Jo kaha gaya hai use is fact se confirm hota hai ki jabki young men geometricians aur mathematicians ban jaate hain aur is kism ke matters mein wise, ek young man ka practical wisdom wala paaya jaana nahi maana jaata. Cause ye hai ki aisi wisdom sirf universals se nahi balki particulars se bhi concerned hai, jo experience se familiar ban jaate hain, lekin ek young man ke paas experience nahi hai, kyunki experience time ki length deti hai; indeed koi ye sawaal bhi pooch sakta hai, kyun ek boy mathematician ban sakta hai, lekin philosopher ya physicist nahi. Kya isliye kyunki mathematics ke objects abstraction se exist karte hain, jabki doosre subjects ke first principles experience se aate hain, aur kyunki young men ko baad wale ke baare mein koi conviction nahi hai balki wo sirf proper language use karte hain, jabki mathematical objects ka essence unke liye kaafi plain hai?

Further, deliberation mein error ya to universal ke baare mein ho sakta hai ya particular ke baare mein; hum fail ho sakte hain ye jaanne mein ki sab water jo heavy weigh karta hai bad hai, ya ki ye particular water heavy weigh karta hai.

Ki practical wisdom scientific knowledge nahi hai ye evident hai; kyunki ye, jaisa kaha gaya hai, ultimate particular fact se concerned hai, kyunki jo kiya jaana hai wo is nature ka hai. Ye, to, intuitive reason ke opposed hai; kyunki intuitive reason limiting premisses ka hai, jinke liye koi reason nahi diya ja sakta, jabki practical wisdom ultimate particular se concerned hai, jo scientific knowledge ka nahi balki perception ka object hai — kisi ek sense ki peculiar qualities ki perception nahi balki ek perception jo us se akin hai jisse hum perceive karte hain ki jo particular figure hamare saamne hai wo ek triangle hai; kyunki us direction mein bhi ek limit hogi. Lekin ye practical wisdom se zyada perception hai, halaanki ye har sense ki peculiar qualities ki perception se ek doosri kism ki perception hai.

## MINOR INTELLECTUAL VIRTUES CONCERNED WITH CONDUCT

**Deliberation mein goodness, ye practical wisdom se kaise related hai**

**9.** Inquiry aur deliberation ke beech ek difference hai; kyunki deliberation ek particular kism ki inquiry hai. Humein deliberation mein excellence ki nature bhi grasp karni chahiye — chahe ye scientific knowledge ka ek form hai, ya opinion, ya conjecture mein skill, ya kisi aur kism ki cheez. Scientific knowledge ye nahi hai; kyunki men un cheezon ke baare mein inquire nahi karte jinke baare mein unhe pata hai, lekin good deliberation deliberation ka ek kism hai, aur jo deliberate karta hai wo inquire aur calculate karta hai. Na ye conjecture mein skill hai; kyunki isme na to koi reasoning involve hoti hai aur ye kuch aisa hai jo apne operation mein quick hai, jabki men lambe time tak deliberate karte hain, aur wo kehte hain ki apni deliberation ke conclusions ko quickly carry out karna chahiye, lekin deliberate slowly karna chahiye. Phir, mind ki readiness excellence in deliberation se different hai; ye conjecture mein ek kism ki skill hai. Na hi excellence in deliberation kisi bhi kism ki opinion hai. Lekin kyunki jo aadmi badly deliberate karta hai wo mistake karta hai, jabki jo well deliberate karta hai wo correctly karta hai, excellence in deliberation clearly correctness ka ek kism hai, lekin na knowledge ka na opinion ka; kyunki knowledge ki koi correctness nahi hai (kyunki knowledge ki koi error nahi hai), aur opinion ki correctness truth hai; aur usi waqt jo bhi opinion ka object hai wo already determined hai. Lekin phir excellence in deliberation reasoning involve karti hai. Reh jaane wala alternative, to, ye hai ki ye thinking ki correctness hai; kyunki ye abhi assertion nahi hai, kyunki, jabki even opinion inquiry nahi hai balki assertion ke stage tak pahunch chuki hai, jo aadmi deliberate kar raha hai, chahe wo well kare ya ill, wo kuch search kar raha hai aur calculate kar raha hai.

Lekin excellence in deliberation deliberation ki ek certain correctness hai; isliye humein pehle inquire karna chahiye ki deliberation kya hai aur ye kis baare mein hai. Aur, correctness ki ek se zyada kism hone ke naate, plainly excellence in deliberation koi bhi aur har kism nahi hai; kyunki (1) incontinent aadmi aur bad aadmi, agar wo clever hai, apni calculation ke result mein wahi paayega jo usne khud ke saamne set kiya hai, isliye usne correctly deliberate kiya hoga, lekin usne khud ke liye ek great evil paaya hoga. Ab well deliberate kiya hona ek good cheez maani jaati hai; kyunki yahi wo kism ki deliberation ki correctness hai jo excellence in deliberation hai, namely, wo jo achieve karne ki tendency rakhti hai jo good hai. Lekin (2) ye possible hai even good ko ek false syllogism se attain karna, aur jo karna chahiye use attain karna lekin right means se nahi, middle term false hote hue; isliye ye bhi excellence in deliberation nahi hai — ye state jiske virtue se koi wo attain karta hai jo usse karna chahiye lekin right means se nahi. Phir (3) ye possible hai isse long deliberation se attain karna jabki doosra aadmi ise quickly attain karta hai. Isliye pehle case mein humein abhi bhi excellence in deliberation nahi mili, jo expedient ke respect mein rightness hai — end, manner, aur time dono ke respect mein rightness. (4) Further, well deliberate kiya hona possible hai ya to unqualified sense mein ya kisi particular end ke reference mein. Unqualified sense mein excellence in deliberation, to, wahi hai jo unqualified sense mein end ke reference mein succeed karti hai, aur ek particular sense mein excellence in deliberation wahi hai jo ek particular end ke relative succeed karti hai. Agar, to, ye practical wisdom wale men ka characteristic hai ki unhone well deliberate kiya ho, excellence in deliberation us cheez ke respect mein correctness hogi jo us end ki taraf conduce karti hai jise practical wisdom truly apprehend karti hai.

**Understanding — wo critical quality jo practical wisdom ki imperative quality ke corresponding hai**

**10.** Understanding, bhi, aur understanding ki goodness, jiske virtue se men ko understanding wale ya good understanding wale kaha jaata hai, na to entirely opinion ya scientific knowledge ke same hain (kyunki us rate par sab men understanding wale hote), na hi ye particular sciences mein se ek hai, jaise medicine, health se connected cheezon ki science, ya geometry, spatial magnitudes ki science. Kyunki understanding na to un cheezon ke baare mein hai jo hamesha hain aur unchangeable hain, na hi coming into being wali cheezon mein se kisi ke bhi baare mein, balki un cheezon ke baare mein jo questioning aur deliberation ke subjects ban sakti hain. Isliye ye practical wisdom ke same objects ke baare mein hai; lekin understanding aur practical wisdom same nahi hain. Kyunki practical wisdom commands issue karti hai, kyunki iska end wo hai jo karna chahiye ya nahi karna chahiye; lekin understanding sirf judge karta hai. (Understanding understanding ki goodness ke identical hai, understanding wale men good understanding wale men ke.) Ab understanding na to practical wisdom ka having hai na acquiring; lekin jaise learning ko understanding kaha jaata hai jab iska matlab knowledge ki faculty ka exercise hai, waise hi 'understanding' opinion ki faculty ke exercise par applicable hai us purpose ke liye ki koi doosra kya kehta hai un matters ke baare mein jinse practical wisdom concerned hai use judge kiya jaa sake — aur soundly judge kiya jaa sake; kyunki 'well' aur 'soundly' same cheez hain. Aur isi se aaya hai 'understanding' naam ka use jiske virtue se men ko 'good understanding wale' kaha jaata hai, namely, word ke application se scientific truth ke grasping mein; kyunki hum aksar aise grasping ko understanding kehte hain.

**Judgement — equitable ka right discrimination: morals mein intuition ka place**

**11.** Jise judgement kaha jaata hai, jiske virtue se men ko 'sympathetic judges' kaha jaata hai aur 'judgement rakhne wale', wo equitable ka right discrimination hai. Ye is fact se dikhta hai ki hum kehte hain equitable aadmi sab logo se upar ek sympathetic judgement wala aadmi hai, aur equity ko certain facts ke baare mein sympathetic judgement se identify karte hain. Aur sympathetic judgement wo judgement hai jo equitable kya hai use discriminate karti hai aur correctly karti hai; aur correct judgement wo hai jo true ko judge karta hai.

Ab humne consider ki gayi sab states converge karti hain, jaisa expect kiya ja sakta hai, same point tak; kyunki jab hum judgement aur understanding aur practical wisdom aur intuitive reason ki baat karte hain hum same logo ko judgement rakhne aur reason ke years tak pahunch chuke hone aur practical wisdom aur understanding rakhne ka credit dete hain. Kyunki ye sab faculties ultimates se deal karti hain, yani particulars se; aur understanding wala aur good ya sympathetic judgement wala hona un cheezon ke baare mein judge karne ke capable hone mein consist karta hai jinse practical wisdom concerned hai; kyunki jo equitable hai wo sab good men ka doosron ke saath apne dealings mein common concern hai. Ab jo sab cheezein ki jaani hain wo particulars ya ultimates mein include hoti hain; kyunki na sirf practical wisdom wale aadmi ko particular facts jaanne chahiye, balki understanding aur judgement bhi karni hain cheezon se concerned hain, aur ye ultimates hain. Aur intuitive reason dono directions mein ultimates se concerned hai; kyunki first terms aur last dono intuitive reason ke objects hain aur ek rational account ke nahi, aur wo intuitive reason jo demonstrations dwara presuppose kiya jaata hai unchangeable aur first terms grasp karta hai, jabki practical reasonings mein involved intuitive reason last aur variable fact grasp karta hai, yani minor premiss. Kyunki ye variable facts end ki apprehension ke liye starting-points hain, kyunki universals particulars se reach kiye jaate hain; inka, isliye, humein perception hona chahiye, aur ye perception intuitive reason hai.

Isi wajah se ye states natural endowments maani jaati hain — isi wajah se, jabki koi bhi nature se philosopher nahi maana jaata, log nature se judgement, understanding, aur intuitive reason rakhte maane jaate hain. Ye is fact se dikhta hai ki hum sochte hain hamari powers hamari life ke time ke corresponding hain, aur ki ek particular age apne saath intuitive reason aur judgement laati hai; ye imply karta hai ki nature cause hai. [Isliye intuitive reason dono beginning aur end hai; kyunki demonstrations inhi se aur inke baare mein hain.] Isliye humein experienced aur older logo ke ya practical wisdom wale logo ke undemonstrated sayings aur opinions par bhi attend karna chahiye demonstrations se kam nahi; kyunki experience ne unhe ek eye di hai isliye wo aright dekhte hain.

Humne state kar diya hai, to, practical aur philosophic wisdom kya hain, aur in mein se har ek kis se concerned hai, aur humne kaha hai ki har ek soul ke ek different part ki virtue hai.

## RELATION OF PHILOSOPHIC TO PRACTICAL WISDOM

**Philosophic aur practical wisdom ka use kya hai? Puzzles, aur kuch solutions**

**12.** Difficulties raise ki ja sakti hain mind ke in qualities ki utility ke respect mein. Kyunki (1) philosophic wisdom un cheezon mein se koi bhi contemplate nahi karegi jo ek aadmi ko happy banaayengi (kyunki ye kisi bhi coming into being se concerned nahi hai), aur halaanki practical wisdom ke paas ye merit hai, kis purpose ke liye humein iski zaroorat hai? Practical wisdom mind ki wo quality hai jo just aur noble aur man ke liye good cheezon se concerned hai, lekin ye wo cheezein hain jo ek good aadmi ka karna mark hai, aur inhe jaanne se hum inhe act karne ke liye zyada able nahi ban jaate agar virtues states of character hain, jaise hum health se sound aur healthy cheezon ko jaanne se zyada able nahi ban jaate act karne ke liye, us sense mein nahi ki produce karne ke balki health ki state se issuing hone ke sense mein; kyunki humare paas medicine ya gymnastics ki art hone se hum act karne ke zyada able nahi ban jaate. Lekin (2) agar humein ye kehna hai ki ek aadmi ko practical wisdom rakhni chahiye moral truths jaanne ki khaatir nahi balki good banne ki khaatir, practical wisdom un logo ke liye koi use ki nahi hogi jo already good hain; lekin phir se ye un logo ke liye bhi koi use ki nahi hai jinke paas virtue nahi hai; kyunki isse koi farak nahi padega ki unke paas khud practical wisdom hai ya wo doosron ko obey karte hain jinke paas hai, aur ye humare liye kaafi hoga wahi karna jo hum health ke case mein karte hain; halaanki hum healthy banna chahte hain, phir bhi hum medicine ki art nahi seekhte. (3) Iske alawa, ye strange lagega agar practical wisdom, philosophic wisdom se inferior hote hue, iske upar authority mein rakhi jaaye, jaisa implied lagta hai is fact se ki jo art kuch bhi produce karti hai wo us cheez ke baare mein rule aur commands issue karti hai.

Ye, to, wo questions hain jinhe humein discuss karna chahiye; ab tak humne sirf difficulties state ki hain.

Ab pehle chaliye kahein ki khud in states ko choice ka worthy hona chahiye kyunki wo soul ke dono parts ki respectively virtues hain, even agar in mein se koi bhi kuch produce na kare. Doosri baat, wo kuch produce karte hain, na ki jaise medicine ki art health produce karti hai, balki jaise health health produce karti hai; isi tarah philosophic wisdom happiness produce karti hai; kyunki, poori virtue ka ek part hote hue, possessed hone se aur khud ko actualize karne se ye ek aadmi ko happy banaati hai. Phir, insaan ka work sirf practical wisdom ke saath saath hi moral virtue ke saath bhi achieve hota hai; kyunki virtue goal ko correct banaati hai, aur practical wisdom us tak le jaane wale ko correct banaati hai. (Soul ke chauthe part ke liye — nutritive — aisi koi virtue nahi hai; kyunki aisi koi cheez nahi hai jo iski power mein ho karna ya na karna.)

Hamare uspar practical wisdom ki wajah se noble aur just karne mein zyada able na hone ke respect mein, chaliye thoda further back se shuru karein, following principle se. Jaisa hum kehte hain ki kuch log jo just acts karte hain necessarily just nahi hain, yani wo jo laws dwara ordained acts unwillingly ya ignorance ki wajah se ya kisi doosre reason ke liye karte hain aur acts ki khud ki khaatir nahi (halaanki, be sure, wo karte hain jo unhe karna chahiye aur sab cheezein jo good aadmi ko karni chahiye), isi tarah lagta hai ki good hone ke liye kisi ko ek certain state mein hona chahiye jab wo several acts karta hai, yani choice ke result mein karna chahiye aur acts ki khud ki khaatir. Ab virtue choice ko right banaati hai, lekin un cheezon ka sawaal jo naturally kiye jaane chahiye hamari choice carry out karne ke liye virtue ki nahi balki doosri faculty ki belong karta hai. Humein in matters par apna attention devote karna chahiye aur inke baare mein ek clearer statement dena chahiye. Ek faculty hai jise cleverness kaha jaata hai; aur ye is tarah ki hai ki wo un cheezon ko kar sake jo humne apne saamne set kiye hain mark ki taraf tend karti hain, aur use hit kar sake. Ab agar mark noble hai, cleverness laudable hai, lekin agar mark bad hai, cleverness sirf smartness hai; isi wajah se hum even practical wisdom wale men ko bhi clever ya smart kehte hain. Practical wisdom ye faculty nahi hai, lekin ye is faculty ke bina exist nahi karti. Aur soul ki ye eye apni formed state virtue ki aid ke bina nahi acquire karti, jaisa kaha gaya hai aur plain hai; kyunki jo syllogisms kiye jaane wale acts se deal karte hain unme ek starting-point involve hota hai, namely, 'kyunki end, yani jo best hai, is aur is nature ka hai', jo bhi ho (argument ki khaatir jo hum chahein wo ho); aur ye good aadmi ke alawa evident nahi hai; kyunki wickedness humein pervert karti hai aur humein action ke starting-points ke baare mein deceive hone ka cause banati hai. Isliye ye evident hai ki practically wise hona bina good hue impossible hai.

**Practical wisdom ka natural virtue, moral virtue, aur correct reason se relation**

**13.** Isliye humein virtue ke baare mein bhi ek baar phir consider karna chahiye; kyunki virtue bhi similarly related hai; jaise practical wisdom cleverness se hai — same nahi, lekin uske jaisi — waise hi natural virtue strict sense ki virtue se hai. Kyunki sab men sochte hain ki har type ka character apne possessors ko kisi na kisi sense mein nature se belong karta hai; kyunki birth ke very moment se hi hum just hain ya self-control ke liye fitted ya brave ya doosri moral qualities rakhte hain; lekin phir bhi hum kuch aur seek karte hain jo strict sense mein good hai — hum aise qualities ki presence ko ek doosre tareeke se seek karte hain. Kyunki dono children aur brutes in qualities ke natural dispositions rakhte hain, lekin bina reason ke ye evidently hurtful hain. Sirf itna hum dekh sakte hain, ki, jabki koi in se astray le jaaya ja sakta hai, jaise ek strong body jo bina sight ke move karti hai badly stumble kar sakti hai apne sight ki kami ki wajah se, phir bhi, agar ek aadmi ek baar reason acquire kar leta hai, ye action mein difference banata hai; aur uski state, abhi bhi jo thi jaisi hi lagte hue, tab strict sense mein virtue hogi. Isliye, jaise humare us part mein jo opinions form karta hai do types hain, cleverness aur practical wisdom, waise hi moral part mein bhi do types hain, natural virtue aur strict sense ki virtue, aur inme se baad wali practical wisdom involve karti hai. Isi wajah se kuch log kehte hain ki sab virtues practical wisdom ke forms hain, aur isi wajah se Socrates ek respect mein right track par the jabki doosre mein wo astray gaye; ye sochne mein ki sab virtues practical wisdom ke forms the wo wrong the, lekin ye kehne mein ki wo practical wisdom imply karti hain wo right the.

Ye is fact se confirm hota hai ki abhi bhi sab men, jab wo virtue define karte hain, state of character aur uske objects ka naam lene ke baad add karte hain 'wo (state) jo correct reason ke according hai'; ab correct reason wo hai jo practical wisdom ke according hai. Sab men, to, kisi tarah divine karte lagte hain ki is kism ki state virtue hai, namely, wo jo practical wisdom ke according hai. Lekin humein thoda aur aage jaana chahiye. Kyunki ye merely wo state nahi hai jo correct reason ke according hai, balki wo state jo correct reason ki presence imply karti hai, jo virtue hai; aur practical wisdom aise matters ke baare mein correct reason hai. Socrates, to, sochte the virtues reason ke instances the (kyunki wo sochte the wo, unme se sab, scientific knowledge ke forms the), jabki hum sochte hain wo reason involve karte hain.

Ye clear hai, to, jo kaha gaya hai usse, ki practical wisdom ke bina strict sense mein good hona possible nahi hai, ya moral virtue ke bina practically wise hona. Lekin is tarah hum us dialectical argument ko bhi refute kar sakte hain jisse contend kiya ja sakta hai ki virtues ek doosre se separation mein exist karti hain; wahi aadmi, koi keh sakta hai, sab virtues ke liye nature se best equipped nahi hai, isliye usne ek acquire kar liya hoga jab usne doosra abhi acquire nahi kiya hoga. Ye natural virtues ke respect mein possible hai, lekin un logo ke respect mein nahi jinke respect mein ek aadmi ko bina qualification ke good kaha jaata hai; kyunki ek quality ki presence ke saath, practical wisdom, sab virtues di jaayengi. Aur ye plain hai ki, even agar ye practical value ka koi na hota, humein iski zaroorat hoti kyunki ye humare us part ki virtue hai jo question mein hai; ye bhi plain hai ki choice practical wisdom ke bina right nahi hogi jitni virtue ke bina nahi; kyunki ek end determine karta hai aur doosra humein un cheezon ko karne banaata hai jo end tak le jaati hain.

Lekin phir se ye philosophic wisdom ke upar supreme nahi hai, yani humare superior part ke upar, jitna medicine ki art health ke upar nahi hai; kyunki ye ise use nahi karti balki iske coming into being ke liye provide karti hai; ye isi ki khaatir orders issue karti hai, lekin isko nahi. Further, iski supremacy maintain karna aisa hoga jaise kehna ki politics ki art gods ko rule karti hai kyunki ye state ke sab affairs ke baare mein orders issue karti hai.

---

# BOOK VII · CONTINENCE AND INCONTINENCE: 

## CONTINENCE AND INCONTINENCE

**Character ki chhe varieties: treatment ka method: current opinions**

**1.** Chaliye ab ek fresh beginning karein aur point out karein ki avoid ki jaane wali moral states teen kism ki hain — vice, incontinence, brutishness. In mein se do ke contraries evident hain — ek ko hum virtue kehte hain, doosra continence; brutishness ke against oppose karna sabse fitting hoga superhuman virtue, ek heroic aur divine kism ki virtue, jaise Homer ne Priam ko Hector ke baare mein kehte hue represent kiya ki wo bahut good tha. 'Kyunki wo, mortal man ka child nahi lagta tha, balki jaise koi jo god's seed se aaya ho.' Isliye agar, jaisa wo kehte hain, virtue ke excess se men gods ban jaate hain, is kism ki honi chahiye evidently wo state jo brutish state ke against opposed hai: kyunki jaise ek brute ke paas vice ya virtue nahi hai, waise hi ek god ke paas bhi nahi hai; uski state virtue se higher hai, aur ek brute ki vice se ek different kism ki state hai.

Ab, kyunki rarely ek godlike aadmi paaya jaata hai — Spartans ke epithet ko use karte hue, jo jab kisi ki highly admire karte hain use ek 'godlike man' kehte hain — waise hi brutish type bhi men mein rarely paaya jaata hai; ye chiefly barbarians ke beech paaya jaata hai, lekin kuch brutish qualities disease ya deformity se bhi produce hoti hain; aur hum is evil naam se un logo ko bhi bulaate hain jo ordinary men se vice mein surpass karte hain. Is kism ki disposition ke baare mein, phir bhi, humein baad mein kuch mention karna chahiye, jabki humne vice ke baare mein pehle discuss kar diya hai; humein ab incontinence aur softness (ya effeminacy), aur continence aur endurance discuss karna chahiye; kyunki humein in dono ko treat karna chahiye na to virtue ya wickedness ke identical roop mein, na hi ek different genus ke roop mein. Humein, jaise doosre sab cases mein, apparent facts humare saamne rakhne chahiye aur, pehle difficulties discuss karke, aage badh kar prove karna chahiye, agar possible ho, in affections of the mind ke baare mein sabhi common opinions ki truth, ya, agar ye nahi ho paaye, to zyadatar aur sabse authoritative opinions ki; kyunki agar hum difficulties resolve bhi karein aur common opinions ko undisturbed bhi chhode, to hum case ko sufficiently prove kar chuke honge.

Ab (1) dono continence aur endurance good aur praiseworthy cheezon mein include maani jaati hain, aur dono incontinence aur softness bad aur blameworthy cheezon mein; aur same aadmi continent aur apni calculations ke result ke saath abide karne ke liye ready maana jaata hai, ya incontinent aur unhe abandon karne ke liye ready. Aur (2) incontinent aadmi, jaanta hue ki jo wo karta hai bad hai, ise passion ke result mein karta hai, jabki continent aadmi, jaanta hue ki uski appetites bad hain, apni rational principle ki wajah se unhe follow karne se refuse karta hai. (3) Temperate aadmi ko sab men continent aur endurance ke disposed kehte hain, jabki continent aadmi ko kuch maintain karte hain hamesha temperate hone ke roop mein lekin doosre nahi; aur kuch self-indulgent aadmi ko incontinent aur incontinent aadmi ko self-indulgent indiscriminately kehte hain, jabki doosre unhe distinguish karte hain. (4) Practical wisdom wala aadmi, wo kabhi kabhi kehte hain, incontinent nahi ho sakta, jabki kabhi wo kehte hain ki kuch jo practically wise aur clever hain wo incontinent hain. Phir, (5) men ko even anger, honour, aur gain ke respect mein bhi incontinent kaha jaata hai. — Ye, to, wo cheezein hain jo kahi jaati hain.

**Current opinions ki discussion**

**2.** Ab hum pooch sakte hain (1) kis kism ka right judgement hai us aadmi ka jo incontinently behave karta hai. Ki wo aise behave kare jab uske paas knowledge ho, kuch kehte hain impossible hai; kyunki ye strange hoga — jaisa Socrates sochte the — agar jab ek aadmi mein knowledge ho, kuch aur ise master kar sake aur ek slave ki tarah ghaseet sake. Kyunki Socrates is question mein view ke entirely opposed the, ye maante hue ki incontinence jaisi koi cheez nahi hai; koi bhi nahi, wo kehte the, jab judge karta hai, uske against act karta hai jo wo best judge karta hai — log aisa sirf ignorance ke reason se karte hain. Ab ye view plainly apparent facts ka contradict karta hai, aur humein poochna chahiye ki aise aadmi ko kya hota hai; agar wo ignorance ke reason se act karta hai, to uski ignorance ka manner kya hai? Kyunki ki jo aadmi incontinently behave karta hai wo, is state mein aane se pehle, ye nahi sochta ki usse aise act karna chahiye, ye evident hai. Lekin kuch log hain jo Socrates ke kuch contentions concede karte hain lekin doosron ko nahi; ki knowledge se stronger kuch nahi hai ye wo admit karte hain, lekin ye nahi ki koi bhi us cheez ke against act nahi karta jo usse better course lagi hai, aur isliye wo kehte hain incontinent aadmi ke paas knowledge nahi hai jab wo apni pleasures se mastered hota hai, balki opinion hai. Lekin agar ye opinion hai aur knowledge nahi, agar ye ek strong conviction nahi hai jo resist karti hai balki ek weak, jaise un men mein jo hesitate karte hain, hum unki failure ke saath sympathize karte hain aise convictions ko strong appetites ke against stand karne mein; lekin hum wickedness ke saath sympathize nahi karte, na hi doosri kisi bhi blameworthy state ke saath.

Kya, to, ye practical wisdom hai jiska resistance mastered hai? Ye sab states mein sabse strongest hai. Lekin ye absurd hai; wahi aadmi ek hi waqt practically wise aur incontinent hoga, lekin koi bhi nahi kahega ki ek practically wise aadmi ka part hai willingly basest acts karna. Besides, ye pehle hi dikhaya ja chuka hai ki practical wisdom wala aadmi wo hai jo act karega (kyunki wo individual facts se concerned aadmi hai) aur jiske paas doosri virtues bhi hain.

(2) Further, agar continence strong aur bad appetites rakhne mein involve karta hai, temperate aadmi continent nahi hoga na hi continent aadmi temperate; kyunki ek temperate aadmi ke paas na to excessive na bad appetites hongi. Lekin continent aadmi ke paas honi chahiye; kyunki agar appetites good hain, us se restrain karne wali state of character bad hai, isliye sab continence good nahi hogi; jabki agar wo weak aur bad na hon, unhe resist karne mein kuch bhi admirable nahi hai, aur agar wo weak aur bad hain, unhe resist karne mein bhi kuch great nahi hai.

(3) Further, agar continence ek aadmi ko koi bhi aur har opinion ke saath stand karne ke liye ready banata hai, ye bad hai, yani agar ye use ek false opinion ke saath bhi stand karne banaata hai; aur agar incontinence ek aadmi ko koi bhi aur har opinion abandon karne ke apt banati hai, to ek good incontinence hogi, jiska Sophocles ke Philoctetes mein Neoptolemus ek instance hoga; kyunki wo praise ka worthy hai us cheez ke saath na khade rehne ke liye jo Odysseus ne usse karne ke liye persuade kiya, kyunki wo ek lie kehne mein pained hai.

(4) Further, sophistic argument ek difficulty present karta hai; wo syllogism jo men ki opponent ke view se arise hone wale paradoxical results expose karne ki wish se aata hai, taaki wo admire kiye jaayein jab wo succeed hon, ek aisa hai jo humein ek difficulty mein daalta hai (kyunki thought bound fast hoti hai jab ye rest nahi karti kyunki conclusion ise satisfy nahi karta, aur advance nahi kar sakti kyunki ye argument ko refute nahi kar sakti). Ek argument hai jisse follow karta hai ki incontinence ke saath coupled folly virtue hai; ek aadmi wahi karta hai jo wo right sochta hai uska opposite, incontinence ki wajah se, lekin sochta hai jo good hai wo evil hai aur kuch jo usse nahi karna chahiye, aur consequence mein wo wahi karega jo good hai aur wo nahi jo evil hai.

(5) Further, jo aadmi conviction par pleasant ko karta hai aur pursue karta hai aur choose karta hai wo us se better maana jaayega jo aisa karta hai calculation ke result mein nahi balki incontinence ke result mein; kyunki wo cure karne mein aasan hai kyunki wo apna mind change karne ke liye persuade kiya ja sakta hai. Lekin incontinent aadmi ke liye ye proverb apply ho sakta hai 'Jab water choke karta hai, koi ise kya se wash down kare?' Agar usse jo wo karta hai uski rightness ke liye persuade kiya gaya hota, wo desist karta jab usse apna mind change karne ke liye persuade kiya jaata; lekin ab wo kuch quite different ke persuaded hone ke bawajood act karta hai.

(6) Further, agar incontinence aur continence kisi bhi aur har kism ke object se concerned hain, kaun hai jo unqualified sense mein incontinent hai? Kisi ke paas bhi incontinence ke sab forms nahi hain, lekin hum kehte hain kuch log bina qualification ke incontinent hain.

**Incontinent aadmi ke knowledge ke baare mein problem ka solution**

**3.** Kuch is kism ki difficulties arise hoti hain; in mein se kuch points refute kiye jaane chahiye aur baaki ko field mein possession mein chhoda jaana chahiye; kyunki difficulty ka solution truth ki discovery hai. (1) Humein pehle consider karna chahiye, to, ki kya incontinent log knowingly act karte hain ya nahi, aur kis kism ki knowledge ke saath; phir (2) kis kism ke objects ke saath incontinent aur continent aadmi concerned kaha jaa sakta hai (yani chahe kisi bhi aur har pleasure aur pain ke saath ho ya certain determinate kisms ke saath), aur kya continent aadmi aur endurance wala aadmi same hain ya different; aur similarly is inquiry ke germane doosre matters ke respect mein. Hamari investigation ka starting-point hai (a) sawaal ki kya continent aadmi aur incontinent apne objects se differentiate kiye jaate hain ya apne attitude se, yani kya incontinent aadmi incontinent hai simply is kism ki objects se concerned hone ke naate, ya, iske bajaye, apne attitude se, ya, iske bajaye, in dono cheezon se; (b) doosra sawaal ye hai ki kya incontinence aur continence kisi bhi aur har object se concerned hain ya nahi. Wo aadmi jo unqualified sense mein incontinent hai wo na to kisi bhi aur har object se concerned hai, balki precisely un se jinse self-indulgent aadmi concerned hai, na hi use simply un se related hone se characterize kiya jaata hai (kyunki tab uski state self-indulgence jaisi hi hoti), balki unse ek certain way mein related hone se. Kyunki ek apni khud ki choice ke according led hota hai, ye sochte hue ki usse hamesha present pleasure pursue karna chahiye; jabki doosra aisa nahi sochta, phir bhi ise pursue karta hai.

(1) Us suggestion ke liye ki ye true opinion hai aur knowledge nahi jiske against hum incontinently act karte hain, isse argument mein koi farak nahi padta; kyunki kuch log opinion ki state mein hote hue hesitate nahi karte, balki sochte hain ki unhe exactly pata hai. Agar, to, ye notion hai ki apni weak conviction ki wajah se jinke paas opinion hai wo apne judgement ke against un se zyada act karne ke likely hain jo jaante hain, hum answer dete hain ki knowledge aur opinion ke beech is respect mein koi difference hona zaroori nahi; kyunki kuch men apne jo sochte hain usme utne hi convinced hote hain doosre apne jaante hain usme jitne; jaisa Heraclitus ke case se dikhta hai. Lekin (a), kyunki hum 'know' word ko do senses mein use karte hain (kyunki dono aadmi jiske paas knowledge hai lekin use use nahi kar raha aur wo jo ise use kar raha hai, unhe janne wale kaha jaata hai), ye difference banayega ki, jab ek aadmi karta hai jo usse nahi karna chahiye, uske paas knowledge hai lekin wo ise exercise nahi kar raha, ya wo ise exercise kar raha hai; kyunki doosra strange lagta hai, pehla nahi.

(b) Further, kyunki premiss ki do kisms hain, isse rokne ke liye kuch nahi hai ki ek aadmi ke paas dono premisses hon aur apni knowledge ke against act kare, provided ki wo sirf universal premiss use kar raha ho aur particular nahi; kyunki particular acts hain jo kiye jaane hain. Aur universal term ke bhi do kisms hain; ek agent ka predicable hai, doosra object ka; jaise 'dry food har man ke liye good hai', aur 'main ek man hoon', ya 'aisa-aisa food dry hai'; lekin kya 'ye food aisa-aisa hai', iski, ek aadmi ke paas ya to nahi hai ya iski knowledge exercise nahi kar raha. Isliye ek enormous difference hogi in tareeko ke jaanne mein, isliye ek tareeke se jaanna kuch strange nahi lagega, jabki doosre tareeke se jaanna extraordinary lagega.

Aur further (c) knowledge ka possession ek doosre sense mein jo abhi naam liye gaye se different hai wo kuch aisa hai jo men ko hota hai; kyunki knowledge rakhne lekin use na karne ke case ke andar hum state ka ek difference dekhte hain, ye possibility admit karte hue ki ek sense mein knowledge rakhna aur phir bhi ise na rakhna, jaise ek aadmi ke instance mein jo asleep hai, mad hai, ya drunk hai. Lekin ab ye bilkul wahi condition hai men ki jo passions ke influence ke under hain; kyunki anger ke outbursts aur sexual appetites aur kuch doosre aise passions, ye evident hai, actually hamari bodily condition ko alter karte hain, aur kuch men mein even madness ke fits produce karte hain. Ye plain hai, to, ki incontinent log kaha jaana chahiye ek similar condition mein hona un men se jo asleep, mad, ya drunk hain.

Ye fact ki men wahi language use karte hain jo knowledge se flow karti hai kuch bhi prove nahi karta; kyunki even men in passions ke influence ke under scientific proofs aur Empedocles ke verses utter karte hain, aur jinhone abhi ek science seekhna shuru kiya hai wo iske phrases string together kar sakte hain, lekin abhi tak ise jaante nahi; kyunki isse khud ka part banna chahiye, aur isse time lagta hai; isliye humein assume karna chahiye ki incontinent state mein men dwara language ka use iske stage par actors dwara utter kiye jaane se zyada kuch nahi hai.

(d) Phir, hum cause ko is tarah bhi dekh sakte hain jaise ek nature ka student karega. Ek opinion universal hai, doosri particular facts se concerned hai, aur yahan hum perception ki sphere ke andar kuch tak aate hain; jab ek single opinion in dono se result hoti hai, soul ko ek kism ke case mein conclusion affirm karni chahiye, jabki production se concerned opinions ke case mein isse immediately act karna chahiye (jaise agar 'har sweet cheez taste ki jaani chahiye', aur 'ye sweet hai', us sense mein ki ye particular sweet cheezon mein se ek hai, jo aadmi act kar sakta hai aur restrain nahi kiya jaata use same time par actually accordingly act karna chahiye). Jab, to, universal opinion humme present hai jo humein taste karne se restrain karti hai, aur ye opinion bhi hai ki 'har sweet cheez pleasant hai', aur ki 'ye sweet hai' (ab ye wahi opinion hai jo active hai), aur jab appetite humme present hone ka happen hota hai, ek opinion humein isse avoid karne bidding karti hai, lekin appetite humein iski taraf leti hai (kyunki ye hamare har bodily part ko move kar sakti hai); isliye ye turn out hota hai ki ek aadmi incontinently behave karta hai reason ke (ek sense mein) aur ek opinion ke influence ke under, aur ek jo khud mein contrary nahi hai, balki sirf incidentally — kyunki appetite contrary hai, opinion nahi — correct reason ke. Isse ye bhi follow karta hai ki yahi wo reason hai ki lower animals incontinent nahi hote, namely, kyunki unke paas koi universal judgement nahi hai balki sirf imagination aur particulars ka memory hai.

Ki ignorance kaise dissolve hoti hai aur incontinent aadmi apni knowledge kaise regain karta hai, iska explanation wahi hai jo drunk ya asleep aadmi ke case mein hai aur is condition ke liye peculiar nahi hai; humein iske liye natural science ke students ke paas jaana chahiye. Ab, last premiss ek perceptible object ke baare mein ek opinion hote hue, aur ye bhi jo hamari actions determine karta hai, ye ek aadmi ke paas ya to nahi hai jab wo passion ki state mein hai, ya use us sense mein hai jisme knowledge rakhna knowing ka matlab nahi tha balki sirf talking, jaise ek drunk aadmi Empedocles ke verses mutter kar sakta hai. Aur kyunki last term universal nahi hai na equally scientific knowledge ka object universal term ke saath, wo position jo Socrates establish karna chahte the actually result hote lagta hai; kyunki ye us knowledge proper ki presence mein nahi hai ki passion hoti hai (na hi ye wo hai jo passion ke result mein 'ghaseeta jaata hai'), balki perceptual knowledge ki presence mein.

Ye sufficient hona chahiye is sawaal ke hamare answer ke roop mein ki kya ek incontinent aadmi knowingly act karta hai ya nahi, aur kis kism ki knowledge ke saath incontinent hona possible hai.

**Us problem ka solution, ki incontinence ka sphere kya hai: iska proper aur extended sense distinguish kiya gaya hai**

**4.** (2) Humein aage discuss karna chahiye ki kya koi bhi hai jo bina qualification ke incontinent hai, ya sab men jo incontinent hain wo ek particular sense mein aise hain, aur agar hai, to kis kism ke objects se wo concerned hai. Ki continent persons aur endurance ke persons dono, aur incontinent aur soft persons, pleasures aur pains se concerned hain, ye evident hai.

Ab jo cheezein pleasure produce karti hain unme se kuch necessary hain, jabki doosri khud mein choice ka worthy hain lekin excess admit karti hain, pleasure ke bodily causes necessary hote hue (aisi cheezon se mera matlab hai dono food se concerned aur sexual intercourse se concerned, yani bodily matters jinse humne self-indulgence aur temperance ko concerned hone ke roop mein define kiya), jabki doosri necessary nahi hain lekin khud mein choice ka worthy hain (jaise victory, honour, wealth, aur is kism ki good aur pleasant cheezein). Ye aisa hone ke naate, (a) jo baad wale ke reference mein excess tak jaate hain, correct reason ke contrary jo khud unme hai, unhe simply incontinent nahi kaha jaata, balki qualification ke saath incontinent 'money, gain, honour, ya anger ke respect mein' — na simply incontinent, is ground par ki wo incontinent people se different hain aur ek resemblance ki wajah se incontinent kahe jaate hain. (Anthropos ka case compare karein, jisne Olympic games mein ek contest jeeta tha; uske case mein man ki general definition uske liye peculiar definition se thoda different thi, phir bhi ye different thi.) Ye is fact se dikhta hai ki incontinence chahe bina qualification ke ho ya kisi particular bodily pleasure ke respect mein, blame kiya jaata hai na sirf ek fault ke roop mein balki ek kism ke vice ke roop mein, jabki in doosre respects mein incontinent koi bhi log aise blame nahi kiye jaate.

Lekin (b) un logo mein se jo bodily enjoyments ke respect mein incontinent hain, jinse hum kehte hain temperate aur self-indulgent aadmi concerned hain, jo pleasant cheezon ke excesses pursue karta hai — aur painful cheezon ke, hunger aur thirst aur heat aur cold aur touch aur taste ke sab objects ke, shun karta hai — choice se nahi balki apni choice aur apne judgement ke contrary, use incontinent kaha jaata hai, qualification 'is ya us respect mein' ke saath nahi, jaise anger ke respect mein, balki simply. Ye is fact se confirm hota hai ki men ko in pleasures ke respect mein 'soft' kaha jaata hai, lekin doosron mein se kisi ke respect mein nahi. Aur is reason ke liye hum incontinent aur self-indulgent, continent aur temperate aadmi ko group together karte hain — lekin doosre in types mein se kisi ko nahi — kyunki wo somehow same pleasures aur pains se concerned hain; lekin halaanki ye same objects se concerned hain, wo similarly unse related nahi hain, balki inme se kuch ek deliberate choice banate hain jabki doosre nahi.

Isi wajah se humein self-indulgent zyada us aadmi ko describe karna chahiye jo bina appetite ke ya bas ek slight appetite ke saath pleasure ke excesses pursue karta hai aur moderate pains avoid karta hai, us aadmi se jo aisa apni strong appetites ki wajah se karta hai; kyunki pehla kya karega, agar uske paas addition mein ek vigorous appetite ho, aur 'necessary' objects ki kami par ek violent pain ho?

Ab appetites aur pleasures mein se kuch generically noble aur good cheezon ki class ke belong karte hain — kyunki kuch pleasant cheezein nature se choice ke worthy hain, jabki doosre inke contrary hain, aur doosre intermediate hain, hamari previous distinction adopt karte hue — jaise wealth, gain, victory, honour. Aur in mein se ya to is kism ke ya intermediate kism ke sab objects ke reference mein men blame nahi kiye jaate in se affected hone ke liye, unhe desire aur pyaar karne ke liye, balki aisa ek certain way mein karne ke liye, yani excess tak jaane ke liye. (Isi wajah se wo sab jo reason ke contrary ya to naturally noble aur good objects mein se ek se mastered hote hain ya use pursue karte hain, jaise wo jo honour ke baare mein ya children aur parents ke baare mein zaroorat se zyada busy rehte hain, <wicked nahi hain>; kyunki ye bhi goods hain, aur jo inke baare mein busy rehte hain wo praise kiye jaate hain; lekin phir bhi in mein bhi ek excess hai — agar Niobe ki tarah koi gods ke against bhi fight kare, ya apne father ke prati utna hi devoted ho jitna Satyrus, jise 'the filial' nickname diya gaya tha, jo is point par bahut silly maana jaata tha.) Koi wickedness nahi hai, to, in objects ke respect mein, is naam liye gaye reason ke liye, namely, kyunki in mein se har ek nature se khud ke liye choice ka worthy hai; phir bhi inke respect mein excesses bad hain aur avoid ki jaani chahiye. Similarly inke respect mein koi incontinence nahi hai; kyunki incontinence sirf avoid ki jaani chahiye nahi balki blame ki bhi worthy cheez hai; lekin feeling ki state mein ek similarity ki wajah se log incontinence naam apply karte hain, har case mein add karte hue ki ye kis respect mein hai, jaise hum ek bad doctor ya ek bad actor describe kar sakte hain jise humein bad nahi kehna chahiye, simply. Isliye, jaisa is case mein hum term ko bina qualification ke apply nahi karte kyunki in mein se har condition badness nahi balki sirf iske analogous hai, waise hi ye clear hai ki doosre case mein bhi sirf wahi incontinence aur continence maani jaani chahiye jo temperance aur self-indulgence ke same objects se concerned hai, lekin hum term ko anger par ek resemblance ki wajah se apply karte hain; aur isi wajah se hum ek qualification ke saath kehte hain 'anger ke respect mein incontinent' jaise hum kehte hain 'honour ke, ya gain ke respect mein incontinent'.

**Incontinence ke extended sense mein ek brutish aur ek morbid form shaamil hai**

**5.** Kuch cheezein nature se pleasant hain, aur inme se kuch bina qualification ke, aur doosri particular classes ke reference mein, chahe animals ki hon ya men ki; jabki doosre nature se pleasant nahi hain, lekin unme se kuch system ki injuries ki wajah se aisi ban jaati hain, aur doosre acquired habits ki wajah se, aur doosre originally bad natures ki wajah se. Ye aisa hone ke naate, ye possible hai har ek in baad wale kisms ke respect mein similar states of character discover karna un se jo pehle wale ke respect mein recognize kiye gaye hain; mera matlab brutish states se hai, jaise us female ke case mein, jo, wo kehte hain, pregnant women ko rip open karti hai aur infants devour karti hai, ya un cheezon mein jinme Black Sea ke aas paas ki kuch tribes jo savage ho gayi hain delight karti maani jaati hain — raw meat mein ya human flesh mein, ya apne bacchon ko ek doosre ko feast karne ke liye lend karne mein — ya Phalaris ki story mein.

Ye states brutish hain, lekin doosre disease ke result mein arise hote hain (ya, kuch cases mein, madness ke, jaise us aadmi ke saath jisne apni mother ko sacrifice aur eat kiya, ya us slave ke saath jisne apne fellow ka liver khaaya), aur doosre morbid states hain jo custom se result hote hain, jaise hair pluck karne ya nails gnaw karne ki habit, ya even coals ya earth, aur inke addition mein paederasty; kyunki ye kuch mein nature se arise hoti hain aur doosron mein, jaise un logo mein jo childhood se lust ke victims rahe hain, habit se.

Ab un logo mein jinme nature aisi state ka cause hai koi bhi unhe incontinent nahi kahega, isse zyada nahi jitna koi women par epithet apply karega, copulation mein unke passive part ki wajah se; na hi koi in par apply karega jo habit ke result mein ek morbid condition mein hain. Habit ki ye various kisms rakhna vice ki limits se pare hai, jaise brutishness bhi hai; kyunki wo aadmi jiske paas ye hain, unhe master kare ya unse mastered ho, wo simple <continence ya> incontinence nahi hai balki wo jo analogy se aisi hai, jaise wo aadmi jo anger ke fits ke respect mein is condition mein hai use us feeling ke respect mein incontinent kaha jaana chahiye, lekin simply incontinent nahi.

Kyunki har excessive state chahe folly ki ho, cowardice ki, self-indulgence ki, ya bad temper ki, ya to brutish hai ya morbid; wo aadmi jo nature se har cheez se fear karne ke apt hai, even ek mouse ke squeak se, cowardly hai ek brutish cowardice ke saath, jabki wo aadmi jo ek weasel se fear kiya wo disease ke consequence mein aisa kiya; aur foolish logo mein se jo nature se thoughtless hain aur sirf apni senses se jeete hain wo brutish hain, jaise distant barbarians ki kuch races, jabki wo jo disease ke result mein aise hain (jaise epilepsy ki) ya madness ki wajah se morbid hain. In characteristics mein se, ye possible hai kuch ke paas sirf times par hona, aur unse mastered na hona, jaise Phalaris ne shayad ek child ki flesh khaane ki desire ko ya unnatural sexual pleasure ke liye ek appetite ko restrain kiya ho; lekin ye bhi possible hai mastered hona, sirf feelings rakhna nahi. Isliye, jaise wickedness jo human level par hai wickedness simply kahi jaati hai, jabki wo jo nahi hai use wickedness simply nahi balki qualification 'brutish' ya 'morbid' ke saath kaha jaata hai, isi tarah ye plain hai ki kuch incontinence brutish hai aur kuch morbid, jabki sirf wo jo human self-indulgence se correspond karti hai incontinence simply hai.

Ki incontinence aur continence, to, sirf un same objects se concerned hain jinse self-indulgence aur temperance concerned hain, aur ki jo doosre objects se concerned hai wo incontinence se ek distinct type hai, aur ek metaphor se incontinence kaha jaata hai simply nahi, ye plain hai.

**Anger ke respect mein incontinence, incontinence proper se kam disgraceful hai**

**6.** Ki anger ke respect mein incontinence appetites ke respect mein incontinence se kam disgraceful hai, ye hum ab dekhne ke liye aage badhenge. (I) Anger reason ko kuch extent tak sunta lagta hai, lekin ise mishear karta hai, jaise hasty servants karte hain jo poori baat sune bina hi bhaag jaate hain jo koi kehta hai, aur phir order muddle kar dete hain, ya jaise dogs bark karte hain agar door par sirf ek knock ho, ye dekhne se pehle ki ye ek friend hai ya nahi; isi tarah anger apni warmth aur hastiness ki nature ki wajah se, sunta to hai, lekin ek order nahi sunta, aur revenge lene ke liye spring karta hai.
