Kyunki reason ya appearance humein inform karti hai ki humne insult ya slight feel kiya hai, aur anger, jaise reasoning karte hue ki isi jaisi kuch bhi fight karni chahiye, straightaway boil up karta hai; jabki appetite, agar reason ya perception sirf kehte hain ki ek object pleasant hai, iske enjoyment ki taraf spring karta hai. Isliye anger ek sense mein reason obey karta hai, lekin appetite nahi karta. Isliye ye zyada disgraceful hai; kyunki jo aadmi anger ke respect mein incontinent hai wo ek sense mein reason se conquered hai, jabki doosra appetite se conquered hai aur reason se nahi.

(2) Further, hum logo ko natural desires follow karne ke liye zyada aasaani se pardon karte hain, kyunki hum unhe zyada aasaani se pardon karte hain aise appetites follow karne ke liye jo sab men ke liye common hain, aur jitne wo common hain; ab anger aur bad temper appetites for excess se zyada natural hain, yani unnecessary objects ke liye. Us aadmi ka example lein jo apni father ko strike karne ke charge par khud ko defend karta hai kehte hue 'Haan, lekin usne bhi apne father ko strike kiya, aur usne apne ko,' (apne child ki taraf point karte hue) 'ye boy mujhe strike karega jab wo man banega; ye family mein chalta hai'; ya wo aadmi jo jab apna son use ghaseet raha tha wo doorway par ruk jaane ko kehta tha, kyunki usne khud apne father ko sirf itni door tak hi ghaseeta tha.

(3) Further, wo log jo doosron ke against plotting mein zyada given hain wo zyada criminal hain. Ab ek angry aadmi plotting mein given nahi hai, na hi anger khud — ye open hai; lekin appetite ki nature illustrate hoti hai us se jise poets Aphrodite kehte hain, 'guile-weaving daughter of Cyprus', aur Homer ke words se uske 'embroidered girdle' ke baare mein: 'Aur wooing ka whisper wahan hai, jiski subtlety wise ke bhi wits chura leti hai, chahe wo kitna bhi prudent ho.' Isliye agar incontinence ka ye form anger ke respect mein wale se zyada criminal aur disgraceful hai, ye dono bina qualification ke incontinence hai aur ek sense mein vice hai.

(4) Further, koi bhi wanton outrage commit nahi karta pain ki feeling ke saath, lekin har koi jo anger mein act karta hai wo pain ke saath act karta hai, jabki jo aadmi outrage commit karta hai wo pleasure ke saath act karta hai. Agar, to, jin acts par angry hona sabse just hai wo doosron se zyada criminal hain, appetite ki wajah se incontinence zyada criminal hai; kyunki anger mein koi wanton outrage involve nahi hota.

Plainly, to, appetite se concerned incontinence anger se concerned se zyada disgraceful hai, aur continence aur incontinence bodily appetites aur pleasures se concerned hain; lekin humein in mein khud ki differences bhi grasp karni chahiye. Kyunki, jaisa beginning mein kaha gaya, kuch human aur natural hain dono kind aur magnitude mein, doosre brutish hain, aur doosre organic injuries aur diseases ki wajah se hain. Sirf pehle wale se temperance aur self-indulgence concerned hain; isi wajah se hum lower animals ko na to temperate na self-indulgent kehte hain, siwaye ek metaphor se, aur sirf agar koi ek race of animals wantonness, destructiveness, aur omnivorous greed mein doosre se as a whole exceed karti hai; inke paas na choice ka na calculation ka power hai, balki wo natural norm se departures hain, jaise, men ke beech, madmen hain. Ab brutishness vice se ek less evil hai, halaanki zyada alarming; kyunki ye nahi hai ki better part perverted ho chuka hai, jaise man mein — unke paas koi better part nahi hai. Isliye ye lifeless cheez ko ek living se badness ke respect mein compare karne jaisa hai; kyunki jo cheez apni movement ka koi originative source nahi rakhti uski badness hamesha kam hurtful hai, aur reason ek originative source hai. Isliye ye injustice ko abstract mein ek unjust aadmi se compare karne jaisa hai. Har ek ek sense mein worse hai; kyunki ek bad aadmi ek brute jitni evil se das hazaar guna zyada evil karega.

**Softness aur endurance: incontinence ke do forms — weakness aur impetuosity**

**7.** Touch aur taste ke through arise hone wale pleasures aur pains aur appetites aur aversions ke respect mein, jinme dono self-indulgence aur temperance pehle narrow ki gayi thi, ye possible hai aisi state mein hona ki even un se bhi defeated ho jaaye jinse zyadatar log master hote hain, ya even un se master ho jaaye jinse zyadatar log defeated hote hain; in possibilities mein se, pleasures se related wo incontinence aur continence hain, pains se related softness aur endurance. Zyadatar logo ki state intermediate hai, halaanki wo worse states ki taraf zyada lean karte hain.

Ab, kyunki kuch pleasures necessary hain jabki doosri nahi, aur ek point tak necessary hain jabki inke excesses nahi hain, na hi deficiencies, aur ye equally true hai appetites aur pains ke liye bhi, jo aadmi pleasant cheezon ke excesses pursue karta hai, ya necessary objects ko excess tak pursue karta hai, aur choice se aisa karta hai, unki khud ki khaatir aur bilkul bhi unse distinct kisi result ki khaatir nahi, wo self-indulgent hai; kyunki aisa aadmi necessarily bina regrets ke hai, aur isliye incurable hai, kyunki ek aadmi bina regrets ke cure nahi ho sakta. Wo aadmi jo inhe pursue karne mein deficient hai self-indulgent ka opposite hai; jo aadmi intermediate hai wo temperate hai. Similarly, ek aadmi hai jo bodily pains ko avoid karta hai isliye nahi ki wo unse defeated hai balki choice se. (Un logo mein se jo aise acts choose nahi karte, ek kism ka aadmi involved pleasure ke result mein unki taraf led hota hai, doosra kyunki wo appetite se arise hone wale pain ko avoid karta hai, isliye ye types ek doosre se differ karte hain. Ab koi bhi ek aadmi ko worse sochega agar bina appetite ke ya weak appetite ke saath wo kuch disgraceful kare, us se jo usne powerful appetite ke influence ke under kiya ho, aur worse usse jo anger mein nahi balki bina anger ke ek blow strike kare; kyunki wo kya karta agar wo strongly affected hota? Isi wajah se self-indulgent aadmi incontinent se worse hai.) Naam ki gayi states mein se, to, baad wali ek kism ki softness hai; pehli self-indulgence hai. Jabki incontinent aadmi ke against continent opposed hai, soft ke against endurance ka aadmi opposed hai; kyunki endurance resist karne mein consist karta hai, jabki continence conquer karne mein consist karta hai, aur resist karna aur conquer karna different hain, jaise not being beaten winning se different hai; isi wajah se continence bhi endurance se zyada choice ka worthy hai. Ab jo aadmi un cheezon ko resist karne ke respect mein deficient hai jinhe zyadatar men dono resist bhi karte hain aur successfully resist bhi karte hain wo soft aur effeminate hai; kyunki effeminacy bhi softness ka ek kism hai; aisa aadmi apna cloak trail karta hai isse uthaane ka pain avoid karne ke liye, aur invalid khelta hai bina khud ko wretched sochte hue, halaanki jise wo imitate karta hai wo ek wretched aadmi hai.

Case similar hai continence aur incontinence ke respect mein bhi. Kyunki agar ek aadmi violent aur excessive pleasures ya pains se defeated hai, isme kuch wonderful nahi hai; indeed hum use pardon karne ke liye ready hain agar usne resist kiya ho, jaise Theodectes ke Philoctetes karta hai jab snake ne bite kiya, ya Carcinus ke Alope mein Cercyon, aur jaise log jo apni laughter restrain karne ki koshish karte hain guffaw mein burst out ho jaate hain, jaisa Xenophantus ke saath hua. Lekin ye surprising hai agar ek aadmi un pleasures ya pains se defeated hai aur inhe resist nahi kar sakta jinke against zyadatar log hold out kar sakte hain, jab ye heredity ya disease ki wajah se na ho, jaise wo softness jo Scythians ke kings mein hereditary hai, ya wo jo female sex ko male se distinguish karti hai.

Amusement ka lover bhi, self-indulgent maana jaata hai, lekin really soft hai. Kyunki amusement ek relaxation hai, kyunki ye work se ek rest hai; aur amusement ka lover un logo mein se ek hai jo isme excess tak jaate hain.

Incontinence ka ek kism impetuosity hai, doosra weakness. Kyunki kuch men deliberate karne ke baad apni deliberation ke conclusions ke saath stand karne mein fail karte hain apni emotion ki wajah se, doosre kyunki unhone deliberate nahi kiya wo apni emotion se led hote hain; kyunki kuch men (bilkul jaise wo log jo pehle doosron ko tickle karte hain khud tickle nahi hote), agar unhone pehle perceive kiya ho aur dekha ho jo aa raha hai aur pehle khud ko aur apni calculative faculty ko rouse kiya ho, wo apni emotion se defeated nahi hote, chahe ye pleasant ho ya painful. Ye keen aur excitable log hain jo especially incontinence ke impetuous form se suffer karte hain; kyunki pehle apni quickness ki wajah se aur doosre apne passions ki violence ki wajah se argument ka await nahi karte, kyunki wo appearance follow karne ke apt hain.

**Self-indulgence, incontinence se worse hai**

**8.** Self-indulgent aadmi, jaisa kaha gaya, koi regrets nahi rakhta; kyunki wo apni choice ke saath stand karta hai; lekin koi bhi incontinent aadmi regrets ke subject hai. Isi wajah se position waisi nahi hai jaisi problem ki formulation mein express ki gayi thi, balki self-indulgent aadmi incurable hai aur incontinent aadmi curable; kyunki wickedness ek disease jaisi hai, jaise dropsy ya consumption, jabki incontinence epilepsy jaisi hai; pehli ek permanent, doosri ek intermittent badness hai. Aur generally incontinence aur vice kind mein different hain; vice khud ke prati unconscious hai, incontinence nahi hai (incontinent men khud mein se, jo temporarily khud se pare ho jaate hain wo un se better hain jinke paas reason hai lekin wo iske saath abide nahi karte, kyunki baad wale ek weaker passion se defeated hote hain, aur doosron ki tarah previous deliberation ke bina act nahi karte); kyunki incontinent aadmi un logo jaisa hai jo quickly aur little wine par drunk ho jaate hain, yani zyadatar logo se kam mein.

Evidently, to, incontinence vice nahi hai (halaanki shayad ek qualified sense mein aisa hai); kyunki incontinence choice ke contrary hai jabki vice choice ke according hai; halaanki wo actions ke respect mein similar hain jinki taraf wo le jaate hain; jaise Demodocus ki saying Milesians ke baare mein, 'Milesians sense se without nahi hain, lekin wo wo cheezein karte hain jo senseless log karte hain,' isi tarah incontinent log criminal nahi hain, lekin wo criminal acts karenge.

Ab, kyunki incontinent aadmi bodily pleasures pursue karne ka apt hai, conviction par nahi, jo excessive aur correct reason ke contrary hain, jabki self-indulgent aadmi convinced hai kyunki wo unhe pursue karne wale kism ka aadmi hai, ye iske contrary hai ki pehla easily persuade kiya jaata hai apna mind change karne ke liye, jabki doosra nahi. Kyunki virtue aur vice respectively first principle ko preserve aur destroy karte hain, aur actions mein final cause first principle hai, jaise hypotheses mathematics mein hain; na to us case mein reason hai jo first principles sikhaata hai, na hi yahan hai — virtue chahe natural ho ya habituation se produced, wahi hai jo right principle ke baare mein right opinion sikhaati hai. Aisa aadmi, to, temperate hai; contrary type self-indulgent hai.

Lekin ek kism ka aadmi hai jo passion ke result mein aur correct reason ke contrary carried away hota hai — ek aadmi jise passion mastered karta hai isliye wo correct reason ke according act nahi karta, lekin usse itna master nahi karta ki wo aise pleasures ko without reserve pursue karne ke liye believe karne ready ho; ye incontinent aadmi hai, jo self-indulgent aadmi se better hai, aur bina qualification ke bad nahi hai; kyunki uske andar ki best cheez, first principle, preserved hai.

Aur iske contrary ek doosra kism ka aadmi hai, wo jo apni convictions ke saath abide karta hai aur carried away nahi hota, kam se kam passion ke result mein. Ye in considerations se evident hai ki baad wala ek good state hai aur pehla ek bad.

**Continence ka obstinacy, incontinence, 'insensibility', temperance se relation**

**9.** Kya continent aadmi wo hai jo kisi bhi aur har reasoning aur kisi bhi aur har choice ke saath abide karta hai, ya wo jo right choice ke saath abide karta hai, aur kya incontinent wo hai jo kisi bhi aur har choice aur kisi bhi aur har reasoning ko abandon karta hai, ya wo jo us reasoning ko abandon karta hai jo false nahi hai aur us choice ko jo right hai; ye hai jaise humne pehle problem ki apni statement mein rakha tha. Ya kya ye incidentally kisi bhi aur har choice hai lekin per se true reasoning aur right choice jiske saath ek abide karta hai aur doosra nahi karta? Agar koi ise choose ya pursue karta hai us cheez ki khaatir, per se wo doosre ko pursue aur choose karta hai, lekin incidentally pehle ko. Lekin jab hum bina qualification ke baat karte hain hum matlab lete hain jo per se hai. Isliye ek sense mein ek abide karta hai, aur doosra abandon karta hai, kisi bhi aur har opinion ko; lekin bina qualification ke, true opinion ko.

Kuch log hain jo apni opinion ke saath abide karne ke apt hain, jinhe obstinate kaha jaata hai, namely, wo jo first instance mein persuade karna hard hain aur easily persuade nahi kiye jaate change karne ke liye; inke paas continent aadmi se kuch likeness hai, jaise prodigal ek way mein liberal aadmi jaisa hai aur rash aadmi confident aadmi jaisa; lekin wo bahut respects mein different hain. Kyunki ye passion aur appetite hai jise ek yield nahi karega, kyunki occasion par continent aadmi reason ko yield karega; lekin ye reason hai jise doosre yield karne se refuse karte hain, kyunki wo appetites form karte hain aur unme se bahut se apni pleasures dwara led hote hain. Ab wo log jo obstinate hain wo opinionated, ignorant, aur boorish hain — opinionated pleasure aur pain se influenced hote hue; kyunki wo victory mein delight karte hain jo wo gain karte hain agar unhe change karne ke liye persuade na kiya jaaye, aur pained hote hain agar unke decisions null aur void ban jaayein jaise decrees kabhi hote hain; isliye wo continent aadmi se zyada incontinent se resemble karte hain.

Lekin kuch aise hain jo apni resolutions ke saath abide karne mein fail hote hain, incontinence ke result mein nahi, jaise Sophocles ke Philoctetes mein Neoptolemus; phir bhi ye pleasure ki khaatir tha ki usne stand fast nahi kiya — lekin ek noble pleasure; kyunki truth batana uske liye noble tha, lekin use Odysseus dwara ek lie kehne ke liye persuade kiya gaya tha. Kyunki har koi jo pleasure ki khaatir kuch bhi karta hai wo na to self-indulgent hai na bad na incontinent, balki wo jo ek disgraceful pleasure ke liye aisa karta hai.

Kyunki ek kism ka aadmi bhi hai jo bodily cheezon mein usse kam delight leta hai jitna usse lena chahiye, aur reason ke saath abide nahi karta, wo jo uske aur incontinent aadmi ke beech intermediate hai wo continent aadmi hai; kyunki incontinent aadmi reason ke saath abide karne mein fail hota hai kyunki wo in mein too much delight karta hai, aur ye aadmi kyunki wo in mein too little delight karta hai; jabki continent aadmi reason ke saath abide karta hai aur na to account par change karta hai. Ab agar continence good hai, dono contrary states bad honi chahiye, jaisa wo actually appear hoti hain; lekin kyunki doosra extreme few logo mein aur seldom dekha jaata hai, jaise temperance sirf self-indulgence ke contrary maani jaati hai, waise hi continence incontinence ke.

Kyunki bahut se naam analogically apply kiye jaate hain, ye analogy se hai ki hum temperate aadmi ki 'continence' ki baat karne aaye hain; kyunki dono continent aadmi aur temperate aadmi aise hain ki wo bodily pleasures ki khaatir reason ke contrary kuch bhi nahi karte, lekin pehle ke paas bad appetites hain aur doosre ke paas nahi, aur doosra aisa hai ki wo reason ke contrary pleasure feel nahi karta, jabki pehla aisa hai ki wo pleasure feel karta hai lekin isse led nahi hota. Aur incontinent aur self-indulgent aadmi bhi ek doosre jaise hain; wo different hain, lekin dono bodily pleasures pursue karte hain — baad wala, phir bhi, ye bhi sochte hue ki usse aisa karna chahiye, jabki pehla ye nahi sochta.

**Practical wisdom incontinence ke saath compatible nahi hai, lekin cleverness hai**

**10.** Na hi wahi aadmi practical wisdom rakh sakta hai aur incontinent ho sakta hai; kyunki ye dikhaya ja chuka hai ki ek aadmi ek hi waqt practically wise hota hai, aur character ke respect mein good. Further, ek aadmi ke paas practical wisdom sirf knowing se nahi balki act karne ke able hone se hoti hai; lekin incontinent aadmi act karne ke unable hai — phir bhi kuch bhi rokta nahi hai ek clever aadmi ko incontinent hone se; isi wajah se kabhi kabhi actually socha jaata hai ki kuch log practical wisdom rakhte hain lekin incontinent hain, namely, kyunki cleverness aur practical wisdom differ karte hain us way mein jo humne apni first discussions mein describe ki hai, aur apni reasoning ke respect mein near together hain, lekin apni choice ke respect mein differ karte hain — na hi phir incontinent aadmi us aadmi jaisa hai jo jaanta hai aur ek truth contemplate kar raha hai, balki us aadmi jaisa jo asleep ya drunk hai. Aur wo voluntarily act karta hai (kyunki wo ek sense mein knowledge ke saath act karta hai dono jo wo karta hai uska aur jis end ke liye wo isse karta hai uska), lekin wicked nahi hai, kyunki uski choice good hai; isliye wo half-wicked hai. Aur wo criminal nahi hai; kyunki wo malice aforethought se act nahi karta; incontinent aadmi ke do types mein se ek deliberation ke conclusions ke saath abide nahi karta, jabki excitable aadmi bilkul deliberate nahi karta. Aur isi tarah incontinent aadmi ek city jaisa hai jo sab right decrees pass karti hai aur good laws rakhti hai, lekin unka use nahi karti, jaise Anaxandrides ki jesting remark mein, 'City ne ise willed kiya, jo laws ki koi parwaah nahi karti'; lekin wicked aadmi ek city jaisa hai jo apne laws use karta hai, lekin wicked laws use karne ke liye rakhta hai.

Ab incontinence aur continence us cheez se concerned hain jo zyadatar men ki characteristic state se excess mein hai; kyunki continent aadmi zyadatar men se zyada apni resolutions ke saath abide karta hai aur incontinent aadmi kam.

Incontinence ke forms mein se, excitable logo ka wo un se zyada curable hai jo deliberate karte hain lekin apni deliberations ke saath abide nahi karte, aur wo jo habituation se incontinent hain wo un se zyada curable hain jinme incontinence innate hai; kyunki ek habit change karna apni nature change karne se aasan hai; even habit change karna hard hai isi wajah se ki ye nature jaisi hai, jaise Evenus kehta hai: 'Main kehta hoon habit long practice hi hai, friend, aur ye end mein men ki nature ban jaati hai.'

Humne ab state kar diya hai continence, incontinence, endurance, aur softness kya hain, aur kaise ye states ek doosre se related hain.

## PLEASURE

**Pleasure ke against teen views aur unke liye arguments**

**11.** Pleasure aur pain ka study political philosopher ke province ka belong karta hai; kyunki wo end ka architect hai, jiske view se hum ek cheez ko bad kehte hain aur doosre ko good bina qualification ke. Further, ye humare necessary tasks mein se ek hai unhe consider karna; kyunki na sirf humne lay down kiya ki moral virtue aur vice pains aur pleasures se concerned hain, balki zyadatar log kehte hain ki happiness pleasure involve karti hai; isi wajah se blessed aadmi ko ek naam se pukara jaata hai jo enjoyment ka matlab denewale word se derived hai.

Ab (1) kuch log sochte hain ki koi bhi pleasure good nahi hai, na khud mein na incidentally, kyunki good aur pleasure same nahi hain; (2) doosre sochte hain ki kuch pleasures good hain lekin zyadatar bad hain. (3) Phir ek teesra view hai, ki even agar sab pleasures goods hain, phir bhi duniya ki best cheez pleasure nahi ho sakti. (1) Us view ke liye diye gaye reasons ki pleasure bilkul bhi ek good nahi hai (a) ye hai ki har pleasure ek natural state ki taraf ek perceptible process hai, aur ki koi process apni end ke same kind ka nahi hota, jaise building ka koi process ek house ke same kind ka nahi hota. (b) Ek temperate aadmi pleasures avoid karta hai. (c) Practical wisdom wala aadmi wo pursue karta hai jo pain se free hai, jo pleasant hai wo nahi. (d) Pleasures thinking ke liye ek hindrance hain, aur jitna zyada koi inme delight karta hai utna zyada, jaise sexual pleasure mein; kyunki koi bhi ismein absorbed hote hue kisi cheez ke baare mein nahi soch sakta. (e) Pleasure ki koi art nahi hai; lekin har good kisi art ka product hai. (f) Children aur brutes pleasures pursue karte hain. (2) Us view ke reasons ki sab pleasures good nahi hain ye hain ki (a) kuch pleasures hain jo actually base hain aur reproach ke objects, aur (b) kuch harmful pleasures hain; kyunki kuch pleasant cheezein unhealthy hain. (3) Us view ka reason ki duniya ki best cheez pleasure nahi hai ye hai ki pleasure ek end nahi hai balki ek process hai.

**Us view ki discussion ki pleasure ek good nahi hai**

**12.** Ye kaafi kuch hain wo cheezein jo kahi jaati hain. Ki in grounds se ye follow nahi karta ki pleasure ek good nahi hai, ya even chief good, ye following considerations se plain hai. (A) (a) Pehla, kyunki jo good hai wo do senses mein se kisi ek mein ho sakta hai (ek cheez simply good aur doosri ek particular person ke liye good), natural constitutions aur being ki states, aur isliye corresponding movements aur processes bhi, correspondingly divisible honge. Un mein se jo bad maani jaati hain unme se kuch bina qualification ke liya jaaye to bad hongi lekin ek particular person ke liye bad nahi, balki uski choice ka worthy, aur kuch even ek particular person ke liye bhi choice ka worthy nahi honge, balki sirf ek particular time par aur ek short period ke liye, halaanki bina qualification ke nahi; jabki doosre pleasures bhi nahi hain, lekin aise lagti hain, namely, wo sab jo pain involve karti hain aur jinka end curative hai, jaise wo processes jo sick persons mein chalte hain.

(b) Further, ek kism ka good activity hote hue aur doosra state, jo processes humein hamari natural state mein restore karte hain wo sirf incidentally pleasant hain; kyunki us matter ke liye appetites mein kaam karti activity humari state aur nature ke itne hisse ki activity hai jo unimpaired reh gaya hai; kyunki actually aise pleasures hain jo koi pain ya appetite involve nahi karti (jaise contemplation ke wale), aisi case mein nature bilkul bhi defective nahi hai. Ki doosre incidental hain ye is fact se indicate hota hai ki men same pleasant objects ko enjoy nahi karte jab unki nature apni settled state mein hai jaisa wo tab karte hain jab ye replenish ho rahi hai, balki pehle case mein wo un cheezon ko enjoy karte hain jo bina qualification ke pleasant hain, doosre mein inke contraries bhi; kyunki tab wo even sharp aur bitter cheezein bhi enjoy karte hain, jinme se koi bhi na to nature se pleasant hai na bina qualification ke. Aur isliye ye pleasures ke saath bhi same hai; kyunki jaise pleasant cheezein differ karti hain, waise hi unse arise hone wali pleasures bhi.

(c) Phir, ye necessary nahi hai ki pleasure se better koi doosri cheez ho, jaise kuch kehte hain end process se better hai; kyunki pleasures processes nahi hain na hi sab process involve karti hain — wo activities aur ends hain; na hi wo arise hoti hain jab hum koi faculty acquire kar rahe hain, balki jab hum ise exercise kar rahe hain; aur sab pleasures ki koi different end nahi hoti khud se, balki sirf un persons ki pleasures ki jo apni nature ki perfecting ki taraf le jaaye jaa rahe hain. Isi wajah se ye right nahi hai kehna ki pleasure perceptible process hai, balki ise natural state ki activity kaha jaana chahiye, aur 'perceptible' ki jagah 'unimpeded'. Ye kuch logo dwara process socha jaata hai sirf isliye kyunki wo sochte hain ye strict sense mein good hai; kyunki wo sochte hain ki activity process hai, jo ye nahi hai.

(B) Ye view ki pleasures bad hain kyunki kuch pleasant cheezein unhealthy hain aisa hai jaise kehna ki healthy cheezein bad hain kyunki kuch healthy cheezein moneymaking ke liye bad hain; dono is mentioned respect mein bad hain, lekin wo is reason ke liye bad nahi hain — indeed, thinking khud kabhi kabhi health ke liye injurious hoti hai. Na practical wisdom na hi being ki koi state usse arise hone wali pleasure se impede hoti hai; ye foreign pleasures hain jo impede karti hain; kyunki thinking aur learning se arise hone wali pleasures humein aur zyada think aur learn karayengi.

(C) Fact ki koi bhi pleasure kisi art ka product nahi hai naturally enough arise hoti hai; kisi doosri activity ki bhi koi art nahi hai, sirf corresponding faculty ki hai; halaanki us matter ke liye perfumer aur cook ki arts pleasure ki arts maani jaati hain.

(D) Wo arguments jo is ground par based hain ki temperate aadmi pleasure avoid karta hai aur practical wisdom wala aadmi painless life pursue karta hai, aur ki children aur brutes pleasure pursue karte hain, sab ek hi consideration se refute ho jaate hain. Humne point out kiya hai kis sense mein pleasures bina qualification ke good hain aur kis sense mein kuch good nahi hain; ab dono brutes aur children baad wale kism ki pleasures pursue karte hain (aur practical wisdom wala aadmi us kism se tranquil freedom pursue karta hai), namely, wo jo appetite aur pain imply karti hain, yani bodily pleasures (kyunki ye hi is nature ki hain) aur inke excesses, jinke respect mein self-indulgent aadmi self-indulgent hai. Isi wajah se temperate aadmi in pleasures ko avoid karta hai; kyunki even uske paas bhi apni khud ki pleasures hain.

**Us view ki discussion ki pleasure chief good nahi hai**

**13.** Lekin further (E) ye agree kiya jaata hai ki pain bad hai aur avoid ki jaani chahiye; kyunki kuch pain bina qualification ke bad hai, aur doosra pain bad hai kyunki ye kisi respect mein humare liye ek impediment hai. Ab jo avoid ki jaani hai uska contrary, ek avoid kiye jaane wali aur bad cheez ke roop mein, good hai. Pleasure, to, necessarily ek good hai. Speusippus ka solution, ki ye us tarah hai jaise greater dono less aur equal ka contrary hai, successful nahi hai; kyunki wo nahi kahenge ki pleasure essentially sirf evil ki ek species hai.

Aur (F) agar certain pleasures bad hain, isse chief good ka kisi pleasure hona rokega nahi, bilkul jaise chief good knowledge ka koi form ho sakta hai halaanki certain kism ki knowledge bad hai. Shayad ye even necessary hai, agar har disposition ki unimpeded activities hain, ki, chahe sab hamari dispositions ki activity (agar unimpeded) ho ya inme se kisi ek ki activity ho happiness, ye humari choice ka sabse worthy cheez hona chahiye; aur ye activity pleasure hai. Isliye chief good kisi pleasure ka hoga, halaanki zyadatar pleasures shayad bina qualification ke bad hon. Aur isi reason ke liye sab men sochte hain ki happy life pleasant hai aur pleasure ko apne happiness ke ideal mein bunte hain — aur reasonably bhi; kyunki koi bhi activity perfect nahi hai jab ye impeded ho, aur happiness ek perfect cheez hai; isi wajah se happy aadmi ko body ke goods aur external goods chahiye, yani fortune ke, namely, taaki wo in tareeko se impede na ho. Wo jo kehte hain ki rack par victim ya wo aadmi jo great misfortunes mein girta hai happy hai agar wo good hai, chahe wo aisa mean karein ya na karein, nonsense baat kar rahe hain.

Ab kyunki humein fortune ki bhi doosri cheezon ki tarah zaroorat hai, kuch log sochte hain good fortune wahi cheez hai jo happiness hai; lekin ye wo nahi hai, kyunki even good fortune khud excess mein hone par ek impediment hai, aur shayad tab ise good fortune nahi kaha jaana chahiye; kyunki iski limit happiness ke reference se fix hoti hai.

Aur indeed ye fact ki sab cheezein, dono brutes aur men, pleasure pursue karte hain iska indication hai ki ye somehow chief good hai: 'Koi bhi voice poori tarah lost nahi hai jo bahut se logo ki hai...' Lekin kyunki koi bhi ek nature ya state na sab ke liye best hai na aisi maani jaati hai, na hi sab same pleasure pursue karte hain; phir bhi sab pleasure pursue karte hain. Aur shayad wo actually us pleasure ko nahi pursue karte jo wo sochte hain wo pursue karte hain na wo jise wo kehte ki wo pursue karte hain, balki same pleasure; kyunki sab cheezon mein nature se kuch divine hai. Lekin bodily pleasures ne naam apne liye appropriate kar liya hai dono is wajah se ki hum aksar apna course inhi ki taraf steer karte hain aur is wajah se ki sab men inme share karte hain; isliye, kyunki ye akele familiar hain, log sochte hain koi doosri nahi hain.

Ye bhi evident hai ki agar pleasure, yani hamari faculties ki activity, ek good nahi hai, to ye case nahi hoga ki happy aadmi ek pleasant life jeeta hai; kyunki kis end ke liye use pleasure ki zaroorat honi chahiye, agar ye good nahi hai lekin happy aadmi even ek painful life jee sakta hai? Kyunki pain na to ek evil hai na ek good, agar pleasure nahi hai; to kyun use ise avoid karna chahiye? Isliye, bhi, good aadmi ki life kisi doosre se zyada pleasant nahi hogi, agar uski activities zyada pleasant nahi hain.

**Us view ki discussion ki zyadatar pleasures bad hain, aur bodily pleasures ko pleasure in general se identify karne ki tendency ki**

**14.** (G) Bodily pleasures ke respect mein, jo log kehte hain ki kuch pleasures bahut zyada choose ki jaani chahiye, namely, noble pleasures, lekin bodily pleasures nahi, yani wo jinse self-indulgent aadmi concerned hai, unhe consider karna chahiye kyun, to, contrary pains bad hain. Kyunki bad ka contrary good hai. Kya necessary pleasures good hain us sense mein jisme even jo bad nahi hai wo good hai? Ya kya wo ek point tak good hain? Kya ye ki jahan aapke paas states aur processes hain jinme too much nahi ho sakta, wahan corresponding pleasure mein bhi too much nahi ho sakta, aur ki jahan ek ka too much ho sakta hai wahan doosre ka bhi ho sakta hai? Ab bodily goods ka too much ho sakta hai, aur bad aadmi bad hai excess pursue karne ke virtue se, necessary pleasures pursue karne ke virtue se nahi (kyunki sab men kisi na kisi tarah dono dainty foods aur wines aur sexual intercourse enjoy karte hain, lekin sab men aisa nahi karte jaise unhe karna chahiye). Contrary case pain ke saath hai; kyunki wo iske excess ko avoid nahi karta, wo bilkul avoid karta hai; aur ye usko peculiar hai, kyunki pleasure ke excess ka alternative pain nahi hai, siwaye us aadmi ke liye jo is excess ko pursue karta hai.

Kyunki humein na sirf truth state karni chahiye, balki error ka cause bhi — kyunki ye conviction produce karne mein contribute karta hai, kyunki jab ek reasonable explanation di jaati hai ki kyun false view true lagta hai, ye true view mein belief produce karne ki tendency rakhta hai — isliye humein state karna chahiye kyun bodily pleasures zyada choice ka worthy lagti hain. (a) Pehla, to, ye isliye hai kyunki ye pain ko expel karti hain; pain ke excesses ki wajah se jo men experience karte hain, wo excessive aur generally bodily pleasure pursue karte hain us pain ke liye ek cure ke roop mein. Ab curative agencies intense feeling produce karte hain — jo reason hai wo pursue kiye jaane ka — kyunki wo contrary pain ke against show up karte hain. (Indeed pleasure in do reasons ke liye good nahi socha jaata, jaisa kaha gaya hai, namely, ki (α) inme se kuch activities hain jo ek bad nature ki belong karti hain — chahe congenital, jaise ek brute ke case mein, ya habit ki wajah se, yani bad men ki; jabki (μ) doosri ek defective nature ko cure karne ke liye meant hain, aur ek healthy state mein hona better hai isme aane se, lekin ye us process ke dauran arise hoti hain jab nature perfect banayi jaa rahi hoti hai aur isliye sirf incidentally good hain.) (b) Further, wo apni intensity ki wajah se pursue ki jaati hain un logo dwara jo doosri pleasures enjoy nahi kar sakte. (Sab surat mein wo apne raaste se hat kar apne liye somehow thirsts manufacture karte hain. Jab ye harmless hain, practice irreproachable hai; jab ye hurtful hain, ye bad hai.) Kyunki unke paas doosri koi cheez nahi hai enjoy karne ke liye aur, iske alawa, bahut se logo ke liye ek neutral state apni nature ki wajah se painful hai. Kyunki animal nature hamesha travail mein hai, jaisa natural science ke students bhi testify karte hain, kehte hue ki sight aur hearing painful hain; lekin hum ise use kar chuke hain, jaisa wo maintain karte hain. Similarly, jabki, youth mein, log, growth ki wajah se jo chal rahi hai, ek situation mein hain drunk men jaisi, aur youth pleasant hai, doosri taraf excitable nature ke log hamesha relief ki zaroorat rakhte hain; kyunki even unki body hamesha torment mein hai apni special composition ki wajah se, aur wo hamesha intense desire ke influence ke under hain; lekin pain contrary pleasure se driven out hota hai, aur kisi bhi chance pleasure se agar wo strong ho; aur in reasons ke liye wo self-indulgent aur bad ban jaate hain. Lekin pleasures jo pains involve nahi karti wo excess admit nahi karti; aur ye un cheezon mein hain jo nature se pleasant hain, incidentally nahi. Cheezon se jo incidentally pleasant hain mera matlab wo hain jo cures ki tarah act karti hain (kyunki kyunki result mein log cure hote hain, us part ki kisi action se jo healthy reh gaya hai, isi reason ke liye process pleasant lagta hai); cheezon se jo naturally pleasant hain mera matlab wo hain jo healthy nature ki action ko stimulate karti hain.

Koi ek cheez nahi hai jo hamesha pleasant hai, kyunki hamari nature simple nahi hai balki hum mein ek doosra element bhi hai, jahan tak hum perishable creatures hain, isliye agar ek element kuch karta hai, ye doosre nature ke liye unnatural hai, aur jab dono elements evenly balanced hain, jo kiya jaata hai wo na painful lagta hai na pleasant; kyunki agar kisi cheez ki nature simple hoti, wahi action hamesha usse sabse zyada pleasant hota. Isi wajah se god hamesha ek single aur simple pleasure enjoy karta hai; kyunki movement ki hi nahi balki immobility ki bhi ek activity hoti hai, aur pleasure movement se zyada rest mein paaya jaata hai. Lekin 'sab cheezon mein change sweet hai', jaisa poet kehta hai, kisi vice ki wajah se; kyunki jaise vicious aadmi changeable hota hai, waisi hi wo nature bhi hai jise change chahiye, vicious hai; kyunki ye na simple hai na good.

Humne ab discuss kar diya hai continence aur incontinence, aur pleasure aur pain, dono ki har ek kya hai aur kis sense mein kuch good hain aur doosre bad; reh jaata hai friendship ke baare mein baat karna.

---

# BOOK VIII · FRIENDSHIP (Dosti)

## Chapter 1 — Dosti zaroori bhi hai, noble (mahaan) bhi hai

Jo humne pehle discuss kiya uske baad, ab dosti (friendship) pe baat karna natural hai, kyunki dosti khud ek virtue (sadgun) hai ya virtue ko imply (sanket) karti hai, aur life jeene ke liye ye sabse zaroori cheez hai. Bina doston ke koi bhi insaan jeena choose nahi karega, chahe uske paas baaki sab kuch ho — dolat, samaan sab kuch. Yahan tak ki ameer log aur jo log power aur position mein hain, unhe bhi sabse zyada doston ki zaroorat hoti hai; kyunki aisi prosperity (khushaali) ka kya fayda agar beneficence (bhalai karna) karne ka mauka hi na ho — aur beneficence sabse zyada aur sabse laudable (sarahniya) form mein doston ke saath hi hoti hai. Ya phir doston ke bina prosperity ko guard (raksha) aur preserve (bacha ke rakhna) kaise kiya jaaye? Jitni zyada prosperity hai, utna zyada risk hai.

Gareebi aur doosri musibaton mein log sochte hain ki dost hi ek refuge (sahara) hain. Dosti jawano ko galtiyon se bachaati hai; buddho ki zaroorat poori karti hai aur unki kamzori ki wajah se jo activities weak ho rahi hoti hain unhe support karti hai; jo log life ke prime (bharpoor jawani) mein hain unhe noble actions ke liye stimulate (prerit) karti hai — kehte hain na "do log saath chalein to behtar" — kyunki doston ke saath insaan behtar soch aur kaam kar paata hai.

Phir, parents apne bacchon ke liye aur bacche apne parents ke liye naturally affection (pyaar) mehsoos karte hain, sirf insaano mein nahi balki pakshiyon aur zyadatar janwaron mein bhi. Ye feeling ek hi race/community ke logon mein mutually (dono taraf se) hoti hai, khaaskar insano mein — isliye hum apne fellow men (saathi manushyon) se pyaar karne walon ki tareef karte hain. Travel karte waqt bhi hum dekhte hain ki har insaan doosre insaan ke kitna kareeb aur pyaara hota hai.

Dosti states (rajyon) ko bhi jode rakhti hai, aur lawgivers (kanoon banane wale) justice se zyada dosti ki care karte hain; kyunki concord (aapsi mel) dosti jaisi hi cheez lagti hai, aur wahi sabse zyada chahte hain, aur faction (phoot/vibhajan) ko apna sabse bada dushman maankar bhagate hain. Jab log dost hote hain to unhe justice ki zaroorat nahi rehti, lekin jab log sirf just (nyaayi) hote hain to unhe dosti bhi chahiye hoti hai — aur justice ka sabse sacha roop ek friendly (dostana) quality hi maana jaata hai.

Lekin dosti sirf zaroori hi nahi, noble (mahaan/shreshth) bhi hai; hum unki tareef karte hain jo apne doston se pyaar karte hain, aur bahut saare dost hona ek achi baat maani jaati hai; aur hum ye bhi sochte hain ki jo good (achhe) log hote hain wahi asal mein dost hote hain.

Dosti ke baare mein bahut saari baatein debate (bahas) ka vishay hain. Kuch log ise ek tarah ki likeness (samaanta) maante hain aur kehte hain ki jaise log jaise logon ke dost hote hain — jahan se kahawatein aayi hain "like to like" (jaisa waisa), "Birds of a feather flock together" (ek jaise pankh wale panchi saath udte hain); iske ulat kuch log kehte hain "Two of a trade never agree" (ek hi dhande wale kabhi nahi milte). Isi sawaal par log aur bhi gehre aur physical (bhautik) causes (karan) dhoondte hain — Euripides ne kaha ki "sookhi zameen baarish se pyaar karti hai, aur baarish se bhara aasman zameen par girna chahta hai," aur Heraclitus ne kaha "jo virodh karta hai wahi madad karta hai" aur "alag-alag suron se hi sabse sundar taal banta hai" aur "sab cheezein strife (sangharsh) se paida hoti hain"; jabki Empedocles aur doosre log iske ulat kehte hain ki jaisa hi jaise ko chahta hai. Ye physical (bhautik) sawaal hum chhod dete hain kyunki wo humari present inquiry (abhi ki jaanch) ka hissa nahi hain; hum sirf unhi cheezon ko dekhenge jo human hain aur character (charitra) aur feeling (bhaavna) se juri hain — jaise, kya dosti kisi bhi do logon ke beech ho sakti hai, ya kya bure log dost nahi ban sakte, aur kya dosti ek hi species (prakaar) ki hai ya usse zyada. Jo log sochte hain ki sirf ek hi type hai kyunki ismein degrees (matrayen) hoti hain, unka indication (sanket) adequate (paryapt) nahi hai; kyunki alag species (prakaar) ki cheezon mein bhi degree ho sakti hai. Iske baare mein humne pehle discuss kar liya hai.

## Chapter 2 — Pyaar ke teen objects (vishay), aur dosti ka matlab kya hai

Dosti ke kinds (prakaar) shayad tab clear ho jaayenge jab hum pehle jaan lein ki pyaar ka object (vishay) kya hai. Kyunki har cheez loved (pyaari) nahi lagti, sirf lovable (pyaar ke laayak) cheez hi lagti hai, aur ye good (achhi), pleasant (sukhad), ya useful (upyogi) hoti hai; lekin jiske through koi good ya pleasure produce hota hai wo bhi useful hi kehlaayega — isliye asal mein good aur pleasant hi ends (antim uddeshya) ke roop mein lovable hain.

To kya log good ko pyaar karte hain, ya jo unke liye good hai use? Ye dono kabhi-kabhi clash (takra) jaate hain. Yahi baat pleasant ke saath bhi hai. Ab ye socha jaata hai ki har koi apne liye jo good hai use pyaar karta hai, aur good bina kisi qualification (shart) ke lovable hai, aur jo har insaan ke liye good hai wo uske liye lovable hai; lekin har insaan asal mein jo uske liye good hai use nahi, balki jo good lagta hai use pyaar karta hai. Isse koi fark nahi padta — hum bas ise "jo lovable lagta hai" keh denge.

Ab teen grounds (aadhar) hain jinpar log pyaar karte hain: nirjeev (lifeless) cheezon ke pyaar ko hum "friendship" nahi kehte, kyunki wahan mutual love (dono taraf ka pyaar) nahi hota, na hi doosre ke liye good chaahne wali baat hoti hai (kyunki wine (sharaab) ki bhalayi chaahna to ridiculous (hasyaaspad) hoga; agar koi uske liye kuch chahta hai to bas ye ki wo bani rahe, taaki khud use rakh sake) — lekin dost ke liye hum kehte hain ki humein uske khud ke liye good chaahna chahiye. Lekin jo log is tarah good chaahte hain unhe hum sirf goodwill (shubhkaamna) kehte hain, agar ye wish reciprocated (dono taraf se) nahi hai; jab goodwill mutual (dono taraf) ho tabhi wo friendship banti hai. Ya shayad humein ye bhi jodna chahiye "jab ye recognized (pehchaana gaya) ho"? Kyunki bahut se log un logon ke liye goodwill rakhte hain jinhe unhone dekha nahi hai lekin unhe good ya useful maante hain; aur inmein se koi ek is feeling ko return bhi kar sakta hai. Ye log ek-doosre ke liye goodwill rakhte lagte hain; lekin unhe dost kaise kaha jaaye jab unhe pata hi nahi ki doosra bhi waisa hi feel karta hai? Dost banne ke liye, unhe mutually recognized (dono taraf se pehchaana gaya) hona chahiye ki wo goodwill rakhte hain aur upar bataye gaye kisi karan se ek-doosre ka bhala chaahte hain.

## Chapter 3 — Dosti ke teen corresponding (sambandhit) kinds

Ye teeno reasons (karan) ek-doosre se kind (prakaar) mein alag hain; isliye pyaar aur dosti ke corresponding forms bhi alag hain. Isliye dosti ke teen kinds hain, utne hi jitni lovable cheezein hain; kyunki har ek ke respect (sandarbh) mein mutual aur recognized love hoti hai, aur jo log ek-doosre se pyaar karte hain wo us respect mein ek-doosre ka bhala chaahte hain jisme wo pyaar karte hain.

Ab jo log utility (upyogita/faayde) ki wajah se pyaar karte hain wo khud ke liye pyaar nahi karte balki us good ki wajah se jo unhe ek-doosre se milta hai. Yahi baat un logon ke saath bhi hai jo pleasure (sukh) ki wajah se pyaar karte hain; ready-witted (chatur/hazir-jawaab) logon se pyaar unke character (charitra) ki wajah se nahi hota, balki isliye kyunki wo pleasant lagte hain. Isliye jo log utility ki wajah se pyaar karte hain wo apne liye jo good hai uski wajah se karte hain, aur jo pleasure ki wajah se pyaar karte hain wo apne liye jo pleasant hai uski wajah se — aur wo pyaar us insaan ki wajah se nahi hota jo wo hai, balki isliye kyunki wo useful ya pleasant hai. Isliye ye friendships sirf incidental (aakasmik/gauna) hoti hain; kyunki loved person ko is roop mein pyaar nahi kiya jaata ki wo kaisa insaan hai, balki isliye ki wo kuch good ya pleasure de raha hai. Aisi friendships isliye aasani se toot jaati hain, agar dono parties waise nahi rehti jaisi wo thi; kyunki agar ek party ab pleasant ya useful nahi rahi to doosra usse pyaar karna chhod deta hai.

Ab useful cheez permanent (sthaayi) nahi hoti, wo hamesha badalti rehti hai. Isliye jab friendship ka reason khatam ho jaata hai, friendship bhi dissolve (khatam) ho jaati hai, kyunki wo sirf un ends (uddeshyon) ke liye exist karti thi. Is tarah ki friendship zyaadatar buddhe logon mein hoti hai (kyunki us age mein log pleasant nahi balki useful cheez ko pursue karte hain), aur jo log prime ya young age mein hain unme se bhi wo log jo utility pursue karte hain. Aise log ek-doosre ke saath zyaada time bhi nahi bitaate; kyunki kabhi-kabhi wo ek-doosre ko pleasant bhi nahi paate; isliye unhe aisi companionship (sangati) ki zaroorat nahi hoti jab tak wo ek-doosre ke liye useful na ho; wo ek-doosre ke liye tabhi pleasant hote hain jab tak wo ek-doosre mein kisi aane wale good ki umeed jagaate hain. Aisi friendships mein log host aur guest (mehmaan-nawaazi) ki friendship ko bhi rakhte hain.

Doosri taraf young logon ki friendship pleasure pe based lagti hai; kyunki wo emotion (bhaavna) ki guidance mein jeete hain, aur sabse zyada wahi cheez pursue karte hain jo unke liye abhi pleasant hai aur jo unke saamne hai; lekin badhti umar ke saath unke pleasures badal jaate hain. Isliye wo jaldi dost bante hain aur jaldi hi dost hona chhod dete hain; unki friendship us object (vishay) ke saath badalti rehti hai jo pleasant paaya jaata hai, aur aisa pleasure jaldi badal jaata hai. Young log amorous (prem-ras mein doobe) bhi hote hain; kyunki love ki friendship ka bada hissa emotion aur pleasure pe depend karta hai; isliye wo jaldi pyaar mein padte hain aur jaldi hi bahar aa jaate hain, ek hi din mein kai baar badal jaate hain. Lekin ye log apne din aur life saath bitaana chahte hain; kyunki isi tarah wo apni friendship ka purpose (uddeshya) achieve karte hain.

Perfect (sampoorn) friendship un logon ki hoti hai jo good hain, aur virtue (sadgun) mein ek jaise hain; kyunki ye log ek-doosre ka bhala usi tarah chaahte hain jaise wo good hain, aur wo khud good hain. Ab jo log apne doston ka bhala unke khud ke liye chaahte hain wo sabse zyada sacchey (truest) dost hote hain; kyunki wo aisa apne khud ke nature (swabhaav) ki wajah se karte hain, incidentally (sirf itthfaaq se) nahi; isliye unki friendship tab tak rehti hai jab tak wo good hain — aur goodness ek enduring (sthaayi) cheez hai. Aur har ek apne aap mein bhi good hota hai aur apne dost ke liye bhi, kyunki good log bina qualification ke good hote hain aur ek-doosre ke liye useful bhi. Isi tarah wo pleasant bhi hote hain; kyunki good log bina qualification ke bhi pleasant hote hain aur ek-doosre ke liye bhi, kyunki har insaan ke liye uski apni activities aur unke jaisi doosri activities pleasurable hoti hain, aur good logon ke actions same ya similar hote hain. Aisi friendship, jaisi expect ki jaani chahiye, permanent hoti hai, kyunki ismein wo saari qualities milti hain jo doston mein honi chahiye.

Kyunki har friendship good ya pleasure ki wajah se hoti hai — chahe wo abstract (nirakaar) roop mein ho ya us insaan ke liye jo friendly feeling rakhta hai — aur ek certain resemblance (samaanta) pe based hoti hai; aur good logon ki friendship mein wo saari qualities unki khud ki nature ki wajah se hoti hain; kyunki is tarah ki friendship mein doosri qualities bhi dono doston mein alike (samaan) hoti hain, aur jo bina qualification ke good hai wo bina qualification ke pleasant bhi hai, aur ye sabse lovable qualities hain. Isliye pyaar aur dosti sabse zyada aur sabse best form mein aise logon ke beech hi milte hain.

Lekin ye natural hai ki aisi friendships kam hi hoti hain; kyunki aise log rare (durlabh) hote hain. Iske alawa, aisi friendship ke liye time aur familiarity (parichay/ghulna-milna) chahiye hoti hai; jaise kahawat hai, log ek-doosre ko tab tak nahi jaan sakte jab tak unhone "saath namak na khaaya ho"; na hi wo ek-doosre ko friendship mein tab tak admit kar sakte hain jab tak har ek ne doosre ko lovable na paaya ho aur trust na kiya ho. Jo log jaldi hi ek-doosre ko friendship ke signs dikhaate hain wo dost banna chahte hain, lekin dost tab tak nahi hote jab tak dono lovable na ho aur ye fact na jaante ho; friendship ki wish (ichha) jaldi paida ho sakti hai, lekin friendship khud jaldi paida nahi hoti.

## Chapter 4 — Best aur inferior (kamtar) kinds ke beech contrast

Ye kind ki friendship, phir, duration (samay-avadhi) ke hisaab se bhi aur baaki sab tarah se bhi perfect hai, aur ismein har koi doosre se lagbhag wahi paata hai jo wo deta hai — jo doston ke beech hona bhi chahiye. Pleasure ki wajah se hone waali friendship iske resemblance (jaisi) hoti hai; kyunki good log bhi ek-doosre ke liye pleasant hote hain. Usi tarah utility waali friendship bhi; kyunki good log ek-doosre ke liye useful bhi hote hain. In inferior sorts (kamtar prakaar) ke logon mein bhi, friendships tab sabse zyada permanent hoti hain jab doston ko ek-doosre se same cheez milti hai (jaise pleasure), aur sirf wahi nahi balki same source (srot) se bhi — jaise ready-witted logon mein hota hai, na ki jaise lover aur beloved (prem karne wala aur pyaara) ke beech hota hai.

Kyunki inhe same cheezon mein pleasure nahi milta — ek ko beloved ko dekhne mein, aur doosre ko apne lover se attention (dhyaan) paane mein; aur jab jawani ka bloom (khilaav) beetne lagta hai to kabhi-kabhi friendship bhi khatam ho jaati hai (kyunki ek ko doosre ko dekhne mein koi pleasure nahi milta, aur doosre ko pehle waali attentions nahi milti); lekin bahut se lovers doosri taraf constant (sthir) bhi rehte hain, agar familiarity (ghulna-milna) ne unhe ek-doosre ke character se pyaar karwa diya ho jo alike (samaan) hain. Lekin jo log apne amour (prem-sambandh) mein pleasure nahi balki utility exchange karte hain wo dono kam sacche dost hote hain aur kam constant bhi. Jo log utility ki wajah se dost hain wo tab alag ho jaate hain jab advantage (faayda) khatam ho jaata hai; kyunki wo ek-doosre ke nahi, apne profit (munafa) ke lovers the.

Pleasure ya utility ki wajah se, bure log bhi ek-doosre ke dost ho sakte hain, ya good log bure logon ke, ya jo na good hai na bura wo kisi bhi tarah ke insaan ka dost ho sakta hai — lekin ye clear hai ki sirf good log hi khud ki wajah se dost ho sakte hain; kyunki bure log ek-doosre mein tab tak khush nahi hote jab tak koi advantage na ho.

Good logon ki friendship, aur sirf yahi, slander (bahtan/badnaami) se proof (surakshit) hoti hai; kyunki us insaan ke baare mein kisi ki baat pe trust karna aasan nahi hota jise humne khud lambe samay tak test kiya ho; aur good logon mein hi wo trust aur ye feeling milti hai ki "wo mujhe kabhi galat nahi karega" aur baaki wo sab cheezein jo true friendship mein zaroori hoti hain. Baaki tarah ki friendships mein aisi evils (buraiyaan) aane se kuch nahi rokta.

Log un logon ko bhi "friends" kehte hain jinka motive (uddeshya) utility hota hai, isi sense mein states (rajya) ko bhi friendly kaha jaata hai (kyunki states ke alliances advantage ke liye hote hain), aur un logon ko bhi jo pleasure ke liye ek-doosre se pyaar karte hain, jaise bacche friends kehlaate hain. Isliye humein bhi shayad aise logon ko friends kehna chahiye, aur ye kehna chahiye ki friendship ke kai kinds hain — sabse pehle aur proper sense mein good logon ki (jo good hone ki wajah se dost hain), aur resemblance (samaanta) ki wajah se baaki kinds; kyunki wo kisi good aur true friendship jaisi cheez ki wajah se dost hain, kyunki pleasure ke lovers ke liye bhi pleasant cheez good hi hoti hai. Lekin ye dono kinds of friendship aksar ek saath nahi milti, na hi same log utility aur pleasure dono ki wajah se dost banate hain; kyunki jo cheezein sirf incidentally connected hoti hain wo aksar saath nahi hoti.

Friendship ko in kinds mein baante hue, bure log pleasure ya utility ki wajah se dost honge, is respect mein ek-doosre jaise; lekin good log khud ki wajah se dost honge, yaani apni goodness ki wajah se. Ye log, phir, bina qualification ke friends hain; baaki log incidentally aur inse resemblance ki wajah se friends hain.

## Chapter 5 — Friendship ki "state" (avastha), "activity" (kriya), aur "feeling" (bhaavna) mein farak

Jaise virtues (sadgunon) ke maamle mein kuch log ek state of character (charitra ki avastha) ke hisaab se good kehlaate hain, aur kuch ek activity ke hisaab se, waise hi friendship ke maamle mein bhi hota hai; kyunki jo log saath rehte hain wo ek-doosre mein khushi paate hain aur ek-doosre ko benefit (fayda) dete hain, lekin jo log so rahe hain ya door hain wo friendship ki activities perform nahi kar rahe, balki unhe perform karne ke liye disposed (prawrit) hain; distance (doori) friendship ko poori tarah khatam nahi karti, sirf uski activity ko rokti hai. Lekin agar absence (door rehna) lambe samay tak rahe, to ye log actually apni friendship bhool jaate hain; isi liye kahawat hai "bahut si friendships baatcheet ki kami se toot jaati hain."

Na hi buddhe log, na hi sour (khatte-mizaaj/chidchide) log aasani se dost banate hain; kyunki unme pleasant cheez bahut kam hoti hai, aur koi bhi apne din us insaan ke saath nahi bita sakta jiski company painful (kashtdayak) ho, ya pleasant na ho, kyunki nature sabse zyada painful cheez se bachna aur pleasant cheez ki taraf jaana chahti hai. Jo log ek-doosre ko approve (pasand) karte hain lekin saath nahi rehte wo actual friends se zyada well disposed (achhi soch rakhne wale) lagte hain. Kyunki friends ke liye saath rehna sabse characteristic (khaas) baat hai (kyunki jo log zaroorat mein hain wo benefits chahte hain, lekin jo log supremely happy (poori tarah khush) hain wo bhi apne din saath bitaana chahte hain; kyunki solitude — akelapan — aise logon ke liye sabse kam suitable hota hai); lekin log saath tab hi reh sakte hain jab wo pleasant hon aur same cheezon mein enjoy karein, jaise companion (sathi) dost karte hain.

Sabse sacchi friendship, phir, good logon ki hoti hai, jaisa humne baar-baar kaha hai; kyunki jo bina qualification good ya pleasant hai wo lovable aur desirable (chaahne laayak) lagta hai, aur har insaan ke liye jo uske liye good ya pleasant hai wo bhi; aur good insaan good insaan ke liye in dono reasons se lovable aur desirable hota hai. Ab aisa lagta hai ki loving (pyaar karna) ek feeling hai, jabki friendship ek state of character hai; kyunki loving to nirjeev cheezon ke liye bhi utna hi feel ho sakta hai, lekin mutual love (dono taraf ka pyaar) mein choice (chunaav) shaamil hoti hai aur choice ek state of character se aati hai; aur log jinse pyaar karte hain unka bhala unke khud ke liye chaahte hain, feeling ke natije mein nahi balki apne character ki state ke natije mein. Aur ek dost se pyaar karte hue log wahi cheez pyaar karte hain jo unke khud ke liye good hai; kyunki good insaan dost bante hue apne dost ke liye khud ek good ban jaata hai. Har ek, phir, apne liye jo good hai use pyaar karta hai, aur goodwill aur pleasantness mein equal (barabar) return karta hai; kyunki friendship ko equality (samaanta) kaha jaata hai, aur ye dono cheezein good logon ki friendship mein sabse zyada paayi jaati hain.

## Chapter 6 — Teeno kinds ke beech various (vibhinn) relations

Sour (khatte-mizaaj) aur buddhe logon mein friendship kam aasani se banti hai, kyunki wo kam good-tempered (khush-mizaaj) hote hain aur companionship ka kam maza lete hain; kyunki ye cheezein friendship ki sabse badi nishaaniyan maani jaati hain aur ise sabse zyada paida karti hain. Isi wajah se, jahan young log jaldi dost bante hain, buddhe log nahi bante; kyunki log un logon ke dost nahi banate jinme unhe khushi nahi milti; aur waise hi sour log bhi jaldi dost nahi banate. Lekin aise log ek-doosre ke liye goodwill rakh sakte hain; kyunki wo ek-doosre ka bhala chaahte hain aur zaroorat mein madad karte hain; lekin wo mushkil se hi dost hote hain, kyunki wo apne din saath nahi bitaate ya ek-doosre mein khushi nahi paate, aur yahi cheezein friendship ki sabse badi nishaaniyan maani jaati hain.

Koi bhi insaan bahut saare logon ka dost nahi ho sakta us sense mein jismein unke saath perfect type ki friendship ho, jaise koi ek saath bahut se logon se pyaar mein nahi ho sakta (kyunki pyaar mein hona ek tarah ka excess of feeling — bhaavna ki adhikta — hai, aur aisi cheez naturally sirf ek hi insaan ke liye feel hoti hai); aur ye bhi aasan nahi hai ki bahut saare log ek hi samay mein same insaan ko itna zyada pasand aayein, ya shayad uski nazar mein achhe bhi lagein. Insaan ko doosre insaan ka kuch experience (anubhav) bhi lena padta hai aur uske saath familiar (parichit) hona padta hai, aur ye bahut mushkil hai. Lekin utility ya pleasure ke liye ye mumkin hai ki bahut saare log ek insaan ko pasand aayein; kyunki bahut saare log useful ya pleasant hote hain, aur ye services kam time lete hain.

In dono kinds mein se jo pleasure ki wajah se hoti hai wo friendship se zyada milti-julti hai, jab dono parties ek-doosre se same cheezein paate hain aur ek-doosre mein ya same cheezon mein khushi paate hain, jaise young logon ki friendships mein hota hai; kyunki aisi friendships mein generosity (udaardil-pan) zyada paayi jaati hai. Utility pe based friendship commercially-minded (vyaapaarik soch wale) logon ke liye hoti hai. Jo log supremely happy hote hain, unhe useful friends ki zaroorat nahi hoti, lekin pleasant friends ki zaroorat hoti hai; kyunki wo kisi ke saath rehna chahte hain aur, chahe wo thodi der ke liye painful cheez bardaasht kar sakein, koi bhi use continuously (lagatar) bardaasht nahi kar sakta, yahan tak ki Good (bhalayi) ko bhi nahi agar wo unke liye painful ho; isi liye wo pleasant friends dhoondte hain. Shayad unhe aise friends dhoondne chahiye jo pleasant hone ke saath-saath good bhi hon, aur unke liye good bhi hon; kyunki tab unme wo saari characteristics hongi jo friends mein honi chahiye.

Authority (satta) mein baithe log aksar do alag classes ke friends rakhte hain; kuch unke liye useful hote hain aur kuch pleasant, lekin same log shaayad hi dono hote hain; kyunki wo aise log nahi dhoondte jinki pleasantness virtue ke saath ho ya jinki utility noble (mahaan) uddeshyon ke liye ho, balki pleasure ki chaah mein wo ready-witted logon ko dhoondte hain, aur apne doosre friends ko unke aadesh maanne mein clever hone ki wajah se chunte hain, aur ye characteristics rarely combine hoti hain. Humne kaha hai ki good insaan ek saath pleasant bhi hota hai aur useful bhi; lekin aisa insaan apne se upar station (paad/hasiyat) waale ka dost tab tak nahi banta jab tak wo virtue mein bhi upar na ho; agar aisa nahi hai, to wo equality establish nahi karta, proportionally (anupaat mein) dono respects mein exceed hote hue. Lekin aise log jo dono respects mein exceed karte hon, unhe dhoondna itna aasan nahi hai.

Jo bhi ho, upar bataayi gayi friendships mein equality shaamil hoti hai; kyunki dost ek-doosre se same cheezein paate hain aur ek-doosre ke liye same cheezein chaahte hain, ya ek cheez ko doosri se exchange karte hain, jaise pleasure ko utility se; humne kaha hai, ki wo dono kam sacchi friendships hain aur kam permanent bhi. Lekin unki likeness (samaanta) aur unlikeness (asamaanta) usi cheez se hoti hai jiski wajah se unhe friendship samjha ya na samjha jaata hai. Wo virtue ki friendship se apni likeness ki wajah se friendships lagti hain (kyunki inmein se ek mein pleasure shaamil hai aur doosri mein utility, aur ye characteristics virtue ki friendship mein bhi milti hain); jabki isliye ki virtue ki friendship slander se proof aur permanent hoti hai, jabki ye jaldi badal jaati hain (aur bhi kai tarah se pehli se alag hoti hain), isliye ye friendships nahi lagti — yaani, virtue ki friendship se unki unlikeness ki wajah se.

## Chapter 7 — Unequal (asamaan) friendships mein proportion (anupaat) maintain karna zaroori hai

Lekin ek aur kind ki friendship hai, jismein dono parties ke beech inequality (asamaanta) shaamil hoti hai — jaise father aur son ke beech, aur generally bade aur chote ke beech, husband aur wife ke beech, aur generally ruler aur subject (shaasak aur praja) ke beech. Ye friendships ek-doosre se bhi alag hoti hain; kyunki parents aur children ke beech jo hota hai wo rulers aur subjects ke beech jaisa nahi hota, aur na hi father ka son ke prati wahi hota hai jo son ka father ke prati hota hai, na hi husband ka wife ke prati wahi hota hai jo wife ka husband ke prati hota hai. Kyunki inmein se har ek ki virtue aur function (kaam) alag hai, aur isliye jin reasons se wo pyaar karte hain wo bhi alag hain; isliye pyaar aur friendship bhi alag hoti hai.

Har party, phir, na doosre se same paata hai, na hi paana chahiye; lekin jab bacche apne parents ko wahi dete hain jo unhe un logon ko dena chahiye jinhone unhe duniya mein laaya, aur parents apne bacchon ko wahi dete hain jo unhe dena chahiye, to aise logon ki friendship abiding (sthaayi) aur excellent (utkrisht) hogi. Inequality waali sab friendships mein pyaar bhi proportional (anupaatik) hona chahiye — yaani, jo behtar hai use zyaada pyaar milna chahiye jitna wo khud pyaar karta hai, aur waise hi jo zyaada useful hai use bhi; aur baaki cases mein bhi waise hi; kyunki jab pyaar parties ke merit (yogyata) ke anupaat mein hota hai, tab ek tarah ki equality aati hai, jo friendship ki characteristic maani jaati hai.

Lekin equality justice ke acts (karyon) mein aur friendship mein same form nahi leti; kyunki justice ke acts mein jo primary sense mein equal hai wo hai jo merit ke anupaat mein hai, jabki quantitative (matraatmak) equality secondary hai; lekin friendship mein quantitative equality primary hai aur merit ke anupaat wali equality secondary. Ye tab clear hota hai jab parties ke beech virtue ya vice (bura swabhaav) ya wealth (dolat) ya kisi aur cheez mein bada interval (antar) ho; kyunki tab wo ab dost nahi rehte, aur dost banne ki expect bhi nahi karte. Ye sabse zyada gods (devताओं) ke case mein manifest (spasht) hota hai; kyunki wo humse har good cheez mein decisively (poori tarah) upar hain. Lekin ye kings (raajaon) ke case mein bhi clear hai; kyunki unke saath bhi, jo log unse bahut inferior (kamtar) hain wo unke dost banne ki expect nahi karte; na hi bekaar log best ya sabse wise logon ke dost banne ki expect karte hain. Aise cases mein exactly define nahi kiya ja sakta ki kis point tak friends dost reh sakte hain; kyunki bahut kuch chhin sakta hai aur friendship phir bhi reh sakti hai, lekin jab ek party bahut door chali jaaye, jaise god hai, to friendship ki possibility hi khatam ho jaati hai. Yahi isliye ye sawaal uthta hai ki kya dost apne doston ke liye sach mein sabse badi cheezein chaahte hain, jaise gods bann jaana; kyunki tab unke dost ab unke dost nahi rahenge, aur isliye unke liye good things nahi rahenge (kyunki dost hi good things hote hain). Jawaab ye hai ki agar hum sahi the jab humne kaha ki dost apne dost ka bhala uske khud ke liye chaahta hai, to uska dost jaisa bhi hai wahi rehna chahiye; isliye jab tak wo insaan hi rehta hai tab tak hi wo uske liye sabse badi cheezein chaahega. Lekin shayad sab sabse badi cheezein nahi; kyunki har insaan sabse zyada khud ke liye hi good chaahta hai.

## Chapter 8 — Pyaar karna, pyaar paane se zyaada friendship ka asal saar hai

Zyaadatar log, honour (samman/izzat) ke pyaar ki wajah se, pyaar paana chahte hain na ki pyaar karna; isi liye zyaadatar log flattery (khushaamad) se pyaar karte hain; kyunki flatterer (khushaamadi) ek inferior position mein friend hota hai, ya aisa hone ka dikhaawa karta hai, aur jitna use pyaar milta hai usse zyaada pyaar karne ka natak karta hai — aur pyaar paana honour paane jaisa lagta hai, aur yahi zyaadatar log chahte hain. Lekin lagta hai ki log honour ko uski khud ki wajah se nahi chunte, balki incidentally (aksmik roop se). Kyunki zyaadatar log authority mein baithe logon se honour paakar apni hopes (ummeedon) ki wajah se khush hote hain (kyunki wo sochte hain ki agar unhe kuch chahiye to wo un logon se mil jaayega; isliye wo honour ko aane waale favour (kripa) ka token (nishaani) maankar khush hote hain); jabki jo log good aur samajhdar logon se honour chahte hain wo apni khud ki opinion (raay) khud ke baare mein confirm karna chahte hain; wo isliye honour se khush hote hain kyunki unhe apni goodness pe yakeen hota hai un logon ke judgement (faisle) ki strength (mazbooti) se jo unke baare mein baat karte hain.

Pyaar paane mein, doosri taraf, log iski khud ki wajah se khush hote hain; isliye ye honour paane se behtar lagta hai, aur friendship khud mein desirable (chaahne laayak) lagti hai. Lekin ye pyaar karne mein zyaada hai, pyaar paane mein kam, jaisa maaon ke pyaar karne ke delight (anand) se pata chalta hai; kyunki kuch maaein apne bacchon ko paalne ke liye kisi aur ko de deti hain, aur jab tak unhe unka fate (bhaagya) pata rehta hai wo unse pyaar karti hain aur badle mein pyaar paane ki koshish nahi karti (agar dono na mil sakein), balki khush lagti hain agar wo dekhein ki unke bacche prosper (unnati) kar rahe hain; aur wo khud apne bacchon se pyaar karti hain chahe wo apni ignorance (anjaan-pan) ki wajah se unhe ek maa ka haq kuch bhi na dein.

Ab kyunki friendship zyaada loving (pyaar karne) pe depend karti hai, aur jo log apne doston se pyaar karte hain unhi ki tareef ki jaati hai, isliye loving hi friends ki characteristic virtue lagti hai, isliye sirf wahi log lasting (sthaayi) friends hote hain jinme ye sahi matra mein paayi jaati hai, aur sirf unki hi friendship endure (tikti) hai.

Isi tarah se, kisi aur tarike se zyaada, unequal log bhi dost ban sakte hain; unhe equalize (barabar) kiya ja sakta hai. Ab equality aur likeness hi friendship hai, khaaskar un logon ki likeness jo virtue mein alike hain; kyunki khud mein steadfast (drishtiman/sthir) hote hue wo ek-doosre se bhi jude rehte hain, aur na hi base (neech) services maangte hain na dete hain, balki (ye keh sakte hain) unhe rokte bhi hain; kyunki good logon ki khaasiyat yahi hai ki na wo khud galat karte hain na apne doston ko karne dete hain. Lekin bure logon mein koi steadfastness (sthirta) nahi hoti (kyunki wo khud bhi ek jaise nahi rehte), lekin thodi der ke liye dost ban jaate hain kyunki wo ek-doosre ki wickedness (buraayi) mein khush hote hain. Jo friends useful ya pleasant hote hain wo zyaada der tak rehte hain — jab tak wo ek-doosre ko enjoyments (anand) ya advantages dete rehte hain.

Utility ke liye friendship shaayad sabse aasani se contraries (viruddh cheezon) ke beech hoti hai, jaise gareeb aur ameer ke beech, anpadh aur padhe-likhe ke beech; kyunki jo cheez insaan ke paas nahi hai wahi wo chaahta hai, aur ek badle mein kuch aur deta hai. Lekin isi category mein lover aur beloved, khoobsurat aur badsoorat bhi aa sakte hain. Isi liye lovers kabhi-kabhi ridiculous (hasyaaspad) lagte hain, jab wo utna hi pyaar paana chahte hain jitna wo karte hain; agar wo equally lovable hain to unka claim shayad justified (uचित) ho sakta hai, lekin jab unme kuch bhi lovable nahi hota to ye ridiculous hota hai. Shayad, halaanki, contrary apni nature se contrary ko nahi chahta, balki sirf incidentally, aur desire asal mein us intermediate (madhya) state ke liye hoti hai; kyunki wahi good hai — jaise dry (sookhi) cheez ke liye good ye nahi ki wo wet (geeli) ho jaaye balki intermediate state mein aa jaaye, aur waise hi hot (garam) ke saath bhi. Ye subjects hum chhod dete hain; kyunki ye humari inquiry se somewhat (kuch hadd tak) foreign (alag) hain.

## Chapter 9 — Dosti aur justice ka parallelism (samaantarta): state sab chhoti communities ko samet leta hai (encapsulate)

Friendship aur justice, jaisa humne shuru mein kaha tha, ek hi objects se related lagte hain aur same persons ke beech dikhte hain. Kyunki har community (samudaay) mein justice ka koi na koi form hota hai maana jaata hai, aur friendship bhi; kam se kam log apne fellow voyagers (saath-yatriyon) aur fellow soldiers (saathi sipahiyon) ko friends kehke address karte hain, aur waise hi kisi bhi doosri tarah ki community mein associated logon ko bhi. Aur unki association (judaav) ka extent (vistaar) hi unki friendship ka extent hota hai, jaise unke beech justice ka extent hota hai. Aur kahawat "jo doston ka hai wo common property (saanjhi sampatti) hai" sach batati hai; kyunki friendship community pe depend karti hai.

Ab bhai aur comrades (saathi) sab cheezein common rakhte hain, lekin baaki jinka humne zikr kiya unke paas definite (nishchit) cheezein common hoti hain — kuch ke paas zyaada, kuch ke paas kam; kyunki friendships mein bhi kuch zyaada aur kuch kam truly friendships hoti hain. Aur justice ke claims (daave) bhi alag hote hain; parents ka children ke prati duty (kartavya) aur bhaion ka ek-doosre ke prati duty same nahi hote, na hi comrades aur fellow citizens (saathi nagrikon) ke, aur waise hi baaki kinds of friendship mein bhi. Isliye in har class ke associates ke prati unjust (anyaaypoorna) acts mein bhi farak hota hai, aur injustice (anyaay) badhti hai jab wo un logon ke prati ki jaaye jo fuller sense (poore roop) mein dost hain; jaise, ek comrade ko dhokha dena ek fellow citizen ko dhokha dene se zyaada terrible (bhayanak) hai, ek bhai ki madad na karna ek ajnabi ki madad na karne se zyaada terrible hai, aur father ko chot pahunchana kisi aur ko chot pahunchane se zyaada terrible hai. Aur justice ki demands (maang) bhi friendship ki intensity (tivrata) ke saath badhti lagti hain, jisse pata chalta hai ki friendship aur justice same logon ke beech exist karte hain aur unka extension (vistaar) barabar hai.

Ab community ke sab forms political community (rajnaitik samudaay) ke parts jaise hain; kyunki log kisi particular advantage ki khoj mein saath yatra karte hain, aur life ke liye jo unhe chahiye wo provide karne ke liye; aur advantage ke liye hi political community bhi originally saath aayi hai aur endure (tiki) hui hai, kyunki yahi legislators (kanoon-banane wale) chahte hain, aur wo usi ko just (nyaayi) kehte hain jo common advantage ke liye ho. Baaki communities bit by bit (thoda-thoda) advantage chahti hain — jaise sailors (naaviq) safar mein jo advantageous hai use chahte hain, paise kamaane ya kisi aisi cheez ke liye; fellow soldiers war mein jo advantageous hai use chahte hain, chahe wo wealth ho ya victory (jeet) ya kisi city ko lena; aur tribe aur deme (chhote samudaay) ke members bhi waise hi karte hain. [Kuch communities pleasure ke liye bhi banti lagti hain, jaise religious guilds (dharmik sangathan) aur social clubs; kyunki ye respectively sacrifice (bali/pooja) chadhaane aur companionship ke liye exist karte hain. Lekin ye sab political community ke andar hi aate hain; kyunki wo present advantage nahi balki poori life ke liye jo advantageous hai uska lakshya rakhti hai] — sacrifices chadhaate hue aur gatherings (jamaawad) karte hue is purpose ke liye, aur gods ko honours dete hue, aur khud ke liye pleasant relaxations (aaraam) provide karte hue. Kyunki ancient (praachin) sacrifices aur gatherings harvest (fasal) ke baad first fruits (pehli upaj) ke roop mein hoti thi, kyunki usi season mein logon ke paas sabse zyaada leisure (fursat) hota tha. Sab communities, phir, political community ke parts lagti hain; aur particular kinds of friendship particular kinds of community se correspond (mel khaayenge) karengi.

## Chapter 10 — Constitutions (shaasan-vyavastha) ka classification: family relations ke saath analogies (samaanta)

Teen kinds ki constitution hain, aur utni hi deviation forms (bhatki hui roop) — jaise unke perversions (bigde hue roop). Constitutions hain: monarchy (raajtantra), aristocracy (kuleentantra), aur teesri wo jo property qualification (sampatti-yogyata) pe based hai, jise timocratic kehna appropriate lagta hai, halaanki zyaadatar log ise polity kehte hain. Inmein sabse best monarchy hai, sabse worst timocracy. Monarchy se deviation tyranny (atyaachaari shaasan) hai; kyunki dono hi one-man rule (ek insaan ka raj) ke forms hain, lekin dono mein bahut bada farak hai: tyrant (atyaachari) apne khud ke advantage ko dekhta hai, king (raja) apni subjects (praja) ke advantage ko. Kyunki koi insaan tab tak king nahi hota jab tak wo khud-nirbhar na ho aur har good cheez mein apni subjects se aage na ho; aur aise insaan ko kuch aur chahiye hi nahi hota; isliye wo apne interests ko nahi, apni subjects ke interests ko dekhega; kyunki jo king aisa nahi hota wo bas titular (naam-maatra) king hota hai. Ab tyranny iska bilkul ulta hai; tyrant apna khud ka good pursue karta hai. Aur tyranny ke case mein ye zyaada clear hai ki ye worst deviation-form hai; lekin best ka contrary hi worst hota hai.

Monarchy tyranny mein badal jaati hai; kyunki tyranny one-man rule ka evil (bura) form hai aur bura king tyrant ban jaata hai. Aristocracy oligarchy (mutthi-bhar logon ka shaasan) mein badal jaati hai rulers ki badness (buraayi) ki wajah se, jo city ki cheezein equity (nyaay-sangat tareeke) ke against baantte hain — saari ya zyaadatar good cheezein khud ko, aur office hamesha same logon ko, wealth ko sabse zyaada mehatva dete hue; isliye rulers kam ho jaate hain aur worthy (yogya) logon ki jagah bure log ban jaate hain. Timocracy democracy (loktantra) mein badal jaati hai; kyunki ye dono coterminous (ek-doosre ke saath judi) hain, kyunki timocracy ka bhi ideal yahi hai ki majority (bahumat) ka raj ho, aur jinke paas property qualification hai wo sab equal maane jaate hain. Democracy deviations mein sabse kam bad hai; kyunki iska form of constitution sirf ek slight deviation hai. Ye hi wo changes hain jinke liye constitutions sabse zyada subject (prone) hain; kyunki ye sabse smallest aur easiest transitions hain.

Insaan constitutions ki resemblance aur unke patterns households (ghar-parivaar) mein bhi paa sakta hai. Ek father ka apne sons ke saath association monarchy ka form leta hai, kyunki father apne bacchon ki care karta hai; isi liye Homer Zeus ko 'father' kehta hai; monarchy ka ideal hi paternal rule (pitratv-shaasan) hona hai. Lekin Persians ke beech father ka rule tyrannical (atyaachaari) hota hai; wo apne sons ko slaves (daas) ki tarah use karte hain. Tyrannical bhi hai master (maalik) ka slaves par rule; kyunki ismein master ka advantage hi laaya jaata hai. Ab ye ek correct form of government lagta hai, lekin Persian type perverted (bigda hua) hai; kyunki alag-alag relations ke liye appropriate rule ke modes (tareeke) alag hote hain. Man aur wife ki association aristocratic lagti hai; kyunki man apni worth (yogyata) ke anusaar rule karta hai, aur un maamlon mein jinme ek man ko rule karna chahiye, lekin jo maamle ek woman ke liye befit (uchit) hain wo unhe hand over kar deta hai. Agar man har cheez mein rule karta hai to relation oligarchy mein badal jaati hai; kyunki aisa karte hue wo apni respective worth ke anusaar act nahi kar raha, aur apni superiority ki wajah se rule nahi kar raha. Kabhi-kabhi, halaanki, women rule karti hain, kyunki wo heiresses (uttaraadhikaarini) hoti hain; isliye unka rule excellence (guṇ) ki wajah se nahi balki wealth aur power ki wajah se hota hai, jaise oligarchies mein. Bhaion ki association timocracy jaisi hai; kyunki wo equal hain, sirf age mein farak ke alawa; isliye agar unki age mein bahut farak ho, to friendship ab fraternal (bhrataritva) type ki nahi rehti. Democracy zyaadatar masterless dwellings (bina maalik ke gharon) mein paayi jaati hai (kyunki yahan sab equal hote hain), aur un gharon mein jahan ruler kamzor hai aur har koi jo chahe wo karne ki licence (chhoot) rakhta hai.

## Chapter 11 — Friendship aur justice ke corresponding forms

Har constitution mein utni hi friendship dekhi ja sakti hai jitni usme justice hai. King aur uski subjects ke beech friendship benefits (fayde) ki ek excess (adhikta) pe depend karti hai; kyunki wo apni subjects ko benefits deta hai agar good insaan hote hue wo unki well-being (bhalayi) ki care karta hai, jaise ek shepherd (gadariya) apni sheep (bhed) ki karta hai (isi liye Homer ne Agamemnon ko 'shepherd of the peoples' kaha). Aisi hi father ki friendship hai, halaanki ye conferred benefits ki greatness (mahaanta) mein doosre se aage nikal jaati hai; kyunki wo apne bacchon ke existence (astitva) ke liye responsible hai, jo sabse bada good maana jaata hai, aur unki nurture (paalan-poshan) aur upbringing (parvarish) ke liye bhi. Ye cheezein ancestors (poorvajon) ko bhi ascribe (attributed) ki jaati hain. Iske alawa, nature se father apne sons pe rule karta hai, ancestors apne descendants (vanshajon) pe, aur king apni subjects pe. Ye friendships ek party ki doosri pe superiority (shreshtata) implyi karti hain, isi liye ancestors ki honour ki jaati hai. Isliye in relations mein jo justice hoti hai wo dono taraf same nahi hoti, balki har case mein merit ke anupaat mein hoti hai; kyunki yahi baat friendship ke liye bhi sach hai. Man aur wife ki friendship, phir, wahi hoti hai jo aristocracy mein paayi jaati hai; kyunki ye virtue ke anusaar hoti hai — behtar ko zyaada good milta hai, aur har ek ko wahi milta hai jo use befit (shobha deta) hai; aur waise hi in relations mein justice bhi. Bhaion ki friendship comrades jaisi hoti hai; kyunki wo equal hain aur same age ke, aur aise log zyaadatar apne feelings aur character mein bhi ek jaise hote hain. Isi jaisi hai timocratic government ke liye appropriate friendship bhi; kyunki aisi constitution mein ideal yahi hai ki citizens equal aur fair (nyaaysangat) hon; isliye rule turn (baari-baari) mein aur equal terms pe liya jaata hai; aur yahan ki friendship bhi isi se correspond karegi.

Lekin deviation-forms mein, jaise justice mushkil se hi exist karti hai, waise hi friendship bhi. Ye worst form mein sabse kam paayi jaati hai: tyranny mein friendship bahut kam ya bilkul nahi hoti. Kyunki jahan ruler aur ruled (shaasit) ke beech kuch bhi common nahi hota, wahan friendship bhi nahi hoti, kyunki justice nahi hoti; jaise craftsman (kaarigar) aur tool (upkaran) ke beech, soul (aatma) aur body (sharir) ke beech, master aur slave ke beech; har case mein baad wala (latter) us se benefit paata hai jo use use karta hai, lekin lifeless (nirjeev) cheezon ke prati koi friendship ya justice nahi hoti. Lekin horse (ghoda) ya ox (bail) ke prati bhi friendship nahi hoti, na hi slave ke prati jab wo sirf slave ho. Kyunki dono parties mein kuch bhi common nahi hota; slave ek living tool (jeevit upkaran) hai aur tool ek lifeless slave. Slave ki tarah, phir, koi uska dost nahi ban sakta. Lekin man ki tarah ban sakta hai; kyunki kisi bhi do manushyon ke beech kuch justice lagti hai jo kisi legal system mein share kar sakte hain ya kisi agreement ka part ban sakte hain; isliye uske saath friendship bhi ho sakti hai jitna wo ek man hai. Isliye jahan tyrannies mein friendship aur justice mushkil se hoti hain, wahin democracies mein wo zyaada poori tarah se hoti hain; kyunki jahan citizens equal hote hain unke paas bahut kuch common hota hai.

## Chapter 12 — Rishtedaaron ke beech friendship ke various forms

Har form of friendship, phir, association (judaav) shaamil karti hai, jaisa kaha ja chuka hai. Halaanki baaki se alag rakha ja sakta hai — kindred (rishtedaar) ki friendship aur comrades ki friendship. Fellow citizens, fellow tribesmen (samaan-kabile ke log), fellow voyagers, aur inke jaise log mere friendships of association (sangati ki dosti) jaise zyaada lagte hain; kyunki wo ek tarah ke compact (samjhaute) pe based lagte hain. Inke saath host aur guest ki friendship bhi rakhi ja sakti hai.

Rishtedaaron ki friendship khud, halaanki wo kai kinds ki lagti hai, har case mein parental friendship (maata-pita ki dosti) pe depend karti lagti hai; kyunki parents apne bacchon se pyaar karte hain kyunki wo unka hi ek hissa hain, aur bacche apne parents se pyaar karte hain kyunki wo khud unse originate (utpann) hue hain. Ab (1) parents apni offspring (santaan) ko unse zyaada jaante hain jitna bacche jaante hain ki wo unke bacche hain, aur (2) originator (janmadaata) apni offspring ko khud se zyaada apna feel karta hai jitna offspring apne begetter (janamdaata) ko; kyunki product (utpaad) producer (nirmaata) ka hota hai (jaise ek daant ya baal ya kuch bhi jiska bhi wo hai), lekin producer product ka nahi hota, ya kam degree mein hota hai. Aur (3) time ki length bhi yahi result deti hai; parents apne bacchon se pyaar karte hain jaise hi wo paida hote hain, lekin bacche apne parents se pyaar tab karte hain jab time beet jaaye aur unhone understanding (samajh) ya senses se discrimination (bhed karne ki shakti) haasil kar li ho.

In considerations se ye bhi clear hota hai ki maaein fathers se zyaada kyun pyaar karti hain. Parents, phir, apne bacchon se khud jaisa pyaar karte hain (kyunki unki issue — santaan — unke apne separate existence ki wajah se ek tarah ka other self — doosra khud — hai), jabki bacche apne parents se pyaar isliye karte hain kyunki wo unse janme hain, aur brothers ek-doosre se isliye pyaar karte hain kyunki wo same parents se janme hain; kyunki unki identity (pehchaan) unse hi unhe ek-doosre ke saath bhi identical (ek-samaan) banaati hai (isi liye log 'same blood' aur 'same stock' jaisi baatein karte hain). Wo, isliye, ek sense mein same cheez hain, halaanki separate individuals mein.

Do cheezein friendship mein bahut contribute karti hain: ek common upbringing aur age ki similarity; kyunki 'do samaan age ke log ek-doosre ki taraf khinchte hain', aur saath badhe hue log comrades bante hain; isi liye bhaion ki friendship comrades ki friendship se akin (milti-julti) hai. Aur cousins aur baaki rishtedaar bhaion se derivation (utpatti) ki wajah se bandhe hote hain, yaani same parents se derived hone ki wajah se. Wo ek-doosre se zyaada kareeb ya zyaada door hote hain original ancestor ki nearness (nikatta) ya distance (doori) ki wajah se.
