Bacchon ki parents ke prati, aur manushyon ki gods ke prati, friendship unke prati ek relation hai jo kisi good aur superior (shreshtha) cheez ke prati hoti hai; kyunki unhone sabse bade benefits diye hain, kyunki wo unke astitva ke, unke poshan ke, aur unki education ke unke janam se hi causes (karan) hain; aur is kind ki friendship mein pleasantness aur utility bhi hoti hai, ajnabiyon se zyaada, kyunki unki life zyaada common (saanjha) hoti hai. Bhaion ki friendship mein comrades jaisi characteristics hoti hain (khaaskar jab wo good hon), aur generally un logon ke beech jo ek-doosre jaise hain, kyunki wo ek-doosre se zyaada belong karte hain aur apne janam se hi ek-doosre ke liye pyaar se shuru karte hain, aur kyunki jo same parents se paida hue aur saath badhe aur similarly educate hue wo character mein zyaada akin hote hain; aur time ka test unke case mein sabse fully aur convincingly apply hua hota hai.

Baaki rishtedaaron ke beech friendly relations due proportion (उचित anupaat) mein paayi jaati hain. Man aur wife ke beech friendship nature se exist karti lagti hai; kyunki man naturally couples (jode) banaane ki taraf inclined (jhukav) hai — cities banaane se bhi zyaada, kyunki household (parivaar) city se pehle aur zyaada necessary hai, aur reproduction (santaan-utpatti) man ko animals ke saath zyaada common hai. Baaki animals mein union (mel) sirf isi point tak extend karta hai, lekin human beings sirf reproduction ke liye hi nahi balki life ke various purposes ke liye bhi saath rehte hain; kyunki shuru se hi functions (kaam) divided hote hain, aur man aur woman ke alag hote hain; isliye wo apne peculiar (khaas) gifts common stock mein daal ke ek-doosre ki madad karte hain. Isi wajah se is kind ki friendship mein utility aur pleasure dono paaye jaate hain. Lekin ye friendship virtue pe bhi based ho sakti hai, agar dono parties good hon; kyunki har ek ki apni virtue hoti hai aur wo isi fact mein delight lenge. Aur bacche bhi ek bond of union (mel ka bandhan) lagte hain (isi liye childless — nissantan — log jaldi alag ho jaate hain); kyunki bacche dono ke liye ek common good hote hain aur jo common hota hai wo unhe jode rakhta hai.

Man aur wife, aur generally friend aur friend, ko ek-doosre ke saath kaise behave karna chahiye — ye wahi sawaal lagta hai ki unke liye just (nyaaysangat) kya hai; kyunki ek insaan ka duty ek friend, ek stranger (ajnabi), ek comrade, aur ek schoolfellow (sahpaathi) ke prati same nahi lagta.

## Chapter 13 — Equals ke beech friendship mein observe kiye jaane waale principles (siddhaant)

Friendship ke teen kinds hain, jaisa humne apni inquiry ki shuruaat mein kaha tha, aur har ek mein kuch log equality (samaanta) ke aadhar pe dost hote hain aur kuch superiority (shreshtata) ke aadhar pe (kyunki sirf equally good log hi dost nahi bante, balki ek behtar insaan bhi ek kamtar insaan se dost ban sakta hai, aur waise hi pleasure ya utility ki friendships mein bhi friends benefits mein equal ya unequal ho sakte hain jo wo ek-doosre ko dete hain). Isliye equals ko love aur baaki sab respects mein equality ke aadhar par required equalization (avashyak samaanikaran) karna chahiye, jabki unequals ko apni superiority ya inferiority ke anupaat mein dena chahiye.

Complaints (shikaayatein) aur reproaches (uljhanien/dosarop) sirf ya mainly utility ki friendship mein hoti hain, aur ye expect kiya jaana chahiye. Kyunki jo log virtue ke aadhar pe dost hain wo ek-doosre ka bhala karne ke liye anxious (utsuk) hote hain (kyunki yahi virtue aur friendship ki nishaani hai), aur jo log isme ek-doosre se emulate (barabari) kar rahe hain unke beech complaints ya jhagde nahi ho sakte; koi bhi us insaan se offended (naaraaz) nahi hota jo use pyaar karta hai aur uska bhala karta hai — agar wo nice feeling (achhi bhaavna) ka insaan hai to wo apna revenge (badla) doosre ka bhala karke leta hai. Aur jo insaan doosre se services (seva) dene mein aage nikal jaata hai wo apne friend ki complain nahi karega, kyunki use wahi milta hai jo wo chahta hai; kyunki har insaan good hi chahta hai. Complaints pleasure ki friendships mein bhi zyaada nahi hoti; kyunki dono ko ek hi samay mein wo milta hai jo wo chahte hain, agar unhe saath samay bitaana achha lagta hai; aur ek insaan jo doosre se complain kare ki wo use pleasure nahi de raha wo ridiculous lagega, kyunki uske paas power hai ki wo uske saath din na bitaaye.

Lekin utility ki friendship complaints se bhari hoti hai; kyunki jab wo ek-doosre ko apne interests ke liye use karte hain wo hamesha bargain (sauda) mein aage nikalna chahte hain, aur sochte hain ki unhe jitna milna chahiye tha usse kam mila hai, aur apne partners ko blame karte hain kyunki unhe wo sab kuch nahi milta jo wo "chahte aur deserve karte hain"; aur jo log doosron ka bhala karte hain wo utna nahi kar paate jitna jinka bhala kar rahe hain wo chahte hain.

Ab lagta hai ki jaise justice do kinds ki hoti hai, ek unwritten (alikhit) aur doosri legal (kaanooni), waise hi utility ki friendship ka bhi ek kind moral (naitik) hota hai aur doosra legal. Aur isliye complaints sabse zyaada tab hoti hain jab log relation ko usi type ki friendship ki spirit (bhaavna) mein dissolve nahi karte jismein unhone use contract kiya tha. Legal type wo hai jo fixed terms (nishchit sharton) pe hoti hai; iski purely commercial (poori tarah vyaapaarik) variety immediate payment (turant bhugtaan) ke aadhar pe hoti hai, jabki zyaada liberal (udaar) variety time deti hai lekin ek definite quid pro quo (ek cheez ke badle doosri cheez) ki maang karti hai. Is variety mein debt (karz) clear aur ambiguous (aspasht) nahi hota, lekin postponement (der karna) mein ek element of friendliness (dostana tatva) hota hai; isliye kuch states aise agreements se uthne waale suits (mukadme) allow nahi karte, balki sochte hain ki jinhone credit (udhaar) ke aadhar pe bargain kiya hai unhe consequences (parinaam) accept karne chahiye.

Moral type fixed terms pe nahi hoti; wo ek gift deti hai, ya jo bhi karti hai wo ek friend ki tarah karti hai; lekin ek expect karta hai ki utna hi ya usse zyaada wapas mile, kyunki usne diya nahi tha balki lend (udhaar) kiya tha; aur agar insaan relation dissolve hone par pehle se worse off (bura haal) hai jitna wo contract hone ke waqt tha to wo complain karega. Ye isliye hota hai kyunki sab ya zyaadatar log, jabki wo noble cheez chahte hain, actually advantageous cheez ko choose karte hain; ab doosre ka bhala repayment (wapasi) ki expectation ke bina karna noble hai, lekin benefits paana advantageous hai.

Isliye agar hum kar sakein to humein jo mila hai uska equivalent (barabar) return karna chahiye (kyunki humein kisi insaan ko uski marzi ke khilaaf apna friend nahi banaana chahiye; humein recognize karna chahiye ki hum shuru mein galat the aur humne us insaan se benefit liya jisse humein nahi lena chahiye tha — kyunki wo friend ki taraf se nahi tha, na hi kisi aise insaan ki taraf se jisne sirf iske liye kiya ho — aur humein waise hi settle up karna chahiye jaise humein fixed terms pe benefit mila ho). Sach mein, koi bhi agar kar sake to repay karne ko agree karega (agar wo na kar sake, to giver — dene wala — bhi expect nahi karega ki wo aisa kare); isliye agar possible hai to humein repay karna chahiye. Lekin shuru mein humein us insaan ko consider karna chahiye jisse humein benefit mil raha hai aur wo kin terms pe act kar raha hai, taaki hum in terms pe benefit accept karein, ya use decline (mana) kar dein.

Ye disputable (vivaadit) hai ki kya humein ek service ko uski utility receiver (praapt karne wale) ke liye measure karni chahiye aur usi ke hisaab se return karna chahiye, ya giver ki beneficence (bhalayi) ke hisaab se. Kyunki jo log receive karte hain wo kehte hain ki unhe apne benefactors (upkaarkarta) se wo mila jo unke liye kam matter karta tha aur jo unhe doosron se bhi mil sakta tha — service ko minimize karte hue; jabki givers, iske ulat, kehte hain ki ye unke paas sabse badi cheez thi, aur jo unhe doosron se nahi mil sakta tha, aur ye danger ya zaroorat ke samay mein diya gaya tha. Ab agar friendship utility ki wajah se hai, to surely receiver ko hui advantage hi measure hai. Kyunki wahi hai jo service maangta hai, aur doosra insaan is assumption pe use help karta hai ki use equivalent milega; isliye assistance (madad) utni hi badi hai jitni receiver ko advantage hui hai, aur isliye use utna hi return karna chahiye jitna usne receive kiya, ya usse bhi zyaada (kyunki wo zyaada noble hoga). Virtue pe based friendships mein, doosri taraf, complaints nahi uthti, balki doer (karne wale) ka purpose (uddeshya) hi ek tarah ka measure hai; kyunki purpose mein hi virtue aur character ka essential element hota hai.

## Chapter 14 — Unequals ke beech friendship mein observe kiye jaane waale principles

Differences (bhinnataayen) superiority pe based friendships mein bhi aati hain; kyunki har ek expect karta hai ki use unse zyaada mile, lekin jab aisa hota hai to friendship dissolve ho jaati hai. Sirf behtar insaan hi nahi sochta ki use zyaada milna chahiye, kyunki good insaan ko zyaada milna chahiye, balki zyaada useful insaan bhi yahi expect karta hai; wo kehte hain ki ek useless (bekaar) insaan ko utna nahi milna chahiye jitna unhe milna chahiye, kyunki agar friendship ke proceeds (parinaam) diye gaye benefits ke worth (mol) ke anusaar nahi hote to ye ek public service (sarvajanik seva) ban jaati hai, friendship nahi. Kyunki wo sochte hain ki jaise ek commercial partnership mein jo zyaada daalte hain unhe zyaada milta hai, waise hi friendship mein bhi hona chahiye. Lekin jo insaan need (zaroorat) aur inferiority (kamtari) ki state mein hai wo opposite claim karta hai; aise log sochte hain ki ek good friend ka kaam yahi hai ki wo zaroorat mand logon ki madad kare; wo kehte hain, ek good insaan ya powerful insaan ka friend hone ka kya fayda, agar usse kuch milna hi nahi hai?

Aakhirkaar dono party ka claim justified lagta hai, aur har ek ko friendship se doosre se zyaada milna chahiye — same cheez ka zyaada nahi, balki superior (shreshtha) ko zyaada honour milna chahiye aur inferior (kamtar) ko zyaada gain (laabh); kyunki honour virtue aur beneficence ka inaam hai, jabki gain wo assistance hai jo inferiority ko chahiye hoti hai.

Ye constitutional arrangements (shaasan-vyavastha) mein bhi aisa hi lagta hai; jo insaan common stock (saanjhi sampatti) mein kuch good contribute nahi karta use honour nahi milti; kyunki jo public ka hai wo us insaan ko diya jaata hai jo public ka bhala karta hai, aur honour public ki hoti hai. Wealth aur honour dono ek saath common stock se paana possible nahi hai. Kyunki koi bhi sab cheezon mein smaller share (chhota hissa) bardaasht nahi karta; isliye jo insaan wealth mein haarta hai use honour di jaati hai, aur jo insaan paise lene ko taiyar hai use wealth di jaati hai, kyunki merit ke proportion (anupaat) mein equalize karna hi parties ko equal banaata hai aur friendship ko preserve karta hai, jaisa humne kaha hai.

Isliye yahi tareeka hai jisse humein unequals ke saath associate hona chahiye; jo insaan wealth ya virtue ke respect mein benefit paata hai use badle mein honour deni chahiye, jo wo kar sake wo return karte hue. Kyunki friendship insaan se wo maangti hai jo wo kar sake, na ki jo case ke merits ke anupaat mein ho; kyunki ye hamesha possible nahi hota, jaise gods ya parents ko di jaane waali honours mein; kyunki koi bhi unhe kabhi wo equivalent wapas nahi de sakta jo usne paaya hai, lekin jo insaan unhe apni poori power se serve karta hai use ek good insaan maana jaata hai.

Isi liye ye theek nahi lagta ki koi insaan apne father ko disown (aswikaar) kare (halaanki father apne son ko disown kar sakta hai); karz mein hote hue, use repay karna chahiye, lekin aisa kuch nahi hai jo karke ek son ne wo equivalent de diya ho jo usne paaya, isliye wo hamesha karz mein hi rehta hai. Lekin creditors (rin-daata) karz maaf kar sakte hain; aur isliye father bhi aisa kar sakta hai. Isi samay ye bhi socha jaata hai ki shayad koi bhi apne son ko repudiate (aswikaar) nahi karega jab tak wo bahut zyaada wickedness (buraayi) mein na doob gaya ho; kyunki father-son ki natural friendship ke alawa bhi ye human nature hai ki koi apne son ki assistance ko reject na kare. Lekin son, agar wo wicked (bura) hai, to naturally apne father ki madad se bachega, ya ismein zealous (utsahit) nahi hoga; kyunki zyaadatar log benefits paana chahte hain, lekin unhe dena avoid (taalna) karte hain, jaise ye ek unprofitable (be-faayde ki) cheez ho.

Itni hi in questions ke baare mein baat thi.

---

# BOOK IX · FRIENDSHIP (cont.)

## 1. Principles jo dhyan mein rakhne chahiye (c) jab dono taraf ke motives (intentions) alag hon

Jitni bhi friendships dissimilar (asaman/alag-alag) logon ke beech hoti hain, unmein — jaisa humne pehle bhi kaha — proportion (anupaat) hi hai jo dono parties ko barabar karta hai aur friendship ko bachaye rakhta hai. Jaise political friendship mein mochi (shoemaker) ko apne juton ke badle uske worth ke hisaab se return milta hai, aur bunkar (weaver) aur baaki sab craftsmen (kaarigar) bhi aisa hi karte hain. Yahan ek common measure (saanjha paimana) diya gaya hai paise ki shakal mein, isliye har cheez ko isi se refer aur measure kiya jaata hai. Lekin lovers ki friendship mein kabhi-kabhi lover complain karta hai ki uska excess of love (zyaadti bhara pyaar) return mein utna pyaar nahi paata — halaanki shayad usmein kuch lovable (pyaar ke laayak) hi nahi hai — jabki aksar beloved (jise pyaar kiya jaata hai) complain karta hai ki lover jo pehle sab kuch promise karta tha ab kuch bhi perform nahi karta.

Aisi ghatnayein tab hoti hain jab lover, beloved ko pleasure (sukh) ke liye pyaar karta hai jabki beloved, lover ko utility (upyogita) ke liye pyaar karta hai, aur dono ke paas woh qualities nahi hoti jo unse expect ki jaati hain. Agar friendship ki bunyaad yehi objects (uddeshya) hon, toh jab unhe woh cheezein nahi milti jo unke pyaar ki motive (prerna) thi, toh friendship dissolve (khatam) ho jaati hai; kyunki dono ne ek-dusre ko khud ke liye nahi, balki unki un qualities ke liye pyaar kiya tha, aur woh qualities enduring (sthaayi) nahi thi — isi wajah se aisi friendships bhi transient (kshanik/aste-thodi der ki) hoti hain. Lekin character (charitra) se hone waala pyaar, jaisa pehle kaha gaya, self-dependent (khud par nirbhar) hone ki wajah se endure (tikta) karta hai.

Differences (matbhed) tab paida hote hain jab jo unhe milta hai woh kuch aur hota hai, aur jo woh chahte the woh nahi milta — kyunki jab hum jo chahte hain woh nahi paate, toh yeh kuch na paane jaisa hi hota hai. Us kissa (kahani) ko yaad karo us aadmi ka jisne ek lyre-bajane waale (lyre-player) se promise kiya tha ki jitna acha woh gayega utna zyaada usse milega, lekin subah jab doosre ne apne promise poore hone ki maang ki, toh usne kaha ki usne pleasure ke badle pleasure de diya. Agar yehi dono chahte the, toh sab theek hota; lekin agar ek enjoyment (aanand) chahta tha aur doosra gain (fayda), aur ek ko jo chahiye woh mil gaya jabki doosre ko nahi mila, toh association (sambandh) ki terms (sharten) sahi tarah se poori nahi hui maani jaayengi — kyunki har insaan jo asal mein chahta hai wahi uska dhyan hota hai, aur usi ke liye woh apna diya hua kuch dega.

Lekin service (seva) ki worth (keemat) kaun tay karega — woh jisne sacrifice (tyag) kiya ya woh jisne advantage (labh) paaya? Kam se kam doosra iske liye pehle waale par hi chhodta lagta hai. Yeh kehte hain ki Protagoras aisa hi karta tha: jab bhi woh kuch bhi sikhata, seekhne waale se kehta ki woh khud us knowledge (gyaan) ki value (mol) assess (aanka) kare, aur jitna woh tay kare utna hi accept kar leta. Lekin aise maamlon mein kuch log iss kehne ko approve karte hain ki 'aadmi ko apna fixed reward (tay shuda inaam) rakhna chahiye.'

Jo log pehle paisa le lete hain aur phir apne kahe hue kaam nahi karte, apni promises ki extravagance (atirekta) ki wajah se, woh naturally complain ka target ban jaate hain — kyunki woh apna kiya wada poora nahi karte. Sophists (vidwaan-sikhane waale) shayad isliye majboor hote hain aisa karne ke liye kyunki unke asli gyaan ke liye koi paisa nahi deta. Toh aise log, agar woh apne liye chuka gaye kaam nahi karte, naturally complain ke haqdar bante hain.

Lekin jahan koi service ka contract (samjhauta) nahi hota, wahan jo log doosri party ke liye kuch chhod dete hain unhe complain nahi kiya ja sakta (jaisa humne kaha) — kyunki yehi virtue (sadgun) waali friendship ka nature (swabhav) hai — aur unhe jo return (badla) diya jaaye woh unke purpose (uddeshya) ke aadhar par hona chahiye (kyunki purpose hi hai jo friend mein aur virtue mein characteristic (visheshta) hoti hai). Aur isi tarah, lagta hai, unhe bhi return dena chahiye jinke saath humne philosophy padhi ho — kyunki unki worth paise se naapi nahi ja sakti, aur unhe koi aisi honour (samman) nahi mil sakti jo unki services ke barabar ho; lekin shayad itna hi kaafi hai, jaise devताओं aur apne parents ke saath hota hai, ki jo de sakte hain woh de diya jaaye.

Agar gift (uphaar) is tarah ka nahi tha, balki return paane ki niyat se diya gaya tha, toh behtar yehi hai ki jo return diya jaaye woh dono parties ko fair (uचित) lage; lekin agar yeh mumkin na ho, toh zaroori — aur just (nyaayसंगत) bhi — hai ki jisne pehli service li hai wahi reward (inaam) tay kare. Kyunki agar doosre ko woh mil jaaye jo beneficiary (labh paane waale) ko mile advantage ke barabar ho, ya woh price jo woh pleasure ke liye deta, toh usne jo fair tha woh paa liya doosre se.

Yeh cheez hum bikri ki cheezon mein bhi dekhte hain, aur kuchh jagahon par kanoon hain ki voluntary contracts (swechchha se kiye samjhaute) se koi legal action (kanooni karvaai) nahi ho sakti — is assumption (dharna) par ki jisse credit diya gaya usi bhavना mein uske saath settle karna chahiye jismein deal hua tha. Kanoon maanta hai ki yeh zyaada just hai ki jise credit diya gaya woh terms (sharten) tay kare, na ki jisne credit diya. Kyunki zyaadatar cheezein unke liye jo unke paas hain aur unke liye jo unhe chahiye, alag value par assess ki jaati hain — har class apni cheez ki aur jo woh offer kar rahe hain uski keemat zyaada aankti hai; phir bhi return receiver (paane waale) ki tay ki hui terms par hi diya jaata hai. Lekin shayad receiver ko cheez ko uski keemat se assess nahi karna chahiye jab woh uske paas ho, balki uske according jo usne cheez paane se pehle assess ki thi.

## 2. Obligations (zimmedariyon) ka conflict (takraav)

Ek aur sawaal yeh hai ki kya aadmi ko har cheez mein apne father (pita) ko preference (pehla darja) deni chahiye aur uski baat manni chahiye, ya jab woh beemar ho toh doctor par trust karna chahiye, aur jab general chunna ho toh military skill waale aadmi ko chunna chahiye; aur isi tarah kya kisi ko service karne mein friend ko ya achhe insaan ko pehle rakhna chahiye, aur benefactor (upkaari) ke prati gratitude (kritagyata) dikhaani chahiye ya friend ki madad karni chahiye, agar dono nahi ho sakte.

Aise saare sawaal mushkil hain, sahi decide karna, hai na? Kyunki inmein service ki magnitude (bade-chhote hone), uski nobility (mahaanta) aur necessity (avashyakta) ke hisaab se bahut variations (bhinnataayein) hoti hain. Lekin yeh saaf hai ki humein har cheez mein ek hi insaan ko preference nahi deni chahiye; aur hume zyaadatar benefits (upkaar) ka badla dena chahiye friends ki madad karne se zyaada — jaise humein creditor (rin-daata) ko udhaar wapas dena chahiye, na ki friend ko udhaar dena. Lekin shayad yeh bhi hamesha sach nahi hota; jaise, kya jo aadmi brigands (daaku) ke haath se ransom (fidiya) dekar chhudaaya gaya ho, use apne chhudaane waale ko waapas ransom dena chahiye, chaahe woh koi bhi ho (ya use payment dena chahiye agar woh khud pakda nahi gaya lekin payment maang raha hai), ya use apne father ko chhudaana chahiye? Aisa lagta hai ki use apne father ko hi chhudaana chahiye, khud se bhi pehle.

Jaisa humne kaha, generally debt (karz) chukaya jaana chahiye, lekin agar gift atyant noble (mahaan) ya atyant necessary hai, toh in considerations (vicharon) ko preference deni chahiye. Kyunki kabhi-kabhi jo mila hai uska barabar return dena bhi fair nahi hota — jab ek aadmi ne kisi ko service ki hai jise woh achha jaanta hai, jabki doosra return de raha hai us insaan ko jise woh bura maanta hai. Kabhi-kabhi to insaan ko us insaan ko udhaar wapas bhi nahi dena chahiye jisne use udhaar diya tha; kyunki ek ne achhe aadmi ko udhaar diya, apna loan wapas paane ki ummeed se, jabki doosra bure maane jaane waale se paane ki koi ummeed nahi rakhta. Isliye agar facts (tathya) waaqai aise hain, toh demand (maang) fair nahi hai; aur agar aise nahi hain, lekin log aisa sochte hain, toh unhe mana karne mein kuch ajeeb nahi maana jaayega.

Jaisa humne baar-baar kaha hai, feelings (bhaavnaon) aur actions (kriyaon) ke baare mein discussions mein utni hi definiteness (spashtata) hoti hai jitni unke subject-matter (vishay-vastu) mein hoti hai.

Yeh bhi saaf hai ki humein har insaan ko ek jaisa return nahi dena chahiye, na hi father ko har cheez mein preference deni chahiye — jaise hum Zeus ko sab kuch sacrifice (bhent) nahi karte. Lekin chunki humein parents, brothers, comrades (saathiyon), aur benefactors ko alag-alag cheezein deni hoti hain, toh humein har class ko woh dena chahiye jo appropriate (uचित) aur becoming (shobhaneey) ho. Aur yehi log asal mein karte bhi hain: shaadiyon mein woh apne kinsfolk (rishtedaron) ko bulaate hain, kyunki unka family ke maamlon mein hissa hota hai. Funerals (antim sanskaar) mein bhi woh maante hain ki kinsfolk ko sabse pehle milna chahiye, isi wajah se.

Aur khaane-peene ke maamle mein humein apne parents ki sabse pehle madad karni chahiye, kyunki hum apna poshan (nourishment) unhi se paate hain, aur apne astitva (existence) ke authors (jankartaon) ki madad karna khud se bhi pehle zyaada honourable (samaanjanak) hai. Honour (samman) bhi humein apne parents ko devताओं jaisa dena chahiye, lekin har tarah ka honour nahi — father aur mother ko ek hi honour nahi dena chahiye, na hi unhe philosopher ya general jaisa honour dena chahiye, balki jaisa father ko chahiye, ya mother ko chahiye waisa dena chahiye. Sab buzurgon ko unki umr ke hisaab se honour dena chahiye — unke liye khade hoke, seat dekar, waghera. Comrades aur brothers ko freedom of speech (khule taur par bolne ki azaadi) aur cheezon ke common use (saanjhe upyog) ki chhoot deni chahiye. Kinsmen (rishtedaron), fellow tribesmen (jaati-bandhuon) aur fellow citizens (saathi nagarikon), aur har doosri class ko humesha woh dena chahiye jo appropriate ho, aur har class ke claims (dawon) ko unki nearness of relation (rishte ki nazdeeki) aur virtue (sadgun) ya usefulness (upyogita) ke hisaab se compare karna chahiye. Comparison (tulna) tab aasan hoti hai jab log ek hi class ke hon, aur zyaada laborious (mehnat-talab) hoti hai jab woh alag hon. Phir bhi, isse hume peechhe nahi hatna chahiye, balki jitna ho sake best decide karna chahiye.

## 3. Friendship todne ke occasions (avsar)

Ek aur sawaal yeh uthta hai ki kya friendships todni chahiye ya nahi jab doosri party pehle jaisi nahi rehti. Shayad hum kah sakte hain ki utility (upyogita) ya pleasantness (sukhad hone) par based friendship todne mein kuch ajeeb nahi hai, jab humare friends mein woh attributes (gun) nahi rehte — kyunki hum unhi attributes ke friend the, aur jab woh khatam ho jaayein toh ab pyaar na karna reasonable (yukti-sangat) hai. Lekin insaan doosre se complain kar sakta hai agar, jab woh humein humari usefulness ya pleasantness ke liye pyaar karta tha, usne pretend (dikhawa) kiya ki woh humare character (charitra) ke liye pyaar karta hai.

Kyunki, jaisa humne shuru mein kaha, friends ke beech zyaadatar differences tab paida hote hain jab woh us spirit (bhaav) mein friend nahi hote jaisa woh sochte hain ki hain. Toh jab kisi ne khud ko dhoka diya ho aur socha ho ki uska pyaar uske character ke liye ho raha hai, jabki doosra aisa kuch nahi kar raha tha, toh use khud ko blame (dosh) dena chahiye; lekin jab use doosre ke pretences (dikhawon) se dhoka mila ho, toh yeh just (nyaay-sangat) hai ki woh apne deceiver (dhokebaaz) se complain kare — aur woh sikke banaawat (counterfeit currency banaane) waalon se complain karne se bhi zyaada justice ke saath complain karega, kyunki yahan galti kuch zyaada valuable (keemti) cheez se juda hai.

Lekin agar koi kisi ko achha maan kar accept karta hai, aur woh bura nikalta hai aur yeh dikhta bhi hai, toh kya use phir bhi pyaar karna chahiye? Zaroor yeh impossible (asambhav) hai, kyunki har cheez pyaar ke laayak nahi hoti, sirf achhi cheez hoti hai. Jo evil (bura) hai use na pyaar kiya ja sakta hai na karna chahiye — kyunki evil ka lover (prem-karta) banna ya bure jaisa banna kisi ka farz nahi hai; aur humne kaha hai ki like, like ko hi pyaara hota hai. Toh kya friendship turant tod deni chahiye? Ya yeh har case mein nahi hota, balki sirf tab jab friend apni wickedness (dushtata) mein incurable (asaadhya) ho? Agar woh reform (sudhar) ho sakte hain toh unke character ya property (sampatti) ki madad karni chahiye — kyunki yeh behtar hai aur friendship ki zyaada characteristic baat hai. Lekin jo insaan aisi friendship khatam karta hai use kuch ajeeb karta hua nahi maana jaayega — kyunki woh us tarah ke aadmi ka friend nahi tha; jab uska friend badal gaya aur woh use bacha nahi paaya, toh woh use chhod deta hai.

Lekin agar ek friend pehle jaisa raha aur doosra behtar ban gaya aur virtue (sadgun) mein use bahut peechhe chhod diya, toh kya doosra pehle waale ko friend maan kar treat kare? Zaroor nahi kar sakta. Jab yeh gap (antar) bada ho toh yeh sabse zyaada saaf ho jaata hai — jaise bachpan ki friendships mein: agar ek friend intellect (buddhi) mein bachcha hi raha jabki doosra pura developed insaan ban gaya, toh woh friend kaise ho sakte hain jab unhe na ek jaisi cheezein pasand aayein aur na ek jaisi cheezon se dukh-sukh ho? Kyunki ek-dusre ke baare mein bhi unke tastes (ruchiyaan) match nahi karengi, aur iske bina (jaisa humne dekha) woh friend nahi ho sakte — kyunki woh saath nahi reh sakte. Lekin humne yeh baat pehle discuss kar li hai.

Toh kya use us insaan ke saath waisa hi behave karna chahiye jaisa agar woh kabhi friend hi na raha ho? Zaroor use unki purani intimacy (gehri dosti) ki yaad rakhni chahiye, aur jaise hum sochte hain ki humein strangers (ajnabiyon) se zyaada friends ki madad karni chahiye, waise hi jo humare friend rah chuke hain unke liye bhi humein kuchh allowance (chhoot) deni chahiye, purani friendship ki wajah se, jab tak breach (rishta toota hona) atyant wickedness ki wajah se na hua ho.

# INTERNAL NATURE OF FRIENDSHIP (Friendship ki antarik prakriti)

## 4. Friendship self-love (khud se pyaar) par based hai

Neighbours (padosiyon) ke saath friendly relations (dosti bhare rishte), aur jin marks (nishaaniyon) se friendships define hoti hain, woh sab lagta hai insaan ke khud ke saath rishte se hi nikle hain. Kyunki (1) hum friend ko us insaan ki tarah define karte hain jo apne friend ke liye achha chahta hai aur karta hai (ya jo achha lagta ho), uske khaatir; ya (2) us insaan ki tarah jo chahta hai ki uska friend exist kare aur jeeye, uske khaatir — jaisa maayein apne bachchon ke liye karti hain, aur jo friends kisi conflict (takraav) mein aa chuke hain woh bhi karte hain. Aur (3) kuch ise define karte hain us insaan ki tarah jo doosre ke saath rehta hai aur (4) uske jaise hi tastes rakhta hai, ya (5) jo apne friend ke saath dukhi aur khush hota hai — aur yeh sabse zyaada maayon mein paaya jaata hai. In hi characteristics mein se kisi ek se friendship define hoti hai.

Ab in sabmein se har ek baat achhe insaan ke apne khud ke saath rishte mein sach hai (aur baaki sab insaanon ke bhi, jitna woh khud ko achha maante hain — virtue aur achha insaan, jaisa kaha ja chuka hai, har class ki cheezon ka measure (paimana) maane jaate hain). Kyunki uski opinions (raaye) harmonious (ekroop) hoti hain, aur woh apni poori aatma se ek hi cheez chahta hai; isliye woh apne liye woh chahta hai jo achha hai aur jo achha lagta hai, aur use karta hai (kyunki achhe cheez par kaam karna achhe insaan ki characteristic hai), aur yeh apne hi khaatir karta hai (kyunki woh apne andar ke intellectual element — buddhi-tatva — ke khaatir karta hai, jise asli insaan maana jaata hai); aur woh chahta hai ki khud jeeye aur bacha rahe, khaas kar woh element jiski wajah se woh sochta hai. Kyunki existence virtuous (sadaachaari) aadmi ke liye achha hai, aur har insaan apne liye achhi cheez chahta hai, jabki koi bhi poori duniya paana nahi chahega agar pehle use koi aur ban jaana pade (aakhir, abhi bhi god achha hi rakhta hai) — woh yeh sirf isi shart par chahta hai ki jo hai wahi rahe; aur woh element jo sochta hai wahi asli insaan hai, ya kisi aur element se zyaada hai.

Aur aisa insaan khud ke saath rehna chahta hai; kyunki woh isse pleasure (aanand) leta hai, kyunki uske pichhle kaamon ki yaadein delightful (sukhad) hoti hain aur bhavishya ke liye uski hopes achhi, isliye pleasant hoti hain. Uska mind bhi contemplation (chintan) ke vishayon se bhara hota hai. Aur woh khud ke saath, kisi aur se zyaada, dukhi aur khush hota hai — kyunki ek hi cheez hamesha painful (dukhad) hoti hai aur ek hi cheez hamesha pleasant, aur ek waqt ek cheez aur doosre waqt doosri nahi hoti; use, ek tarah se, kisi baat ka regret (pachhtaava) nahi hota.

Isliye, chunki in sab characteristics mein se har ek achhe insaan ka apne khud ke saath rishta hai, aur woh apne friend se waise hi related hai jaise khud se (kyunki friend doosra khud hai), friendship bhi in hi attributes mein se ek maani jaati hai, aur jinke paas yeh attributes hote hain unhe friend maana jaata hai. Kya insaan aur khud ke beech friendship hai ya nahi — yeh sawaal abhi ke liye chhod dete hain; lagta hai ki friendship hoti hai jab insaan do ya zyaada roopon mein ho, upar bataye gaye friendship ke attributes se, aur is fact se ki friendship ki extreme (parakashtha) khud se pyaar jaisi hi maani jaati hai.

Lekin yeh bataye gaye attributes zyaadatar logon mein bhi paaye jaate hain, chaahe woh kitne bhi ghatiya (poor) kyun na hon. Toh kya hum kahein ki jitna woh khud se santusht hain aur khud ko achha maante hain, utna hi woh in attributes mein share karte hain? Zaroor koi bhi jo poori tarah bura aur impious (adharmi) hai, uske paas yeh attributes nahi hote, na hi aisa dikhta hai. Yeh inferior (nikrisht) logon mein bhi shayad hi paaye jaate hain, kyunki woh khud se hi at variance (asahmat) hote hain — unmein kuch cheezon ke liye appetites (laalsa) aur kuch cheezon ke liye rational desires (yukti-sangat ichchhayein) hoti hain. Yeh incontinent (asanyami) logon ke baare mein sach hai — jo cheez unhe khud achhi lagti hai uske badle woh pleasant lekin hurtful (haani-karak) cheezon ke peechhe jaate hain; jabki kuch aur, cowardice (kaayarta) aur laziness (aalasya) ki wajah se, woh karne se katate hain jo unhe apne liye best lagta hai. Aur jinhone bahut se terrible (bhayaanak) kaam kiye hain aur apni wickedness ki wajah se hated (ghrinit) hain, woh life se hi shrink (peechhe hatna) karte hain aur khud ko destroy (nasht) kar lete hain. Iske alaawa, wicked (dusht) log doosron ke saath samay bitaane ke liye logon ki talaash karte hain, aur khud se bhaagte hain — kyunki jab woh akele hote hain toh unhe apne bahut se grievous (dukhad) karm yaad aate hain, aur waise hi doosre karmon ka anticipate (poorvanuman) karte hain; lekin doosron ke saath hone par woh bhool jaate hain. Aur unmein kuch bhi lovable na hone ki wajah se unhe khud se koi feeling of love nahi hoti. Isliye aise log khud ke saath na khush hote hain na dukhi — kyunki unki soul (aatma) faction (phoot) se phati hoti hai, aur uska ek element apni wickedness ki wajah se dukhi hota hai jab woh kuch karmon se rukta hai, jabki doosra part khush hota hai — aur ek use ek taraf khinchta hai aur doosra doosri taraf, jaise woh unhe tukdon mein kheench rahe hon.

Agar insaan ek hi samay mein dukhi aur khush nahi ho sakta, toh kam se kam thodi der baad woh dukhi hota hai kyunki woh khush hua tha, aur usne chaha hota ki yeh cheezein use pleasant na lagti — kyunki bure log regrets (pachhtaavon) se bhare hote hain. Isliye bura aadmi khud ke saath bhi amicable (mitrata-poorn) nahi lagta, kyunki uske andar pyaar karne laayak kuch hai hi nahi; toh agar yeh hi wretchedness (dukhad dasha) ki inti-ha (parakashtha) hai, toh humein wickedness se bachne aur achha banne ki poori koshish karni chahiye — kyunki tabhi insaan khud ka bhi friend ban sakta hai aur doosre ka bhi.

## 5. Friendship ka goodwill (shubh-ichchha) se rishta

Goodwill friendship ki characteristic hai, lekin friendship ke barabar nahi hai — kyunki insaan un logon ke liye bhi goodwill rakh sakta hai jinhe woh jaanta nahi, aur unke jaane bina bhi, lekin friendship nahi rakh sakta. Yeh baat pehle bhi kahi ja chuki hai. Lekin goodwill toh friendly feeling (mitrata-poorn bhaavna) bhi nahi hai — kyunki isme intensity (tivrata) ya desire (ichchha) shaamil nahi hoti, jabki yeh cheezein friendly feeling ke saath hoti hain; aur friendly feeling mein intimacy (gehraayi) implied hoti hai jabki goodwill achaanak paida ho sakti hai, jaise ek contest (pratiyogita) ke competitors (pratiyogiyon) ke liye — hum unke liye achaanak goodwill mehsoos karte hain aur unki wishes (kaamnaon) mein share karte hain, lekin unke saath kuch karenge nahi; kyunki, jaisa humne kaha, hum achaanak goodwill mehsoos karte hain aur unhe sirf superficially (upari taur par) pyaar karte hain.

Goodwill lagta hai ki friendship ki shuruaat hai, jaise aankh ka pleasure pyaar ki shuruaat hota hai. Kyunki koi bhi pyaar nahi karta agar use pehle beloved ke roop se khushi na mili ho, lekin jo doosre ke roop se khush hota hai woh isse pyaar nahi karta, jab tak woh usse door hone par bhi use chahta na ho aur uski presence (uपस्थिति) ke liye tarasta na ho. Isi tarah log friend nahi ban sakte agar unhone ek-dusre ke liye goodwill mehsoos na ki ho, lekin jo goodwill mehsoos karte hain woh isliye friend nahi ban jaate — kyunki woh sirf un logon ke liye achha chahte hain jinke liye unhe goodwill hoti hai, aur unke saath kuch karenge ya unke liye mehnat nahi karenge.

Toh ek extension (vistaar) ke roop mein 'friendship' ka term use karke koi kah sakta hai ki goodwill inactive (nishkriya) friendship hai, halaanki jab yeh lambe samay tak chalti hai aur intimacy tak pahunchti hai toh friendship ban jaati hai — na woh friendship jo utility par based ho, na woh jo pleasure par based ho; kyunki goodwill bhi in shartein par nahi uthti. Jisne koi benefit (labh) paaya ho woh badle mein goodwill deta hai jo uske saath hua uske liye, lekin aisa karke woh sirf just (nyaayसंगत) kaam kar raha hota hai; jabki jo kisi ke prosper (samriddh) hone ki kaamna karta hai kyunki use uske through enrichment (samriddhi) ki ummeed hai, woh usse nahi balki khud ke prati zyaada goodwill rakhta hai — jaise ek insaan doosre ka friend nahi hota agar woh use kisi use ke liye pasand karta hai. General taur par, goodwill kisi excellence (utkrishtata) aur worth ki wajah se uthti hai, jab ek insaan doosre ko sundar ya bahaadur ya aisa hi kuch lagta hai, jaisa humne contest ke competitors ke case mein dikhaya.

## 6. Friendship ka concord (samajhauta/ekmat hona) se rishta

Concord bhi friendship ki characteristic maani jaati hai. Isliye yeh identity of opinion (raaye ki samaanta) nahi hai — kyunki yeh un logon mein bhi ho sakti hai jo ek-dusre ko jaante hi nahi; aur hum nahi kehte ki jo log kisi bhi vishay par ek jaisi raaye rakhte hain woh accord (samanjasya) mein hain — jaise jo log heavenly bodies (aakashiya pindon) ke baare mein sehmat hain (kyunki inke baare mein concord friendship ki characteristic nahi hai) — balki hum kehte hain ki ek city accord mein hoti hai jab log apne interest (hit) ke baare mein ek hi opinion rakhte hain, ek hi actions choose karte hain, aur jo unhone milkar decide kiya hai woh karte hain.

Isliye actions ke baare mein hi log accord mein kahe jaate hain, aur inmein bhi un baaton mein jo consequence (mahatva) rakhti hain aur jinmein dono ya sab parties ko woh mil sake jo woh chahte hain — jaise ek city accord mein hoti hai jab uske sab citizens sochte hain ki offices (padvi) elective (chunaav se) honi chahiye, ya unhe Sparta ke saath alliance (gathbandhan) karna chahiye, ya Pittacus ko unka ruler (shaasak) hona chahiye — jab woh khud bhi shaasan karne ko taiyaar tha. Lekin jab do logon mein se har ek khud ke liye woh cheez chahta hai, jaise Phoenissae ke captains, toh woh faction (phoot) ki sthiti mein hain — kyunki yeh concord nahi hai jab do parties ek hi cheez ke baare mein sochein, jo bhi woh ho, balki tabhi hota hai jab woh us ek cheez ke baare mein ek hi haathon mein sochein — jaise jab common people aur better class dono chahte hain ki best log hi shaasan karein; kyunki isi tarah aur sirf isi tarah sabko jo woh chahte hain woh milta hai.

Toh concord political friendship lagta hai, jaisa aam taur par kaha bhi jaata hai — kyunki yeh un baaton se sambandhit hai jo humare interest se juda hai aur humari zindagi par asar daalti hain. Aisi concord achhe logon mein paayi jaati hai — kyunki woh khud mein bhi aur ek-dusre ke saath bhi accord mein hote hain, ek tarah se ek hi mann ke hote hain (kyunki aise logon ki wishes sthir hoti hain, na ki samundar ki dhaara jaisi badalti rehti hain), aur woh justice (nyaay) aur advantage (labh) ke liye chahte hain, aur yeh unke saanjhe endeavour (prayaas) ke objects bhi hote hain. Lekin bure log accord mein bahut kam ho sakte hain, jitna woh friends ho sakte hain — kyunki woh apne hisse se zyaada advantage paane ki koshish karte hain, jabki labour (mehnat) aur public service mein apne hisse se kam karte hain; aur har insaan khud ke liye advantage chahte hue apne padosi ki nindaa karta hai aur uska raasta rokta hai — kyunki agar log dhyaan se na dekhein toh common weal (saanjha bhala) jaldi hi barbaad ho jaata hai. Natija yeh hota hai ki woh faction ki sthiti mein hote hain, ek-dusre par majboori dalte hain lekin khud jo just hai woh nahi karna chahte.

## 7. Beneficence (upkaar) ka pleasure

Benefactors (upkaari log) ko lagta hai ki woh unse zyaada pyaar karte hain jinki unhone madad ki hai, us pyaar se jo un logon ka apne upkaari ke liye hota hai jinki madad hui — aur yeh baat paradoxical (viparyaay-poorn) lagti hai discuss karne mein. Zyaadatar log sochte hain ki isliye kyunki wo doosre debtors (karzdaar) ki tarah hain aur pehla waala creditor (rin-daata) ki tarah — isliye jaise, loans (karzon) ke maamle mein, debtors chahte hain ki unke creditors exist hi na karein, jabki creditors asal mein apne debtors ki safety (suraksha) ka khyaal rakhte hain — waise hi socha jaata hai ki benefactors chahte hain ki jinki madad ki hai woh exist karte rahein, taaki unhe gratitude mile, jabki jinki madad hui hai woh yeh return karne mein interest nahi lete.

Epicharmus shayad kehta ki log yeh isliye kehte hain kyunki woh 'cheezon ko unke bure pehlu se dekhte hain,' lekin yeh human nature (manushya-swabhav) jaisa hi lagta hai — kyunki zyaadatar log bhool-bhulaiyya (forgetful) hote hain, aur doosron ke saath achha karne se zyaada khud ke saath achha hone ki fikr karte hain. Lekin iska cause (kaaran) shayad cheezon ki nature (prakriti) mein zyaada gehra hai — jinhone paisa udhaar diya hai unka case toh analogous (samaan) bhi nahi hai. Kyunki unhe apne debtors ke liye koi friendly feeling nahi hoti, sirf yeh chaahat hoti hai ki woh mehfooz rahein taaki unse jo milna hai woh mil sake; jabki jinhone doosron ki seva ki hai, woh unke liye friendship aur pyaar mehsoos karte hain jinki unhone seva ki, chaahe woh unke kisi kaam ke na hon aur kabhi na hongen.

Yeh craftsmen ke saath bhi hota hai — har insaan apni handiwork (haath se banaayi cheez) ko usse zyaada pyaar karta hai jitna woh uski handiwork se pyaara jaata agar woh zinda ho jaaye; aur yeh shayad poets (kaviyon) mein sabse zyaada hota hai, kyunki unhe apni kavitaon se excessive (ati-adhik) pyaar hota hai, unhe apne bachchon jaisa maankar. Yehi benefactors ki position bhi hai, kyunki jinki unhone madad ki hai woh unki handiwork hai, aur isliye woh isse zyaada pyaar karte hain us handiwork se, jitna handiwork apne maker (banaane waale) se karti hai. Iska cause yeh hai ki existence har insaan ke liye choose karne aur pyaar karne laayak cheez hai, aur hum activity (kriya) ke through hi exist karte hain (yaani jeene aur karm karne se), aur handiwork ek tarah se producer (nirmaata) hi hai actuality (waastavikta) mein — woh apni handiwork se isliye pyaar karta hai kyunki woh apne existence se pyaar karta hai. Aur yeh cheezon ki nature mein hi hai, kyunki jo woh potentiality (sambhaavna) mein hai, uski handiwork actuality mein dikhati hai.

Isi ke saath, benefactor ke liye noble (mahaan) wahi hai jo uske action (karm) par depend karta hai, isliye woh apne karm ke object se khush hota hai; jabki patient (jiski madad hui) ke liye agent (madadgaar) mein kuch bhi noble nahi hota, zyaada se zyaada kuch advantageous (labh-daayak), aur yeh kam pleasant aur kam lovable hota hai. Jo pleasant hai woh hai present (vartamaan) ki activity, future (bhavishya) ki hope (aasha), past (bhoot) ki memory (yaad); lekin sabse pleasant woh hai jo activity par depend karta hai, aur yehi sabse lovable bhi hai. Ab jis insaan ne kuch banaaya hai uska kaam bacha rehta hai (kyunki noble cheez lasting/sthaayi hoti hai), lekin jispar act kiya gaya uske liye utility guzar jaati hai. Aur noble cheezon ki memory pleasant hoti hai, lekin useful cheezon ki utni pleasant nahi hoti, ya kam hoti hai — halaanki expectation (poorvashaa) ke maamle mein ulta sach lagta hai.

Iske alaawa, pyaar activity jaisa hai, aur loved (pyaar kiya jaana) passivity (nishkriyata) jaisa; aur pyaar karna aur uske saath judi cheezein un logon ki attributes hain jo zyaada active (kriyaasheel) hote hain. Phir, sab log usse zyaada pyaar karte hain jo unhone labour (mehnat) se paaya ho — jaise jinhone khud paisa kamaaya hai woh use inherit (viraasat mein paayi) karne waalon se zyaada pyaar karte hain apne paise se; aur achhi tarah treat kiye jaane mein koi labour nahi lagta, jabki doosron ke saath achha karna ek laborious (mehnat-talab) kaam hai. Yehi wajah hai ki maayein apne bachchon se fathers se zyaada attached hoti hain — unhe bachcha paida karne mein zyaada dard uthaana padta hai, aur woh zyaada achhi tarah jaanti hain ki bachche unke apne hain. Yehi baat benefactors par bhi apply hoti hai.

## 8. Asli self-love (khud se pyaar) ki prakriti

Yeh sawaal bhi discuss hota hai ki kya insaan ko khud se sabse zyaada pyaar karna chahiye, ya kisi aur se. Log un logon ko criticize karte hain jo khud se sabse zyaada pyaar karte hain, aur unhe self-lovers (khudgarz) kehte hain, ise ek disgrace (aprataśta) ke epithet (upnaam) ki tarah use karte hue — aur ek bura aadmi lagta hai ki sab kuch apne hi liye karta hai, aur jitna zyaada woh wicked hota hai, utna zyaada — isliye log use taane dete hain, jaise ki woh apne interest ke alaawa kuch nahi karta — jabki achha aadmi noble ke liye karm karta hai, aur jitna zyaada achha, utna zyaada, aur apne friend ke liye karm karta hai, aur apna interest sacrifice kar deta hai.

Lekin facts (tathya) in arguments (tarkon) se takrate hain, aur yeh koi ashcharya ki baat nahi. Kyunki log kehte hain ki insaan ko apne best friend se sabse zyaada pyaar karna chahiye, aur insaan ka best friend woh hai jo apni wish (kaamna) ke object (paatra) ke liye achha chahta hai, uske hi khaatir, chaahe koi jaane ya na jaane — aur yeh attributes sabse zyaada insaan ke apne khud ke prati attitude (dhukh) mein paaye jaate hain, aur waise hi baaki sab attributes jinse friend define hota hai — kyunki, jaisa humne kaha, isi rishte se hi friendship ki saari characteristics padosiyon tak pahunchi hain.

Saare proverbs (kahaavatein) bhi isse sehmat hain, jaise 'ek hi soul', aur 'friends ki cheezein common property (saanjhi sampatti) hoti hain,' aur 'friendship equality (barabari) hai,' aur 'ghutna pindli se zyaada nazdeek hai' — kyunki yeh sab marks (nishaaniyaan) insaan ke khud ke saath rishte mein sabse zyaada milti hain; woh khud ka sabse achha friend hai, isliye use khud se sabse zyaada pyaar karna chahiye. Toh yeh ek reasonable sawaal hai ki hum in do views mein se kaunsa follow karein, kyunki dono plausible (vishvasaneey) lagte hain.

Shayad humein aise arguments ko ek-dusre se alag karna chahiye aur decide karna chahiye ki har view kahan tak aur kis roop mein sahi hai. Ab agar hum yeh samajh lein ki har school (vichaardhaara) 'self ka lover' phrase kis sense mein use karti hai, toh sach saamne aa sakta hai. Jo log ise reproach (taane) ke term ki tarah use karte hain, woh self-love us insaan par lagate hain jo khud ko wealth (dhan), honours (samman), aur bodily pleasures (shaareerik sukh) ka zyaada hissa deta hai — kyunki yehi cheezein hain jo zyaadatar log chahte hain, aur unmein aise busy rehte hain jaise woh sabse achhi cheezein hon, jo yeh bhi wajah hai ki yeh competition (pratispardha) ka object bante hain.

Toh jo log in cheezon ke liye grasping (lolupata bhare) hote hain, woh apni appetites (laalsayein) aur general taur par apni feelings aur soul ke irrational element (buddhihiin tatva) ko gratify (santusht) karte hain; aur zyaadatar log aise hi hote hain (isi wajah se yeh epithet aise use hota hai — yeh self-love ke prevailing type (prachlit prakaar) se apna meaning leta hai, jo ek bura type hai); isliye jo log is tarah se self-lover hain unhe reproach karna justly (nyaayसंगत) hi hai. Yeh saaf hai ki jo log aise objects mein khud ko preference dete hain unhe hi zyaadatar log self-lover kehte hain — kyunki agar koi insaan hamesha isi baat ki chinta karta ho ki woh khud, sabse pehle, justly, temperately (sanyam se), ya kisi aur virtue ke anusaar karm kare, aur general taur par hamesha apne liye noble cheez hasil karne ki koshish kare, toh koi use self-lover ya blame ka paatra nahi kahega.

Lekin aisa insaan doosre se zyaada self-lover lagta hai — akhir woh khud ko sabse noble aur best cheezein deta hai, aur apne andar ke sabse authoritative (adhikaari) element ko gratify karta hai, aur har cheez mein isi ko follow karta hai; aur jaise ek city ya koi bhi systematic whole (vyavasthit samagra) sabse zyaada apne sabse authoritative element se hi identify hota hai, waise hi insaan bhi — isliye jo insaan isse pyaar karta hai aur ise gratify karta hai woh sabse zyaada self-lover hai. Iske alaawa, insaan ke paas self-control (aatm-niyantran) hai ya nahi yeh iss baat par kaha jaata hai ki uska reason (yukti) control mein hai ya nahi — is assumption par ki yehi asli insaan hai; aur jo karm insaan rational principle (yukti-sangat siddhant) ke anusaar karta hai woh sabse zyaada uske apne aur voluntary (swechchhik) karm maane jaate hain.

Toh yeh saaf hai ki yehi insaan hai, ya kisi aur cheez se zyaada yehi hai, aur achha insaan sabse zyaada isi part se pyaar karta hai. Isse yeh nikalta hai ki woh sabse sacchai se self-lover hai, ek doosri tarah ka self-lover jo reproach ka vishay nahi — utna hi alag jitna rational principle ke anusaar jeena passion (jazbaat) ke anusaar jeene se alag hai, aur noble cheez chahna advantageous lagne waali cheez chahne se alag hai. Toh jo log exceptional (asaadharan) taur par noble actions mein busy rehte hain unhe sab log approve aur praise karte hain; aur agar sab log noble ki taraf koshish karein aur noblest deeds karne ki poori koshish karein, toh sab kuch common weal ke liye theek hoga, aur har insaan apne liye sabse badi goods (nemat) haasil karega, kyunki virtue sabse badi good hai.

Isliye achhe insaan ko self-lover hona chahiye (kyunki noble karmon se woh khud bhi labhaanvit hoga aur apne saathiyon ko bhi fayda pahunchayega), lekin wicked insaan ko nahi — kyunki woh khud ko aur apne padosiyon dono ko nuksaan pahunchayega, apni evil passions ko follow karte hue. Wicked insaan ke liye, jo woh karta hai woh usse takrata hai jo usse karna chahiye; lekin achha insaan jo karna chahiye wahi karta hai — kyunki reason har ek apne rakhne waale mein khud ke liye best chunta hai, aur achha insaan apne reason ko follow karta hai. Yeh sach hai ki achha insaan bhi apne friends aur apne desh ke liye bahut kaam karta hai, aur agar zaroorat pade toh unke liye jaan bhi de deta hai — kyunki woh wealth aur honours aur general taur par competition ki cheezein phenk dega, apne liye nobility haasil karte hue; kyunki woh ek chhoti si intense pleasure ki avadhi ko lambe mild enjoyment (halke aanand) se zyaada prefer karega, ek saal ki noble life ko humdrum (nirasse) astitva ke bahut saalon se, aur ek badi aur noble action ko bahut si trivial (chhoti) actions se.

Ab jo log doosron ke liye jaan dete hain woh nissandeh yeh result paate hain — isliye yeh unke liye ek bada prize hai jo woh khud ke liye chunte hain. Woh wealth bhi phenk denge is shart par ki unke friends zyaada paayein — kyunki jab friend wealth paata hai toh woh khud nobility haasil karta hai; isliye woh khud ko hi zyaada good de raha hota hai. Yehi baat honour aur office (padvi) ke saath bhi sach hai — yeh sab woh apne friend ke liye sacrifice karega, kyunki yeh khud ke liye noble aur laudable (prashansaneey) hai. Toh sahi hi use achha maana jaata hai, kyunki woh sabse pehle nobility chunta hai. Lekin woh apni actions bhi apne friend ke liye chhod sakta hai — shayad khud karm karne se zyaada noble ho apne friend ke karm karne ka cause banna. Toh un sab actions mein jinke liye insaan ki praise hoti hai, achha insaan dikhta hai ki woh khud ko noble cheez ka zyaada hissa de raha hai.

Is sense mein, jaisa kaha ja chuka hai, insaan ko self-lover hona chahiye; lekin jis sense mein zyaadatar log hote hain, use nahi hona chahiye.

# FRIENDSHIP KI ZAROORAT

## 9. Khushnaseeb insaan ko friends ki zaroorat kyun hoti hai?

Yeh bhi disputed (vivaadit) hai ki kya khush insaan ko friends ki zaroorat hogi ya nahi. Kaha jaata hai ki jo log supremely happy (parama sukhi) aur self-sufficient (aatm-nirbhar) hain unhe friends ki koi zaroorat nahi hoti — kyunki unke paas achhi cheezein hain, aur isliye self-sufficient hone ki wajah se unhe aur kuch nahi chahiye, jabki friend, jo ek doosra khud hi hai, woh dega jo insaan khud apne prayaas se nahi de sakta — isi se yeh kahaavat aayi hai 'jab fortune (bhagya) meherbaan hai, toh friends ki kya zaroorat?'

Lekin yeh ajeeb lagta hai, jab hum khush insaan ko sab achhi cheezein dete hain, use friends na dena — jinhe sabse bade external goods (baahari nemat) mein se maana jaata hai. Aur agar friend ki zyaada characteristic baat yeh hai ki woh doosre ke saath achha kare, na ki khud ke saath achha ho, aur benefits dena achhe insaan aur virtue ki characteristic hai, aur strangers se zyaada apne friends ke saath achha karna zyaada noble hai, toh achhe insaan ko aise log chahiye jinke saath woh achha kar sake. Isi wajah se yeh sawaal poocha jaata hai ki hume friends ki zyaada zaroorat prosperity (samriddhi) mein hoti hai ya adversity (vipatti) mein — is assumption par ki sirf adversity mein hi insaan ko koi apna bhala karne waala nahi chahiye, balki jo prosper kar rahe hain unhe bhi apne saath achha karne waale log chahiye.

Yeh bhi ajeeb hai ki supremely happy insaan ko akela bana diya jaaye — kyunki koi bhi poori duniya paana pasand nahi karega akele rehne ki shart par, kyunki insaan ek political creature (samajik praani) hai jiska nature doosron ke saath rehna hai. Isliye khush insaan bhi doosron ke saath rehta hai — kyunki uske paas woh cheezein hain jo nature se achhi hain. Aur saaf hai ki apne din friends aur achhe logon ke saath bitaana strangers ya kisi bhi chance persons (achaanak mile logon) se behtar hai. Isliye khush insaan ko friends ki zaroorat hai.

Toh pehle view rakhne waalon ka kya matlab hai, aur woh kis maayne mein sahi hain? Kya yeh hai ki zyaadatar log friends ko useful (upyogi) logon se identify karte hain? Aise friends ki toh supremely happy insaan ko koi zaroorat nahi hogi, kyunki uske paas pehle se hi achhi cheezein hain; na hi use un logon ki zaroorat hogi jinhe log unki pleasantness ki wajah se friend banate hain, ya bahut kam zaroorat hogi (kyunki uski life, pleasant hone ki wajah se, adventitious (bahri, aakasmik) pleasure ki zaroorat nahi rakhti); aur isliye kyunki use aise friends ki zaroorat nahi, isliye maana jaata hai ki use friends ki zaroorat nahi.

Lekin yeh sach nahi hai. Kyunki humne shuru mein kaha hai ki happiness ek activity hai; aur activity saaf taur par exist mein aati hai, koi property (sampatti) ki tarah shuru se present nahi hoti. Agar happiness jeene aur active hone mein hai, aur achhe insaan ki activity virtuous aur khud mein pleasant hai, jaisa humne shuru mein kaha, aur kisi cheez ka apna hona uski un attributes mein se ek hai jo use pleasant banati hain, aur hum apne padosiyon ko khud se behtar contemplate (mannan) kar sakte hain aur unke actions ko apne se behtar — aur agar unke friend, virtuous logon ke actions achhe logon ke liye pleasant hain (kyunki inmein woh dono attributes hain jo naturally pleasant hain) — agar yeh sach hai, toh supremely happy insaan ko aise friends ki zaroorat hogi, kyunki uska purpose worthy (yogya) actions aur apni khud ki actions ko contemplate karna hai, aur achhe insaan ka, jo uska friend hai, actions mein yeh dono qualities hoti hain.

Phir, log sochte hain ki khush insaan ko pleasantly (sukhpoorvak) jeena chahiye. Ab agar woh solitary (akela) hota, toh uske liye life mushkil hoti — kyunki akele continuously (nirantar) active rehna aasan nahi; lekin doosron ke saath aur unki taraf yeh aasan hai. Doosron ke saath uski activity zyaada continuous hogi, aur yeh khud mein pleasant hai, jaisa ki honi chahiye us insaan ke liye jo supremely happy hai — kyunki achha insaan achha hone ki wajah se virtuous actions mein khush hota hai aur vicious (durachari) actions se vyathit hota hai, jaise musical (sangeet-priya) insaan khoobsurat sur sunke khush aur bure sur sunke dukhi hota hai. Achhe logon ki company se virtue ki bhi kuch training milti hai, jaisa Theognis ne humse pehle kaha hai.

Agar hum cheezon ki nature mein aur gehra dekhein, toh ek virtuous friend virtuous insaan ke liye naturally desirable (chaahne laayak) lagta hai. Kyunki jo cheez nature se achhi hai, humne kaha, woh virtuous insaan ke liye khud mein achhi aur pleasant hai. Ab life animals (praniyon) ke case mein perception (anubhooti) ki power se define hoti hai, insaan ke case mein perception ya thought (vichaar) ki power se; aur power us corresponding activity se define hoti hai jo essential (mool) baat hai; isliye life essentially perceive ya think karne ka hi karm lagta hai. Aur life un cheezon mein se hai jo khud mein achhi aur pleasant hain, kyunki yeh determinate (nishchit) hai aur determinate hona hi good ki nature hai; aur jo nature se achha hai woh virtuous insaan ke liye bhi achha hai (yehi wajah hai ki life sab logon ko pleasant lagti hai); lekin humein ise wicked aur corrupt (bhrasht) life par, ya pain mein bitayi gayi life par apply nahi karna chahiye — kyunki aisi life indeterminate hai, jaise uske attributes.

Pain ki nature aage aur saaf hogi. Lekin agar life khud achhi aur pleasant hai (jaisa yeh lagta hai, is fact se ki sab log ise chahte hain, khaas kar jo achhe aur supremely happy hain — kyunki aise logon ke liye life sabse zyaada desirable hai, aur unka astitva sabse zyaada supremely happy hai); aur agar jo dekhta hai use pata hota hai ki woh dekh raha hai, aur jo sunta hai use pata hota hai ki woh sun raha hai, aur jo chalta hai use pata hota hai ki woh chal raha hai, aur baaki sab activities mein isi tarah kuch hota hai jo perceive karta hai ki hum active hain, isliye agar hum perceive karte hain, toh hum perceive karte hain ki hum perceive kar rahe hain, aur agar hum sochte hain, toh hum perceive karte hain ki hum soch rahe hain; aur agar yeh perceive karna ki hum perceive ya think kar rahe hain, yeh perceive karna hai ki hum exist karte hain (kyunki existence perceive ya think karne se define ki gayi thi); aur agar yeh perceive karna ki hum jeete hain khud mein pleasant cheezon mein se ek hai (kyunki life nature se achhi hai, aur khud mein present achhi cheez ko perceive karna pleasant hota hai); aur agar life desirable hai, aur khaas kar achhe logon ke liye, kyunki unke liye existence achha aur pleasant hai (kyunki woh khush hote hain us achhi cheez ki consciousness (chetna) se jo unke andar hai) — aur agar jaisa virtuous insaan khud ke saath hai, waise hi woh apne friend ke saath bhi hai (kyunki friend doosra khud hi hai) — agar yeh sab sach hai, toh jaise har insaan ke liye apna astitva desirable hai, waise hi, ya lagbhag waise hi, uske friend ka astitva bhi hai.

Ab uska astitva isliye desirable dekha gaya kyunki woh apni achhaayi ko perceive karta hai, aur aisi perception khud mein pleasant hoti hai. Isliye use apne friend ka astitva bhi apne khud ke saath perceive karna chahiye, aur yeh tabhi realize hoga jab woh saath rahenge aur discussion aur thought share karenge — kyunki insaan ke case mein saath rehne ka yehi matlab lagta hai, na ki jaise cattle (maweshi) ek hi jagah chaara khaate hain. Toh agar being (astitva) khud mein supremely happy insaan ke liye desirable hai (kyunki yeh apne nature se achha aur pleasant hai), aur uske friend ka astitva bhi lagbhag waisa hi hai, toh friend un cheezon mein se ek hoga jo desirable hain. Ab jo cheez uske liye desirable hai, woh use honi chahiye, warna woh iss maamle mein deficient (kam) hoga. Toh jo insaan khush hona hai use virtuous friends ki zaroorat hogi.

## 10. Friends ki sankhya ki seema (limit)

Toh kya humein jitne ho sake utne friends banane chahiye, ya — jaise hospitality (mehmaan-nawaazi) ke maamle mein yeh suitable advice maani jaati hai ki insaan 'na bahut mehmaanon waala ho na kisi mehmaan ke bina' — kya yeh friendship par bhi apply hota hai? Kya insaan na friendless (bina dost ke) hona chahiye na excessive (atyadhik) sankhya mein friends rakhne chahiye?

Utility ke liye banaaye gaye friends par yeh kahaavat poori tarah applicable lagti hai — kyunki bahut se logon ko return mein services dena ek laborious task hai aur zindagi itni lambi nahi ki iske liye kaafi ho. Isliye humari apni zindagi ke liye jitne sufficient (kaafi) hain unse zyaada friends superfluous (adhikta ke, faaltu) hain, aur noble life mein hindrance (rukaawat) hain — isliye unki zaroorat nahi. Pleasure ke liye banaaye gaye friends bhi thode hi kaafi hote hain, jaise khaane mein thoda seasoning (masaala) kaafi hota hai.

Lekin achhe friends ke maamle mein, kya humein jitne ho sake utne rakhne chahiye, ya kya friends ki sankhya ki bhi ek limit hai, jaise ek city ki hoti hai? Tum das aadmiyon se city nahi bana sakte, aur agar ek lakh hon toh woh city nahi rehti. Lekin sahi sankhya shayad ek single number nahi, balki kuch fixed points ke beech kuch bhi hai. Toh friends ke liye bhi ek fixed sankhya hai — shayad sabse badi sankhya jinke saath insaan saath reh sake (kyunki, jaisa humne dekha, yeh friendship ki bahut characteristic baat maani jaati hai); aur yeh saaf hai ki insaan bahut se logon ke saath reh nahi sakta aur khud ko unmein baant nahi sakta. Iske alaawa, unhe bhi ek-dusre ka friend hona chahiye agar sab ne saath din bitaane hain, aur yeh bade sankhya ke saath poora karna mushkil kaam hai.

Yeh bhi mushkil hai bahut se logon ke saath intimate (gehri) taur par khush aur dukhi hona, kyunki aisa ho sakta hai ki insaan ko ek hi samay mein ek friend ke saath khush aur doosre ke saath shok manaana pade. Toh, shayad, behtar yeh hai ki jitne ho sake utne friends dhoondhne ke bajaaye utne hi rakhe jaayein jitne saath rehne ke purpose ke liye kaafi hon — kyunki bahut se logon ka great friend ban paana asambhav lagta hai. Yehi wajah hai ki insaan bahut se logon se love nahi kar sakta — love friendship ka ek excess (adhikta) hai, aur yeh sirf ek insaan ke prati mehsoos ki ja sakti hai; isliye great friendship bhi sirf thode se logon ke prati mehsoos ki ja sakti hai. Yeh practice (vyavahar) mein bhi confirm hota lagta hai — kyunki humein comradely (saathi) tarah ki friendship rakhne waale bahut se log nahi milte, aur is tarah ki mashhoor friendships hamesha do logon ke beech hi hoti hain.

Jinke bahut se friends hote hain aur woh sabke saath intimate taur par milte-julte hain, unhe kisi ka bhi friend nahi maana jaata, sivaay us tarah ke jaisa fellow citizens (saathi nagarikon) ke beech hota hai, aur aise log obsequious (khushaamadi) bhi kahe jaate hain. Fellow citizens ki tarah, sach hai, insaan bahut se logon ka friend ho sakta hai aur phir bhi obsequious nahi, balki genuinely (sacchi) achha insaan ho sakta hai; lekin bahut se logon ke saath virtue aur apne friends ke character par based friendship nahi rakhi ja sakti, aur humein santusht rehna chahiye agar humein thode se bhi aise mil jaayein.

## 11. Kya humein friends ki zyaada zaroorat achhe fortune mein hoti hai ya bure mein?

Kya humein friends ki zaroorat achhe fortune mein zyaada hoti hai ya bure mein? Unhe dono mein dhoondha jaata hai — kyunki adversity mein log madad chahte hain, jabki prosperity mein unhe aise log chahiye jinke saath rahein aur jinke saath apna beneficence (upkaar) share karein — kyunki woh doosron ke saath achha karna chahte hain. Toh friendship bad fortune mein zyaada necessary hai, isliye is case mein humein useful friends chahiye hote hain; lekin good fortune mein yeh zyaada noble hai, isliye hum achhe logon ko bhi friend banaana chahte hain, kyunki inhe benefits dena aur inke saath rehna zyaada desirable hai.

Kyunki friends ki presence (upasthiti) achhe aur bure dono fortune mein pleasant hoti hai, kyunki jab friends humare saath dukh manaate hain toh dukh halka ho jaata hai. Isliye koi sawaal kar sakta hai ki kya woh humara bojh baantte hain, ya — bina yeh hue bhi — unki presence apni pleasantness se, aur unke humare saath dukhi hone ke khayal se, humara dard kam kar deti hai. Chaahe yeh in wajahon se ho ya kisi aur wajah se, humara dukh halka ho jaata hai — yeh sawaal chhod diya ja sakta hai; kam se kam jo humne describe kiya woh hota hua dikhta hai.

Lekin unki presence mein alag-alag factors (tatvon) ka mixture (mishran) lagta hai. Apne friends ko dekhna hi pleasant hai (khaas kar jab insaan adversity mein ho), aur yeh dukh ke against ek safeguard (suraksha) ban jaata hai (kyunki friend humein uski nazar aur uske shabdon se comfort deta hai, agar woh tactful hai, kyunki woh humara character aur jo humein pleasure ya pain deta hai woh jaanta hai); lekin use humari misfortunes se pained (vyathit) dekhna painful hota hai — kyunki har koi apne friends ko pain dene ka cause banne se bachta hai. Isi wajah se manly (purushocit) nature waale log apne friends ko apne saath dukhi karne se bachte hain, aur, jab tak woh pain ke prati exceptionally (asaadharan) insensible (asamvedansheel) na ho, aisa insaan apne friends par aane waale pain ko bardaasht nahi kar paata, aur general taur par fellow mourners (saath shok manaane waale) ko admit nahi karta kyunki woh khud mourning (shok) mein nahi rehta; lekin auratein aur womanly (streevat) purush apne sympathizers (sahaanubhooti dikhaane waalon) ko unke dukh mein enjoy karte hain, aur unhe friends aur sorrow (dukh) ke companions (saathiyon) ki tarah pyaar karte hain. Lekin har cheez mein humein zaahir hai ki behtar type ke insaan ki imitate (nakal) karni chahiye.

Doosri taraf, humari prosperity mein friends ki presence humare samay ko pleasant banaati hai aur unki khushi ka pleasant khayal deti hai humari khud ki achhi fortune par. Isi wajah se lagta hai ki humein apne friends ko readily (khushi se) bulaana chahiye humari achhi fortune mein share karne ke liye (kyunki beneficent (upkaari) character noble hai), lekin unhe humari bad fortune mein hesitation (jhijhak) ke saath bulaana chahiye — kyunki humein unhe humari buraiyon mein jitna ho sake utna kam share dena chahiye — isliye kahaavat hai 'meri musibat kaafi hai.' Humein apne friends ko sabse zyaada tab bulaana chahiye jab woh thodi si takleef sehkar humein badi service kar sakte hon.

Iske ulta, jo log adversity mein hain unki madad ke liye bina bulaaye aur khushi se jaana appropriate hai (kyunki friend ki characteristic yeh hai ki woh services de, khaas kar unko jo zaroorat mein hain aur jinhone maang nahi ki — aisi action dono ke liye zyaada noble aur pleasant hai); lekin jab humare friends prosperous (samriddh) hon toh humein unki activities mein khushi se shaamil hona chahiye (kyunki unhe in cheezon ke liye bhi friends chahiye hote hain), lekin unki kindness (dayaalu bhaav) paane mein aage aane mein dheema hona chahiye — kyunki benefits paane ke liye eager (utsuk) hona noble nahi hai. Phir bhi, humein zaroor bachna chahiye kill-joys (rang mein bhang daalne waale) kehlaane se unhe repulse (thukra) karke — kyunki yeh kabhi-kabhi hota hai.

Toh friends ki presence sab circumstances (paristhitiyon) mein desirable lagti hai.

## 12. Friendship ka saar (mool tatva) hai saath rehna

Toh kya yeh nahi nikalta ki, jaise lovers ke liye beloved ka roop dekhna hi sabse zyaada pyaari cheez hoti hai, aur woh iss sense (indriya) ko baaki sabse zyaada prefer karte hain kyunki isi par pyaar ka hona aur uski shuruaat sabse zyaada depend karti hai, waise hi friends ke liye sabse desirable cheez saath rehna hai? Kyunki friendship ek partnership (sanjhedaari) hai, aur jaisa insaan khud ke liye hai, waisa hi woh apne friend ke liye hai; ab apne case mein apna hona perceive karna desirable hai, isliye apne friend ka hona perceive karna bhi desirable hai, aur perceiving active hoti hai jab woh saath rehte hain, isliye yeh natural hai ki woh isi ki taraf koshish karein.

Aur har class ke logon ke liye jo bhi existence ka matlab hai, jiske liye woh life ko value karte hain, usi mein woh apne friends ke saath busy rehna chahte hain; isliye kuch log saath sharaab peete hain, kuch saath dice khelte hain, kuch saath athletic exercises (khel-kood) aur hunting (shikaar) karte hain, ya philosophy ka adhyayan karte hain, har class apne din us cheez mein bitaate hain jo unhe life mein sabse zyaada pyaari hai — kyunki woh apne friends ke saath rehna chahte hain, toh woh un cheezon mein hissa lete hain aur karte hain jo unhe saath rehne ka ehsaas dete hain.

Isliye bure logon ki friendship ek evil (bura) cheez ban jaati hai (kyunki apni instability (asthirta) ki wajah se woh bure pursuits (kaamon) mein ekjut hote hain, aur iske alaawa woh ek-dusre jaise ban kar evil ban jaate hain), jabki achhe logon ki friendship achhi hoti hai, unki companionship (saath) se badhti hui; aur maana jaata hai ki woh apni activities se aur ek-dusre ko improve karke behtar bhi ban jaate hain — kyunki woh ek-dusre se un characteristics ka mould (dhaancha) lete hain jo unhe pasand hain — isi se kahaavat aayi hai 'achhe logon se noble karm.'

Toh friendship ke baare mein itna hi — hamara agla kaam pleasure (sukh) discuss karna hai.

---
